No new security subsystem; the harness additionally asserts the **policy deny path** (blocks a known forbidden claim write and appends a `deny` row to `audit.jsonl`), pinning the ADR-28 gate behavior in CI (test-env-harness-plan Green Criteria; deny-slice already shipped per `tests/test_policy_gate_plugin.py:41`).

### Docs / correctness gates

- **What:** New `docs_doctor.py` rule 7 — **bare `(ADR-NN)` code detection**. `BARE_ADR_CODE_RE = (?<!\[)\(ADR-\d+\)`; `check_bare_adr_codes()` flags unlinked ADR mentions in published docs (ADR files and repo-internal release/testing/contributing docs exempt via `_published`); offending pages fixed. **Why:** ADR-73 (docs reference conventions) was PARTIAL — "Rule 2 ('never bare `(ADR-NN)` codes outside explanation pages') is doc-only and violated" (gap analysis §6). Chose enforce-in-doctor over one-time fix "so it can't regress" (exec-plan WS-3 #626).

- **What:** Large **single-source-of-truth de-duplication sweep** across docs/ per ADR-73 "link, don't repeat" (commits 11b32c2d ~59 files, 1b360075, 4a54c13f). Canonical owners keep the spec; duplicating pages collapse to a summary + cross-link. Examples: `frontmatter.md`'s links-vs-relationships table collapsed to a pointer to `linking.md`; `note-types.md`'s inbox-card field tables deferred to canonical pages; glossary/telemetry/vault-eval enum and cron duplications linked to owners. Verified counts corrected (21→22 note types; 16→20 templates; 8→12 plugins; `.pre-commit-config.yaml` ruff pinned to v0.15.17; underscore-vs-hyphen doctor-script regex fixes). ADR metadata integrity fixes (ADR-51 supersedes 36; ADR-57 ADR-69 vocab note; forward-pointers ADR-46→69, ADR-45→75, ADR-55→76). **Why:** enforce ADR-73's single-source rule now that the audit surfaced live violations; "each fact keeps one canonical home" (commit 11b32c2d body).

### ADRs

- **What:** **ADR-80 created and moved deferred→accepted within the release.** Born `status: deferred` in commit 7426b139 (`80-ephemeral-containerized-test-env.md`), extended to cover L0–L4 model-free (aada1dff), then set `status: accepted`, `date_resolved: 2026-06-17`, `nav_exclude` dropped, at cut (4aaa8c4b). Phase 2 (live-model L5, visual golden-diffs, chaos/perf) stays gated with its triggers. **Why:** the deferred-ADR implementability review found ADR-80 mis-filed as "genuinely blocked (Tier C)" — "Phase 1 is model-free by the ADR's own words; the remaining blocker is engineering effort, not an external prerequisite. Only Phase 2 (live GPU model) is genuinely cost-gated" (`tmp/deferred-adr-implementability-verification.md`; moves recorded in commits 1d64542e, f5fff38a). ADR-80 `assumes: [28, 29, 64, 76]`.

- **What:** **Stale-assumption text corrected in four deferred ADRs — 39/59/65/76** (commit c5a5d2f2, no decision change). ADR-59: the "`[!suggestions]` weighted scorer" and controlled-vocab tag classifier "described as existing machinery to reuse … neither exists" (ranking is the LLM `catalog-rank-candidate` skill) — reframed as unbuilt, "no new subsystems" premise dropped (#628). ADR-65: `vision_analyze` "is not an available-but-unwired path — it does not exist in the ingest pipeline," so figure-informed `_aspects` is blocked not deferred; `extends` baseline already ships in `link-suggest-claim` (#629). ADR-76: "11 `__file__` bootstraps" is now 17 across 13 files, and the standalone policy core "already exists (`memoria_runtime/policy/`)" — residual is gate-shim vendoring (#630). ADR-39: re-entry trigger path `30-synthesis/01-claims/` corrected to real home `notes/claims/` (#631). **Why:** "A code-level re-verification of the 14 deferred ADRs at HEAD found four ADRs asserting current state that no longer holds" — alpha.5 silently invalidated triggers, and the audit method explicitly refuses to trust an ADR's own `assumes:`/trigger text (commit c5a5d2f2 body; implementability-verification "Stale-assumption items").

- **What:** ADR-38/41/35 trigger text corrected in the cadence review (commit 06de3f66): ADR-38 trigger (a) "live qmd index in retrieval" marked **now met**; ADR-41 noted the review_mode/schema_version attribution stamp already shipped; ADR-35 classify-miss instrumentation now exists; ADR-59 ID-first record-linkage pass already ships in `link.py`; ADR-76 step-1 tooling marked landed in alpha.4. **Why:** same skeptical re-verification — leaving only the genuinely-remaining slice of each deferred ADR as its trigger.

- **What:** Cut-time ADR status maintenance (release plan §7): the audit's accepted-ADR gaps recorded as moving PARTIAL→implemented (ADR-31, -78, -10, -70, -77, -07, -73); ADR-74 stays `deferred` with the static-manifest precursor + remaining updater/CI-doctor work recorded. Retire-sweep expected no-op ("no question is dissolved by alpha.6"). **Why:** keep ADR status honest against built state — the whole raison d'être of the release.

### Removed / retired

- **What:** Inline `_self_test`/`self_test` functions, their `--self-test` CLI flags, dispatch branches, docstring usage lines, and newly-unused `tempfile`/`sys` imports stripped from **10 shipped modules** (commit 70e01ba3): `cluster_mcp.py`, `patterns_mcp.py`, `tasks_mcp.py`, `golden_restore.py`, `hub_handoff.py`, `precommit_check.py`, `inbox.py`, `schema.py`, `worklists.py`, `structural_impact.py`. Legitimate `main()`/CLI entrypoints kept. **Why:** ADR-44 conformance — "'the deployed vault carries zero test code': 10 shipped modules still carried inline `_self_test` … dead code, since both `python-selftest.yml` and `scripts/test.sh` run `pytest tests/` and every module already has a `tests/test_*.py` equivalent" (commit 70e01ba3 body). "The ADRs are correct; the implementation had drifted."

- **What:** Residual `agent_verdict` back-compat fallback reader dropped from `board_export.py`; its test updated to assert the rename is one-way. **Why:** ADR-18 conformance — "'only this ADR retains the old name': dropped the residual `agent_verdict` back-compat fallback" (commit 70e01ba3 body).

- **What (deferred, not shipped):** Harness Phase 2, packaging (ADR-76 #521), cross-vault/multi-machine (ADR-60/63), corpus-calibration-blocked items, and always-on/transport work — all explicitly out of scope with named reasons (release plan §5). **Why:** each is model-cost-gated, cadence-gated, dormant-by-design under single-researcher scope, or blocked on real-corpus/always-on infrastructure that a clean scaffold cannot exercise ("this checkout is a clean scaffold (0 claims, 0 papers, 0 real projects)" — implementability-verification method note).

## alpha.7 — Clean-slate Obsidian UI & navigation (the persistent gate shell)

**Theme.** A ground-up redesign of the Obsidian front end: retire the ADR-68 three-workspace layout-swap model and re-implement navigation as **four job-named dashboard notes in a single persistent shell**, backed by a consolidated **Bases view layer**, **schema-generated capture forms**, and **Portals** folder navigation. This is the "UI/navigation release."

**What drove it.** Three shipped-UI issues (#659 "no single clear title," #665 "the same base shown 3–4×," #667 "using a base to navigate is unintuitive"), plus #663/#664/#666/#668, converged on one verdict: *Bases-as-navigation was rough and the workspace-swap machinery over-implemented the requirement.* The team ran a clean-slate design pass (four scratch design docs under `tmp/`, reviewed by a non-author reviewer and sandbox-verified against Obsidian 1.12.7), then shipped only the **verified, low-risk substrate** and explicitly **deferred** the speculative half (a general projector engine, projected telemetry bases, the Canvas/argument-graph spatial axis, and a dedicated edge-authoring control) in ADR-81. It closed as an untagged internal checkpoint (`released: false`), and the alpha.6-penciled shadow/instrument telemetry harvest (#370/#611/#416/#371) was consciously *not* absorbed and rolled to alpha.8.

---

### Vault / concepts & schemas

- **What:** New top-level `gates/` folder and a new `gate` category/type. `folders.yaml` gains `gates` in `categories`, maps `gate: gates` in the type→home table, and adds `gates` to the `skeleton:` build list (`src/.memoria/schemas/folders.yaml`); a new `src/.memoria/schemas/types/gate.yaml` defines the type (`enums.gate: [inbox, library, knowledge, project]`, `lifecycle: [current, archived]`, `gated: false`, required `type/lifecycle/title/gate`). — **Why:** gate dashboards are now *vault content* (notes), not plugin layout state, so they need a first-class folder, type-home, and Linter-checkable schema. ADR-81 Decision: "Gate switching becomes vault content instead of plugin layout state… easier to diff, restore, and test." The four-gate enum hard-codes the derived JTBD set from `workspaces-design.md` §3 (Inbox/Library/Knowledge/Project; Studio deferred).

- **What:** New `worker-card` type schema (`src/.memoria/schemas/types/worker-card.yaml`): `category: system`, home `system/board`, `status` enum `[triage, todo, ready, running, blocked, retrying, done]`, required `task_id/lane/status/title`, optional `as_of/review_status/retry_count/reason/expected_outputs/created`. Detectors add `gate: gates/` to `TYPE_HOME`, `gates` to `KNOWN_TOP_DIRS`, `NOTE_FOLDERS`, and the design-scan prefixes (`src/.memoria/operations/integrity/linter/detectors.py`). — **Why:** the board mirror is now read by a real Base (`board.base`) and must be schema-legible like any other collection. Previously the projected cards carried an ad-hoc `type: board-card` with no schema; the redesign makes the *one projection that already exists* conform to the type system so the Linter and Bases treat it uniformly (`ui-architecture-alpha7.md` §2–§3: "authored bases vs the one projected base"). The detector edits are the mechanical consequence of adding a permitted top-level folder — without them a stray-folder detector would flag `gates/`.

- **What:** `board_export.py` rewrites card frontmatter from the old key list (`task_id/status/assignee/review_status/retry_count/reason/last_updated` + `type: board-card`) to the full `worker-card` schema shape — `title`, `type: worker-card`, `lifecycle: current`, `lane` (renamed from `assignee`), `status`, `as_of` (renamed from `last_updated`), `created` (`src/.memoria/mcp/board_export.py`). — **Why:** to satisfy the new `worker-card` schema and let `board.base` sort on the payload-native `as_of` rather than `file.mtime` (all cards in a pass share a generation mtime, so mtime is meaningless — `ui-architecture-alpha7.md` §2: "Sort on `as_of`, not `file.mtime`"). The `assignee→lane` rename aligns the projection with the schema's `lane` grouping key used by the base's "By lane" view.

---

### Profiles / runtime (skills)

- **What:** Two map-lane skills ship, moving out of the deferred list: `map:graph-claims` and `map:canvas-hub`, both registered under `memoria-librarian/skills/` and added to the Librarian row of `docs/reference/hermes-cli.md` (commit `54b91cf7`, closes #381). Both are **propose-class JSON Canvas emitters** over the cluster engine's typed graph (`cluster_build_graph` / `cluster_emit_canvas`), write only to `notes/fleeting/` + `inbox/`, and raise one `candidate` card. — **Why:** they were the two *unblocked* graph/canvas map skills — modeled on the shipped `map:seed-canvas` and carrying **no score, threshold, or calibration** behavior, so they don't depend on the calibration gate that still blocks `map:score-writability`/`map:score-readiness`. Commit body: "Both are propose-class JSON Canvas emitters over the cluster engine's typed graph… No score, threshold, or calibration behavior (the score-* map skills stay deferred, calibration-gated)." They honor the engine-writes/agent-judges split (ADR-33: the cluster engine deliberately does *not* emit Canvas; the skill is the propose-class half) and `tests/test_profiles.py` enforces frontmatter/tool-resolution/write-scope (13 passed). Note these landed in the same range but are logically an *unblocked skill*, not part of the UI shell.

---

### Retrieval / view layer (Bases)

The core design bet of the release: **Bases is the universal tabular view layer, Dataview shrinks to a single cross-collection surface, and every `.base` view leads with `title`.**

- **What:** Every authored base's `order:` now leads with the `title` property instead of `file.name` (`inbox.base`, `sources.base`, `claims.base`, `catalog.base`, `patterns.base`, `project-gate.base`; catalog entity views lead with `name`). — **Why:** the direct fix for **#659** ("one clear title"). The design deliberately *keeps a stable slug filename* (agents/API write raw `links:` wikilinks that must not churn on rename) but leads the visible column with the readable `title` property, paired with `showInlineTitle:false`, so collections read as titles while links stay stable (`ui-architecture-alpha7.md` §5: "Keep a *stable* filename… Make the slug human-readable… lead every Bases `order:` with the `title` property"). No migration was needed because the only vault is the rebuildable `Memoria-test` sandbox.

- **What:** `inbox.base` is consolidated into **four non-overlapping views** — "Needs me" (`proposed`), "Drift watch" (flag/alert), "Loose ends" (notice-loudness flags), "All cards" — with a new `loudness_rank` formula (block→0, alert→1, notice→2) driving priority sort and an `age_days` formula (`src/inbox/inbox.base`). — **Why:** kills **#665** ("same base shown 3–4×") *by construction* — the triplication was an artifact of the old layout; one base with disjoint views deletes it (`ui-architecture-alpha7.md` §3, §5: "The four views are non-overlapping… deletes #665 by construction"). The `loudness_rank` formula orders the queue by urgency (block-first) since Bases can't sort an enum by semantic severity directly.

- **What:** `sources.base` renames "To read & distill" → **"Reading pipeline"** (now `proposed || provisional`, grouped by lifecycle) and adds a **"Discuss queue"** view (`provisional`, oldest-first via `file.ctime` ASC) plus an `age_days` formula; adds `evidence_level`/`research_area` to the order (`src/system/dashboards/sources.base`). — **Why:** these are the composed surfaces of the Library gate (`ui-architecture-alpha7.md` §3/§5). "Discuss queue" (oldest first) drains read-but-not-distilled sources through a Co-PI pass; the reading pipeline distills into claims in the Knowledge gate. Fields shown are the judgment-relevant ones a reader triages on.

- **What:** `claims.base` replaces the old By-maturity/Retracted pair with **four views**: "By maturity" (now excludes `superseded_by`), "Open questions" (orphans via new `is_orphan: file.backlinks.isEmpty()` formula), "Contradictions" (`!links.contradicts.isEmpty()`), and "Retracted (lineage)"; adds `is_orphan`/`age_days` formulas (`src/system/dashboards/claims.base`). — **Why:** the Knowledge gate is the synthesis surface (`ui-architecture-alpha7.md` §3). "Open questions" = current claims with zero inbound = the synthesis backlog; "Contradictions" surfaces open tensions before advancing a claim. Both filters were **live-verified native** at 300- and 10k-note scale (§7: nested-map `!links.contradicts.isEmpty()` and orphan `file.backlinks.isEmpty()` work without a materialized field), which is *why* the design could drop its `has_contradiction`/`inbound_count` materialization fallback. The "Retracted (lineage)" flat table is flagged as a stopgap — proper DAG lineage is deferred to the spatial axis.

- **What:** New `hubs.base` (`src/notes/hubs/hubs.base`, one "Hubs index" view) and new `projects.base` (`src/projects/projects.base`, views "Active projects"/"Saturation"/"Project gaps"), plus new `board.base` (`src/system/board/board.base`, "By lane," `age_min` on `as_of`). — **Why:** the Knowledge and Project gates need their own composed collections; hubs fold into a single view rather than a heavyweight dedicated base ("avoid a dedicated base for a handful of files," §3). `projects.base` is a clean-slate replacement for `project-gate.base` that also folds in `gap` cards; `board.base` is the read layer for the one shipped projection. The projected *telemetry* bases (`fleet-health`/`eval-trend`/`skill-lifecycle`) were deliberately **not** created — they depend on the deferred projector engine (ADR-81 deferred set).

- **What:** The home Dataview status strip is the single surviving cross-collection surface; everything else is Bases. — **Why:** the primitive-selection rule (`ui-architecture-alpha7.md` §1/§6): a Base row is exactly one markdown file and can't join across collections, so the "reviews pending · blocked · HIGH/CRITICAL" one-liner is the *one* thing that must stay Dataview. (Its exact composed queries were left as an "open before merge" item, #664.)

---

### Discovery / navigation chrome (Portals)

- **What:** Portals is adopted as the left-sidebar folder navigator — added to `community-plugins.json`, vendored under `src/.obsidian/plugins/portals/` (main.js/styles.css/manifest/data.json), and provenance-locked. Config: six folder portals (`inbox`, `catalog`, `notes/sources`, `notes/claims`, `notes/hubs`, `projects`), `replaceFileExplorer: true`, `hiddenItems` routing `system/` + `.memoria` to Hidden, `tagNotesFolderPath: system/_tag-notes`, and trimmed side modules (`recent/bookmarks/context-notes/trash`) — dropping `journal` and `properties` (`portals-design.md` §4/§6, `docs/reference/obsidian-plugins.md`). — **Why:** the direct fix for **#667** (raw type-first file tree is unintuitive) and **#663** (`system/` shouldn't be user-facing). The design pins Portals to a strict lane: it *reaches* folders, it does **not** classify (that's frontmatter), does **not** switch gates (verified: it pins folder/tag "spaces," not notes, and has no public API), and does **not** query (that's Bases) — the "three orthogonal layers" boundary (`portals-design.md` §5). No tag-portals because Memoria classifies by typed frontmatter, not `#tags`, so tag-portals and the auto `_Tag Notes` folder are dead weight (§1); `journal`/`properties` modules dropped because there's no daily-note workflow and properties are redundant with the Bases/badge tier (§4).

- **What:** Portals *replaces* the file explorer only via its own `replaceFileExplorer: true`; the core `file-explorer` plugin stays enabled as fallback. — **Why:** Portals replaces a *core Obsidian surface*, so if it breaks on an upgrade, navigation breaks — disabling the core plugin would also break reveal-in-explorer, context menus, drag-and-drop, and Portals' own integration (`portals-design.md` §7, `ui-architecture-alpha7.md` §10). This is a gated adoption under ADR-74, not a free "adopt."

---

### UI / navigation shell (the headline change)

- **What:** Gate navigation is re-implemented as **four dashboard notes in one persistent shell**, retiring the ADR-68 workspace-swap. New `src/gates/{inbox,library,knowledge,project}.md`, each `type: gate`, embedding its gate's Bases views via `![[base#View]]`, carrying empty-state `[!brief]` copy and a **wikilink nav row** header (`**Inbox** · [[gates/library|Library]] · …`). — **Why:** a gate is a *job*, not a saved pane layout; implementing it as an Obsidian workspace over-implemented the requirement — a layout swap tears down the PI's open notes (violates "preserve context"), must be re-vendored as plugin state (fights ship-in-vault), and needs an extra plugin (`workspaces-design.md` §0–§4; ADR-81 Context/Decision). The switch is *"opening a different note,"* not *"rebuilding the window."* Base-embed + per-view targeting (`![[claims.base#By maturity]]`) and tab-reuse on a plain wikilink click were both **sandbox-verified** (Obsidian 1.12.7), which is what made the zero-plugin nav row shippable.

- **What:** The gate set is **Inbox / Library / Knowledge / Project**; the triage gate is renamed **Desk → Inbox** and **Studio is deferred**. — **Why:** derived from JTBD verbs against surfaces that actually ship (`workspaces-design.md` §3). The ADR-68 "room metaphor" (Desk/Library/Studio) *broke* once Knowledge and Project gates were added — those aren't rooms — so "Desk" became the odd label; "Studio" was the spatial-synthesis/Canvas mode, and Canvas is deferred, so shipping a Studio gate would violate the "no gate whose content is deferred" rule (R7). ADR-81 explicitly **overrides ADR-68's rejection of "Inbox"**: the collision with `inbox/` is coherent (the gate *is* the inbox queue) rather than harmful, so it's the one-name-per-thing rule, not a violation.

- **What:** `src/home.md` is gutted from a ~133-line control panel (Dataview status strip + Act buttons + Workspaces buttons + Dashboards suggestion callouts) down to a single `[[gates/inbox|Open Inbox]]` link plus a "Homepage opens Inbox; this is a fallback" note (`src/home.md`). The Homepage plugin's target changes `home` → `gates/inbox` (`src/.obsidian/plugins/homepage/data.json`). — **Why:** the PI should land on "what needs me?" every session, not a separate control panel (ADR-81: "launch opens the working gate rather than a separate control panel"). Global actions moved from `home.md` Buttons into the Commander ribbon so they're reachable from any note, fixing #664's column-of-buttons.

- **What:** Commander loses its three workspace-switch ribbon entries (`open Desk/Library/Studio workspace`) (`src/.obsidian/plugins/cmdr/data.json`); the ribbon keeps capture ×3 + delegate + resolve. — **Why:** the gate switcher is now the dashboard nav row, so the ribbon carries only the cross-cutting *global* actions (capture/delegate/resolve), which are gate-agnostic (ADR-72 action layer; `workspaces-design.md` §4 "capture is cross-cutting chrome, never a gate"). Gate-switch ribbon buttons were made *optional* (only if the QuickAdd open-note choices are adopted for hotkeys) and not shipped.

- **What:** Six schema-generated capture forms replace the two hand-maintained ones. Modal Forms `data.json` grows from `source`+`project` to `fleeting/source/claim/hub/project/thesis`; a new generator `scripts/gen-forms.py` (194 lines) emits the form stanzas from `.memoria/schemas/types/*.yaml` + `system/vocabulary.md`, with an extended `tests/test_modalforms.py` drift test. `source` gains `evidence_level`; `entity`→note-picker scoped to `catalog/`; `sources`→catalog-sourced multiselect; `output_mode`→radio (`src/.obsidian/plugins/modalforms/data.json`, `scripts/gen-forms.py`). — **Why:** Modal Forms reads its own `data.json`, not the YAML schemas, so the two silently drift; generating the form from the schema (with a failing pytest on drift) makes the schema the single source of truth (ADR-71 structured capture; `ui-architecture-alpha7.md` §4 "The schema→form consistency mechanism is load-bearing"). Control-by-cardinality (radio ≤4, dropdown 5–12, note-picker for vault refs) kills broken-wikilink entry *at the source* (§4 clean-slate deltas). Forms deliberately **don't** cover inbox cards (engine-written), catalog entities (ingest engine), or projected rows.

- **What:** `src/.obsidian/app.json` ships Memoria-tuned editor settings (was `{}`): `showInlineTitle:false`, `readableLineLength:true`, `newLinkFormat:absolute`, `alwaysUpdateLinks:true`, `newFileLocation:folder`→`notes/fleeting`, `attachmentFolderPath:attachments`, `trashOption:local`, `propertiesInDocument:visible`. — **Why:** each is a targeted fix (`ui-architecture-alpha7.md` §10 table): `showInlineTitle:false` kills the filename+H1 duplication (the direct #659 fix); `newLinkFormat:absolute` gives links the folder prefix the link-color CSS keys on; `alwaysUpdateLinks:true` makes readable-slug renames safe; `newFileLocation:folder` sends a raw Ctrl-N note to fleeting instead of root clutter; `trashOption:local` feeds Portals' Trash module. *(Note: `newLinkFormat:absolute` was flagged "must-verify" against nested-map backlink resolution — an accepted open risk, since the orphan/contradiction views depend on that backlink behavior.)*

- **What:** Core-plugin toggles: `tag-pane`, `daily-notes`, and `templates` all flipped `true → false` (`src/.obsidian/core-plugins.json`). — **Why:** `tag-pane` is low value (Memoria classifies by frontmatter, not `#tags`); `daily-notes` is unused (capture is form-based `fleeting`); core `templates` is superseded by vendored Templater (`ui-architecture-alpha7.md` §10). Lean disables, no back-compat cost given the sandbox-only vault.

- **What:** Empty-state copy is treated as a **release decision**, not a footnote — every gate dashboard carries a `[!brief]` "nothing here yet?" callout, and G6 gates it. — **Why:** alpha.7 ships a near-empty vault; first impressions of the whole UI form on empty Bases, so "empty must read as intentional, not broken" (`ui-architecture-alpha7.md` §8, release plan G6). This was elevated from an open-items line to a top-line release risk in the honest-reframe pass (commit `954c74bf`).

---

### Gate / provenance / edge-authoring

- **What:** No dedicated PI edge-authoring "relate" control ships; `links:` frontmatter remains the sole system of record for edges, authored only via agent propose→confirm (ADR-52) or hand-edit. The Knowledge dashboard carries an explicit `[!verification]` callout naming this gap (`src/gates/knowledge.md`). — **Why:** the architecture pivots on `links:` being the one system of record, but the relate-control is net-new/unbuilt, so it's deferred honestly rather than faked (`ui-architecture-alpha7.md` §0/§4; ADR-81 Consequences: "an acknowledged alpha.7 limitation"). This is a conscious [[pi-direct-access-rule]] gap — flagged as a known limitation, with the relate-control named the priority follow-on. Alternative rejected: rushing a half-built control to close the gap for the deadline (the honest-reframe pass, commit `954c74bf`, explicitly refused to overstate readiness).

---

### Security / supply chain

- **What:** Portals adoption is gated under ADR-74: added to `community-plugins.json` **and** `plugin-provenance-lock.json` (sha256 over vendored files), required plugin count 12→13 (`docs/reference/obsidian-plugins.md`). Workspaces Plus is adopted into **neither** list. — **Why:** Portals is a fourth bundled plugin that replaces a *core surface* and whose install/inspection required explicit human authorization (untrusted-code policy — the agent cannot self-verify this tier), so it must ride the version smoke-test with pinned provenance (`portals-design.md` §7, `ui-architecture-alpha7.md` §9 risk gate / "Open before merge #2"). The design deliberately caps how many core-surface plugins get bundled precisely because of that agent-unverifiable fraction.

---

### Distribution / eval / tests

- **What:** `scripts/install/manifest.sh` adds a line (the `gates/` tree / Portals artifact); `tests/test_workspaces.py` is largely rewritten (309 lines churned) and `test_quickadd.py` drops the workspace-choice assertions; `test_modalforms.py`/`test_schemas.py`/`test_templates.py` extend for the six-form set and new types. — **Why:** golden-copy and drift coverage must follow the retired workspace mechanism and the new gate/form/schema surface (release plan S0–S5 stages; validation log: 383 pytest passed, `dashboard-field-drift,design-system-drift` clean, e2e-smoke green). The e2e smoke asserts a fresh vault "lands on the intentional Inbox shell… reads as empty rather than broken" (G6/S5).

- **What:** The alpha.7 release-doc set: `README.md`, `release-plan-0.1.0-alpha.7.md`, `validation-log.md`, and four `tmp/` scratch design docs (`ui-architecture-alpha7.md` shippable scope, `ui-architecture-future.md` deferred set, `ui-architecture-design.md` full working design, `workspaces-design.md`, `portals-design.md`, `exec-plan`, draft `tmp/dashboards/`). — **Why:** the version's own authoritative intent record. The full design was split by a **non-author reviewer** into "ships = verified/built/low-risk" vs "defer = speculative/unbuilt," and the plan scopes alpha.7 as the UI release while explicitly rolling the shadow/instrument harvest to alpha.8 (scope-reconcile). The honest-reframe §0.1 (commit `954c74bf`) corrected header/§0/§7 overclaims — naming that the projector engine "the real risk, is prose-only, unbuilt, untested" and that "deterministic = mechanism, not trustworthy data."

---

### ADRs

- **What:** New **ADR-81 "Persistent gate dashboards"** (accepted, `assumes: [13,55,70,72,74]`, `supersedes: [68]`); ADR-68 flipped to `status: superseded`, `superseded_by: [81]`; README index updated (`docs/adr/81-…md`, `docs/adr/68-…md`, `docs/adr/README.md`). — **Why:** the durable decision record. Per the ADR-only decision model, the clean-slate design (four scratch docs) had to be folded into an accepted ADR before build. ADR-81 records all four amendments to ADR-68 — the gate set, the switching mechanism (dashboard notes, not workspace swap), the Desk→Inbox rename, and the deferred set — and its Alternatives section documents each rejected path: keep ADR-68 + add a 4th workspace (rejected — still treats a mode as a layout), adopt Workspaces Plus (rejected — removes the *need* for a switcher plugin entirely), use Portals as the switcher (rejected — Portals pins folders/tags, not notes, no API), keep the Desk name (rejected — only coherent inside the retired room metaphor).

---

### Removed / retired (and why)

- **`load-workspace.js` and `open-project-gate.js`** deleted (`src/system/scripts/`), plus the QuickAdd workspace macros and the three Commander workspace ribbon entries. — **Why:** the workspace-swap model is retired *entirely*, with **nothing** replacing it — the switcher is now vault-native dashboard nav rows. This is the net-simplification argument for the whole redesign (`workspaces-design.md` §6; ADR-81 Consequences).
- **Workspaces Plus: never adopted.** — **Why:** it was the planned mechanism to make ADR-68's swap "shippable"; the dashboard-note model removes the need for a workspace-switching plugin, resolving **#666 by elimination** ("there is no workspace-switching mechanism to build," `workspaces-design.md` §6).
- **`workspaces.json` collapsed** from three per-gate layouts (Desk/Library/Studio) to a **single "Memoria" reset layout** (`src/.obsidian/workspaces.json`), with the core Workspaces plugin kept enabled only to *reset* a disarranged window, never per-gate (`saveOnSwitch` off). — **Why:** reproducibility (ADR-55) without the per-gate swap; a mode change is a change of focus, not a window teardown (`workspaces-design.md` §4).
- **`home.md` control-panel** (status strip, Act/Workspaces/Dashboards button clusters) removed. — **Why:** replaced by launch-into-Inbox + Commander ribbon + gate dashboards (ADR-81).
- **`map:graph-claims`/`map:canvas-hub` removed from the deferred list** in `hermes-cli.md` — the graph-visualization pair now ships (#381); only the calibration-gated `map:score-writability`/`map:score-readiness` remain deferred.
- **Deferred (not retired), recorded in ADR-81:** the general projector engine beyond the board mirror, projected telemetry bases (`fleet-health`/`eval-trend`/`skill-lifecycle`), the Canvas/argument-graph spatial axis (and the future Studio gate), the dedicated edge-authoring "relate" control, and a tab/title-bar prose-title plugin (replaced for now by `showInlineTitle:false` + title-led Bases). — **Why:** for a near-empty alpha vault, "fewer surfaces + more Dataview + accept manual refresh beats building a reconciler"; each deferred item is gated on a real triggering need (vault size, demonstrated demand), not a release deadline (`ui-architecture-future.md` §0 gating-triggers table).

---

### Docs (design-bearing reference updates)

- `navigate-the-dashboards.md`, `use-workspaces.md` (retitled "Use the reset workspace"), `obsidian-workspaces.md`, `obsidian-command-palette.md`, `system-actions.md`, `obsidian-plugins.md`, and `set-up-obsidian.md` all rewritten from the three-workspace model to the four-gate/nav-row/Portals model, citing ADR-81. — **Why:** the shipped UI changed, so the how-to/reference surface had to match the folder-of-truth (`obsidian-command-palette.md` now lists the workspace commands as **Retired**: "Gate switching is the nav row in `gates/*.md`"; `obsidian-plugins.md` adds the Portals settings contract and drops "workspace switching" from the Commander/Buttons descriptions).

## alpha.8 — Runtime foundations, observability, and vocabulary discipline (a decisions-and-docs checkpoint)

alpha.8 is the "runtime-foundations & observability" checkpoint whose *implementation* is scoped to every `Readiness: Ready` tracker issue behind the ADR-76 package spine — but whose *shipped* content in this range is almost entirely design: a clean-slate telemetry re-derivation (three planes, ADRs 104-106), the graduation of the ADR-76 deployment spine and a batch of deferred ADRs to `accepted`, the retirement of the `deferred` ADR status in favor of issue-tracker readiness, the split of five bundle ADRs into eighteen single-decision ADRs (84-100), and two large vocabulary corrections — the navigation "gates → spaces" rename (ADR-101 superseding the just-authored ADR-82) and the `graph_maturity/saturation_state` field renames. The only behavior-bearing vault/runtime changes that actually land are the `src/gates/ → src/spaces/` move with its schema, the model-config templating for a local-model overlay, and the enum renames in the project structural-impact code; the rest is decisions recorded and a docs audit enforcing "history lives only in ADRs and `releasing/`." The pressure throughout is that two organizing vocabularies for one activity space, one word ("gate") carrying four load-bearing senses, and a logging posture that "grew signal-by-signal" were all standing signs of unfinished design that a checkpoint had to settle before feature work built on them.

---

### Release process & planning

- **What:** Added the alpha.8 release plan + living ExecPlan — a 9-gate / 6-stage untagged internal checkpoint covering all 17 `Ready` issues behind the ADR-76 package spine (`docs/releasing/0.1.0-alpha.8/release-plan-0.1.0-alpha.8.md`, `README.md`, `tmp/execplan-alpha8-ready-issues.md`; commit c80b6427). Scope is explicitly "refactor + observability + telemetry-shadow plus two already-accepted read-only surfaces, **not** new autonomous behavior" — no calibrated enforcement, no auto-merge/auto-block, no relation-vocabulary expansion, no installer distribution. — **Why:** Like alpha.5-7 the checkpoint stays untagged (`released: false`) because there is no external audience yet; the plan states its own boundary so the "biggest thing between here and cut" (the #727 package spine, hard ordering blocker for #728/#729/#730/#731) governs sequencing and the deferred items are named rather than silently in scope (release plan §1, §4, §5).
- **What:** Release-state moved out of the plan doc entirely into GitHub — the "Release v0.1.0-alpha.8" parent issue (#740) plus gate sub-issues (#741-#749) and stage sub-issues (#756-#761); the plan links rather than restating (release-plan §2-3, §12). — **Why:** "a second list would drift" — the plan summarizes and links so a re-plan does not strand stale dates, consistent with the ADR-75 decision to model live work state in issue fields, not markdown.
- **What:** Retired/disposed all carried-forward `tmp/` scratch across alpha.4-7 release folders (deletions under `docs/releasing/0.1.0-alpha.{4,5,6,7}/tmp/`; commits be840217, aa02089f, 2593076e) after routing durable content to ADRs/issues (README "Tmp disposition check"). — **Why:** the release template's close-out sweep requires every tracked `tmp/` file to be dispositioned into ADRs/system/reference/how-to before a checkpoint closes; e.g. `ui-architecture-future-alpha7.md` split into ADR-102/ADR-103, `install-a-real-package-alpha5.md` folded into ADR-76, `test-env-design-alpha5.md` into ADR-80.

### ADR lifecycle & governance

- **What:** The `deferred` ADR status was **retired entirely**; the lifecycle is now `proposed → accepted → superseded (or rejected)`, and scheduling/readiness moved to the linked GitHub issue's Readiness field (`docs/adr/README.md` "Status lifecycle" and "Mechanics"; `docs/adr/_template.md`; commit 4f524fce). ADR status now "records decision state only." — **Why:** the old rule ("`deferred` is revisited each release cycle, not gated") conflated *is it decided* with *is it ready to build*; separating them lets an accepted decision still carry an implementation issue at Readiness `Later`/`Blocked`/`Needs shaping`, so the ADR set stops doubling as a backlog (README "Scheduling is issue state, not ADR state").
- **What:** As a direct consequence, a batch of previously-`deferred` ADRs graduated to `accepted` with a `date_resolved`: ADR-35 (cross-run skill insights), 38 (pre-file similarity gate), 39 (note-acceptance checklists), 41 (configurable review-gate mode), 60 (cross-vault sharing), 63 (multi-machine deployment), 66 (triage/ranking) — plus the three below given their own scope notes (README index diff). — **Why:** with `deferred` gone, a settled-but-unscheduled decision is simply `accepted`; the graduation is a status-vocabulary migration, not a re-decision (README lifecycle rule).
- **What:** Five "proposal bundle" ADRs were split into single-decision ADRs and marked `superseded`: ADR-58 → 84,85,86,87,88; ADR-59 → 89-94; ADR-61 → 95,96,97; ADR-65 → 98,99,100 (commit 44106756; ADR-58 body now just a "Superseded — split into one ADR per surface" pointer). — **Why:** each bundle recorded "the forward-looking ones together so the felt need is detectable per release," but a bundle can't carry per-decision status once `deferred` is gone and each surface trips its own trigger; splitting gives each a real status (mostly `proposed`) and a tracking issue, e.g. #711/#713 (ADR-58 old body; index diff).
- **What:** New ADR authored-and-accepted this cycle: **ADR-83 Direct PI relate control**, **ADR-84 Read-only Obsidian Inspector**, **ADR-100 Exploration-trace capture** (commit 0bbfe1cf accepts 76/84/100). New `proposed`: **ADR-102 Disposable projection engine**, **ADR-103 Projected Canvas spatial axis**, **ADR-107 OKF interchange bundle** (c2e321c9/8a476f27), **ADR-108 LiteParse** (c2e321c9). — **Why:** covered per-area below.

### Vault / concepts & vocabulary

- **What:** **Navigation "gates" renamed to "spaces"; "gate" reserved for the approval checkpoint** (ADR-101, `accepted`, *supersedes ADR-82*). The four surfaces are now the Inbox · Library · Knowledge · Project **spaces**; note type `gate → space`, enum field `gate → space`, `src/gates/*.md → src/spaces/*.md`, schema `types/gate.yaml → types/space.yaml` (`type: space`, `category: spaces`, `space:` enum), `folders.yaml` map `gate: gates → space: spaces` and category list `gates → spaces`, Homepage/workspace startup target repointed to `spaces/inbox`, plugin-provenance lock digest re-pinned (commit 9aba2c65; ADR-101 Consequences). — **Why:** ADR-82 had just made the four surfaces canonical and called them "gates," but "gate" was already the architecturally central word for the structural human approval checkpoint (ADR-03) — a lexical audit found the approval sense outnumbering the navigation sense ~480:190, and "the gate" had become genuinely ambiguous (plus minor collisions: git pre-commit "commit gate," the Hermes "gateway"). The rightful owner (the industry-standard approval-gate sense) keeps the word; navigation takes the newer term. "Spaces" beat "views" because Obsidian already overloads "view" natively — reusing it would relocate the overload, not remove it (ADR-101 Context, Decision, Alternatives). The project *readiness* gate (`project-gate.*`) keeps "gate" — it is a genuine quality gate, now disambiguated from the Project space.
- **What:** **ADR-82 Four-gates canonical vocabulary** authored then immediately superseded — it retired the parallel **Compile/Compose "knowledge cycle"** vocabulary and its phase names, regrouped `how-to-guides/{compile,compose,curate}/ → {inbox,library,knowledge,project}/` (30+ guide renames), deleted `workflows/compile-and-compose.md`, and reconciled `knowledge-cycle.md` to "gates above, lanes beneath" (commit a7323a43; ADR-82). — **Why:** the system described one activity space with two overlapping-but-unaligned vocabularies — the JTBD gates the user actually navigates, and a Compile/Compose pipeline organizing the docs — plus a third partial "two modes" framing; carrying two organizing vocabularies "taxes the reader's cognitive model and is a standing sign of an unfinished design." A flow is a *process* decomposition, not a *jobs* decomposition, and it hid the high-frequency Inbox job — so the gates win and the cycle is removed outright, not demoted to a narrative (a narrative in its own vocabulary is still a second model to reconcile). The agent lanes are untouched — they are the agents' internal work breakdown, a different actor (ADR-82 Decision/Alternatives).
- **What:** Renamed project/gap/thesis schema enums: `graph_maturity → argument_stage` (with value `immature → developing`) and `saturation_state → evidence_saturation`, across `schemas/types/{project,gap,thesis}.yaml` and the computing code `operations/processing/project/structural_impact.py` (commit a7323a43). — **Why:** part of the one-JTBD-vocabulary terminology cleanup — the field names now say what they measure (argument development stage; evidence saturation) rather than graph-jargon, and `developing` reads as a stage rather than a judgment ("immature") (commit a7323a43 body).
- **What:** Documented the **Project Readiness field** and recorded the retirement of `Area`/`Type`/`Priority` GitHub Project fields (ADR-75 amendment note: "the live Project carries `Status` and `Readiness` only"; commits f2f0520a/ee2e753e/89588b3d; `docs/contributing/issue-tracking.md` rewrite). — **Why:** `Readiness` was added to "separate 'is it decided' from 'is it ready to build'" — the exact split that let `deferred` be removed from ADRs; `Area/Type/Priority` were retired as unused planning overhead. The decision to model planning state in Project fields (not labels/markdown) is unchanged (ADR-75 amendment).

### Profiles / runtime

- **What:** Per-profile Hermes `config.yaml` model block changed from hardcoded kilocode cloud gateway (`provider: kilocode`, `base_url: https://api.kilo.ai/...`, `default: ~anthropic/claude-haiku-latest`) to installer-substituted tokens `{{MODEL_PROVIDER}}` / `{{MODEL_BASE_URL}}` / `{{MODEL_DEFAULT}}` plus a `{{MODEL_LOCAL_CONTEXT}}` overlay marker, across all profile configs; the config header now says the installer substitutes "Python, vault, qmd, and model tokens at deploy time" (commit 30075fb3; `docs/reference/installer.md`). — **Why:** the "local model overlay" work — deployment shouldn't bake one cloud provider into shipped config; templating the model reference at install lets a local-model deployment be an overlay rather than a fork of every profile. **Why (partial):** commit message is terse ("Finish alpha7 QA docs and local model overlay") — inferred from the diff and installer.md that this enables an offline/local-model deployment option; not fully documented in-range.
- **What:** Executed the **`engine → operation` rename** (ADR-69, already decided) across `src/` and docs prose — tool-registry, vocabulary.md, why-specialist-profiles, and dozens of skill/SOUL files now say "operations" not "engines"; the "Linter and the sweeps" are described as *operations*, not agents (commit a7323a43; `tool-registry.yaml`, `why-specialist-profiles.md`). — **Why:** ADR-69 named the deterministic layer "operations"; this is execution of that decision, closing residual "engine" terminology so the posture argument reads cleanly (zero-LLM deterministic work "has no posture at all, so it is not an agent: it is an operation").
- **What:** Cleaned the tool-registry / why-specialist-profiles prose of lineage/history — dropped the "seven specialists it used to run," the old Librarian/Mapper/Socratic/Verifier/Coder/Linter derivation, and the "ADR-21 retired the alpha.1 Coder-lane terminal+file exception" aside; the Engineer is now stated plainly as "MCP-only — no terminal or file access (ADR-21)" (commit ab9a43c8; `tool-registry.yaml`, `why-specialist-profiles.md`). — **Why:** the docs-audit rule that history lives only in ADRs and `releasing/` — everywhere else reads as current-state; the seven→five consolidation narrative is ADR-48's record, not standing rationale (commit ab9a43c8 body).

### Gate / provenance / telemetry

- **What:** **Telemetry re-derived from first principles as three planes** (ADR-104, `accepted`; new `docs/explanation/architecture/telemetry-architecture.md`; commit c75a2290): **Audit** (forensic, content-free, append-only, per-write SHA-256 pairing), **Analytics** (content-free operational/publication events; derived metrics are pure reproducible projections, never a second source of truth), **Diagnostic** (why Memoria's own deterministic code broke — the previously *missing* plane). — **Why:** logging "grew signal-by-signal" and its *posture* was never decided as a whole; the three needs have opposite requirements (forensic permanence vs content-free analytics vs content-bearing debugging), so one substrate "applies the strictest rule to everything and still leaves debugging unserved" — which was the actual state (failures left only a stderr print). Rejected: one log family with levels (serves none), one merged event stream (a wash at n=1, and one bad line poisons everything), a correlation/trace ID (can't thread the unmodified Hermes runtime) (ADR-104 Decision/Alternatives).
- **What:** **Audit integrity substrate is Git, not in-file hash chaining** — Memoria explicitly does *not* add a per-entry `prev_hash` chain; per-write pairing stays, external anchoring (OpenTimestamps/RFC-3161) deferred (ADR-104). — **Why:** the vault is already a Git repo — commit history is a Merkle chain and an out-of-your-control remote is a genuine second trust domain; a linear in-file chain *forks* under multi-machine writes (ADR-63) and is recomputable by whoever owns the file, so it "adds complexity without a guarantee Git does not already give." Tamper-evidence is honestly framed as detective-not-preventive; anchoring against a distinct adversary would be "theater" under single-researcher scope (ADR-24) (ADR-104, telemetry-architecture.md).
- **What:** **Multi-machine partitioning recorded as the migration target** — when >1 machine writes, every Git-synced plane moves to per-machine files (a `machine` stamp in envelope + filename); until then single-machine files stay valid (ADR-104 "Multi-machine partitioning"). — **Why:** exactly one dispatcher runs per vault but the dispatching machine can change over time (ADR-63); per-machine files let two machines append across a Git sync without colliding. Recorded now "so the move is a refactor, not a redesign."
- **What:** **Content-light diagnostic plane** (ADR-105, `accepted`): Memoria's own Python MCP servers/Operations only; lives *outside the vault and outside Git* under `$XDG_STATE_HOME/memoria/diagnostics/`; content-light and deny-by-default for raw payloads (typed error code + SHA-256+length, never the payload); raw capture only via an ephemeral self-disarming session with a visible banner and no persistent "content=on" key; leveled/rotated/bounded; no remote telemetry — sharing is a single user-triggered redacted bundle guarded by a golden-corpus redaction self-test (commit c75a2290). — **Why:** this plane is "the first place vault-derived content could land in a log," and done naively "converts a content-never-logged system into one where a forgotten debug flag plus a routine `git push` exfiltrates unpublished research." The norm across comparable local tools (Obsidian plugins, VS Code, local AI runtimes) is ship-diagnostics-but-default-quiet-and-never-auto-exfiltrate. Rejected: content in `system/logs/` behind an allow-list (can't sanitize free-text error bodies / malformed lines whose payload *is* the content, and that tree is Git-pushed); a persistent content toggle (the classic forgotten-leak foot-gun for a single non-expert user, ADR-24) (ADR-105 Context/Alternatives).
- **What:** **Cost/disposition capture re-pointed to points Memoria controls** (ADR-106, `accepted`): per-card cost/tokens read from the **Hermes session store** (`hermes kanban show <id> --json` → `runs[].metadata.worker_session_id` joined to `~/.hermes/profiles/<lane>/state.db`), emitting Hermes's already-priced figures with provenance (`cost_source`, `pricing_version`); disposition captured at the **review action** (the board/QuickAdd accept/edit/reject), never inferred. Guarded by a pinned Hermes version + a fail-closed "Hermes cost doctor" (commit c75a2290; affects `src/.memoria/mcp/board_export.py`). ADR-20 gap re-pointed from "upstream Hermes limitation" to this capture-path fix (commit 89588b3d). — **Why:** the reference doc's claim that cost was empty because Hermes doesn't surface a card overlay "showed that explanation is misleading" — verification against installed Hermes v0.14.0 found it *does* compute and persist per-call cost, in the session store, reachable without modifying Hermes; the exporter simply queried the one endpoint that drops it. These signals can't be back-filled, so "every day they stay empty is permanently lost data" — the fix must not wait on an upstream change that isn't actually required. Rejected: wait for the overlay (indefinite empty signal); a local model-gateway proxy (re-captures priced data, adds a daemon in the inference hot path) (ADR-106 Context/Decision).
- **What:** **ADR-74 (pinned Obsidian plugin provenance) accepted** — repo now ships a static machine-readable `src/.obsidian/plugin-provenance-lock.json` recording plugin identity, upstream repo, pinned release/commit, artifact digest, license, patch status; a provenance doctor validates it (commit 0bbfe1cf; ADR-74 diff). — **Why:** bundled plugins (ADR-26/55 repo-as-install-unit) previously had no way to prove where a changed `main.js`/`manifest.json` came from; the lock closes the supply-chain gap so CI can verify provenance, while updater/download automation stays deferred behind the doctor being stable (release plan §5).

### Pipeline / ingest / enrichment

- **What:** **ADR-108 LiteParse** proposed (deferred): evaluates replacing the `pymupdf4llm` + OCR local-parse fallback in `extract.py` with LiteParse (LlamaIndex, Rust, Apache-2.0, local-only, no LLM, built-in Tesseract OCR, PDF+DOCX/XLSX/PPTX); keeps the subprocess `rlimit` sandbox and coherence checks; adoption gated behind a head-to-head trial on the real Zotero corpus (commit c2e321c9). — **Why:** PyMuPDF is AGPL-3.0 (the strictest license obligation in the dependency set) and a C parse surface with a CVE history (the reason ADR-30's sandbox exists); LiteParse drops the AGPL dep, swaps a memory-safe Rust core, and adds office-doc/OCR capability, and its design statement is "nearly a restatement of ADR-30/ADR-32." Deferred, not adopted: the local-parse tier is a last-resort fallback (most full text arrives pre-extracted), so the upside is bounded and "does not justify betting the deterministic spine on a library with no track record" (~3 months old) (ADR-108 Context/Proposal).
- **What:** **ADR-107 OKF import** — a foreign Open Knowledge Format bundle may enter as a new source type through the deterministic ingest pipeline (ADR-30), subject to the normal write/link gates (commit 8a476f27). — **Why:** Memoria's tolerance of OKF's "consumers MUST NOT reject" permissiveness stops at ingest — the gate, not OKF's permissive consumer rule, governs what reaches a canonical surface (ADR-107 Import).

### Retrieval / store / interchange

- **What:** **ADR-107 OKF as import/export bundle format** proposed (deferred): a projection or navigation space may serialize as an OKF Knowledge Bundle (one note → one OKF concept), run through the projection engine's reconciliation (ADR-102); export is **lossy by contract** (typed `links:`/`relationships:` collapse to untyped prose-typed markdown links; `lifecycle`/`maturity`/gate state survive only as ignorable custom frontmatter; the bundle carries no gate/Linter/MCP). Also borrows two cheap conventions: a standardized `index.md` progressive-disclosure manifest and OKF's reserved `# Schema`/`# Examples`/`# Citations` headings (commit 8a476f27). — **Why:** Memoria's substrate was independently arrived at by Google Cloud's OKF (typed-markdown concepts, path-derived IDs, links, reserved `index.md`/`log.md`) — validation of ADR-47/ADR-26 — but Memoria's outbound layer is "its least-defined" and OKF supplies the missing runtime-independent unit, de-risking the deferred Path-4 open-artifact release (ADR-20). Adopted strictly at the boundary, never internally: OKF's prose-typed relationships are "the inverse of Memoria's thesis" (typed edges, ADR-08→52; strict schemas, ADR-28) — "Memoria is deliberately *ahead* of OKF here." Gated because it's a v0.1 draft with a concrete-consumer trigger (ADR-107 Context/Proposal/When).

### Discovery

- **What:** The nightly-discovery / method-displacement / triage decisions were unbundled into individual `proposed` ADRs: ADR-89 learning-to-rank triage, 90 claim-sentence classification, 91 classical prose metrics for the export gate, 92 discovery relevance scoring, 93 keyphrase extraction for tag candidates, 94 record-linkage entity dedup, 95 nightly proactive discovery loop, 96 code-lane keep/revert experiment loop, 97 Writer-proposed candidate claim notes, 98 relation-vocabulary expansion, 99 MASSW-aligned paper aspects (from ADR-59/61/65; commit 44106756). — **Why:** each is a distinct classical-method-over-LLM or discovery-loop decision with its own trigger and tracking issue; bundling hid per-decision readiness once `deferred` was removed. No discovery *behavior* ships this checkpoint — pre-file similarity and shadow proposers stay report-only/telemetry-shadow (release plan §5, G6).

### UI / navigation

- **What:** New `src/spaces/{inbox,library,knowledge,project}.md` space dashboards replace `src/gates/*.md`, with first-run empty-state copy (e.g. Inbox: "Inbox empty? That's the goal.") and a "spaces" nav row; the four dashboards must "read as intentional when empty" (commit 9aba2c65; release plan G8). — **Why:** the gates→spaces rename (ADR-101) plus the day-1 UX gate — empty dashboards previously read as broken rather than as the goal state.
- **What:** Removed the Workspaces-v2 **Desk / Library / Studio** dashboards (`src/system/dashboards/{desk,library,studio}.md` deleted; commit 30075fb3), and renamed the operational-health `skill-lifecycle.md → skill-state.md` dashboard (docs + `src/system/dashboards/`). — **Why:** ADR-81 (persistent gate dashboards) superseded ADR-68 (Desk/Library/Studio workspaces), so the old surfaces are dead code; "lifecycle" is reserved for the note field, so the skill dashboard is renamed to "state" (commit a7323a43 body). "The desk" prose collapsed to "the Co-PI pane."
- **What:** Renamed the agent-client explanation `agent-client-picker.md → agent-client-pane.md` and rewrote it to the current one-agent design, dropping the "four ACP profiles behind a picker" history (commit ab9a43c8). — **Why:** the picker is gone — ADR-48 consolidated conversational roles into the read-only Co-PI, so the doc is retitled to what exists and the picker lineage moves to ADR-48's record (docs-audit: current-state everywhere but ADRs/releasing).
- **What:** **ADR-83 Direct PI relate control accepted** — an Obsidian command/form to pick source, relation type, target, preview the frontmatter change, and write a schema-valid `links:` entry; a convenience writer over the existing contract, not a new source of truth (commit 0bbfe1cf). — **Why:** ADR-52 makes `links:` the authored edge layer, but confirming a relation still meant hand-editing YAML or accepting a proposal through raw note editing; the missing surface "is not a new graph model; it is a safer, faster way for the PI to write the existing field." Rejected: sidecar/standalone edge notes (splits the authored-edge source of truth); Canvas as editor (spatial view, not authoritative); agents writing confirmed relations (relation choice is PI judgment under ADR-52) (ADR-83).
- **What:** **ADR-84 Read-only Obsidian Inspector accepted** (supersedes ADR-58 slice) — a sidebar pane showing board counts, WIP depth, recent audit entries, Linter verdict band; read-only, no write path (commit 0bbfe1cf). — **Why:** debugging surfaces are too scattered to answer "what is loaded, what just happened, what is unhealthy?" without context-switching; stays inside Obsidian and read-only, so it respects ADR-32's MCP-gated boundary. Covers the *live* operational-health view; static HTML snapshots (ADR-87) stay a separate deferred concern (ADR-84).
- **What:** **ADR-102 Disposable projection engine** proposed — a deterministic engine rendering non-markdown sources of record (audit windows, metrics, eval runs, skill state) into disposable, regenerated, consumer-only markdown rows under a strict reconciliation/failure contract (1 source row → 1 artifact; dirty rows quarantined; enum-checked; projector failures raise an Integrity signal + a "last refresh failed" dashboard state) (commit c80b6427/scratch split). — **Why:** the board mirror is the one existing projection and several future surfaces want the same pattern; building them as ad-hoc emitters "would multiply stale-row, schema-drift, cold-cache, and failure-surfacing bugs." Rejected: one-off emitters (repeat the hard parts everywhere); making projections authoritative (second source of truth) (ADR-102).
- **What:** **ADR-103 Projected Canvas spatial axis** proposed — Canvas as a spatial *projection* of authored `links:`, not an authoritative edge store; scratch Canvas is a sense-making workspace whose edges become durable only through the ADR-83 relate control; hardest requirement is incremental-stable layout, proven by a spike or else persisted positions in a governed registry (commit c80b6427/scratch split). — **Why:** ADR-79 gives Project work an argument-graph vocabulary but Canvas JSON is invisible to the Linter/Bases/graph ops — treating hand-drawn edges as truth "would repeat the off-store failure ADR-71 rejected"; without layout stability "regenerated views erase the PI's mental map." ADR-81 amended to point its deferred UI set at ADR-102/103 and its relate-control mention at the now-accepted ADR-83 (commit 89588b3d).

### Distribution / eval / testing

- **What:** **ADR-76 (versioned vault release / reconciling installer) accepted** with a staged "Accepted scope" note (commit 0bbfe1cf): the import-hygiene package half (`src/`-layout, editable install, console scripts, deleting the 17 `sys.path`/`__file__` bootstraps) and the in-process policy core are cleared to proceed; the tarball/signing/copy-install *distribution* half stays deferred (Readiness `Later`) until a no-checkout audience exists — git-tag remains the delivery posture. The installer's reconciliation model was refined from three layers to five lifecycle layers — **Code**, **Authored boundary/contract** (release-wins: gate shim, shipped `lane-overrides/<lane>.yaml`, baseline schemas, crons), **PI configuration** (customize-preserve: `SOUL.md`/`SKILL.md`, PI-added types, lane overlay), **Host-side config** (rendered `~/.hermes/profiles/…`), and **State** — with shipped lane policy re-classified as boundary/contract and PI lane tuning moved to a separate **tighten-only** preserved overlay (may add denies / remove allows, never widen past baseline). The policy core is now *imported* from the installed venv package (bare-interpreter CI-guarded, fail-closed) rather than a vendored copy (ADR-76 diff). — **Why:** the deployable is "a configured vault, not a Python package," and the earlier "make it a wheel" framing "optimizes only the first third" and can't carry SOUL/SKILL/gate-shim/crons. Splitting the authored layer into boundary-vs-PI-config was forced because a security or schema fix must land (release-wins) while PI customization must survive (preserve) — one manifest, per-layer verdicts. The in-process import (over a vendored duplicate) is preferred because a hand-maintained copy "can drift at authoring time"; a boundary that can't load its policy denies rather than waves calls through (ADR-76 Context/Decision).
- **What:** **ADR-29 testing model gained a behavior-named aliasing layer** — `static-contract / component / vault-assembly / workflow-replay / runtime-integration / release-acceptance` alias the historical L0-L5, and the opt-in `scripts/test-l2.sh` live-Hermes smoke is explicitly non-PR/nightly, with ADR-80's model-free `workflow-replay` cassette replay covering the deterministic slice but *not* replacing L2b's live dispatch signal (commit eb6b7440; also commit db4d3817 fixed an e2e-smoke teardown gc-race that failed the gate on a docs-only change). — **Why:** the historical layer names are decision vocabulary but don't say what each layer *proves*; the aliasing is a reader-facing migration, not a required-check rename (CI status-check names stay stable until branch protection and `ruleset-doctor` are updated deliberately). The release plan's stages (S0-S5) map directly onto these behavior names (ADR-29 "Current implementation mapping"; release-plan §3).

### Security

- **What:** No security *behavior* changed; the security posture was strengthened by decision and provenance recording rather than new enforcement — the diagnostic plane's content-exfiltration contract (ADR-105, out-of-Git, deny-by-default, redaction self-test), the ADR-76 fail-closed policy-core import + tighten-only lane overlay, the ADR-74 plugin-provenance lock, and hardened editor paste behavior for the docs vault (disabling VSCode paste-as-formatted-link and file/URL copy-into-workspace; commit 8ab8f59d). — **Why:** each closes a concrete leak/drift surface (research exfiltration via a forgotten debug flag; policy widening past the shipped baseline; unprovable plugin artifacts; silent link/file rewrites into the vault) without adding autonomous enforcement, consistent with the checkpoint's "observability, not new autonomous behavior" boundary (ADR-105/76/74; commit 8ab8f59d body).

### Docs audit (cross-cutting)

- **What:** Enforced "history lives only in `docs/adr` and `docs/releasing`; everywhere else reads as current-state" (commit ab9a43c8, follow-up ee5921f5): rewrote why-specialist-profiles and the agent-client pane to current design, removed the glossary "Retired terms" table (each retirement now lives in its ADR) and the dangling intro pointer, and dropped lineage asides ("the renamed MOC," "the old Verifier," "the Coder-lane exception, now yours," "formerly `_shared.py`," "formerly inline `--self-test` blocks"). Kept as current behavior: the installer's stale-profile pruning, `github_doctor`'s stale-term guard, the cron copy-and-rename at deploy. Also trimmed verbatim repetition in the highest-traffic overview/rationale essays (commit f9e6c066) and tightened the telemetry ADR proposals (commits 9f3d585d/d40f3316). — **Why:** duplicated history in non-historical docs is drift waiting to happen and taxes the reader; ADRs and release folders are the single record of "why it used to be different," and the ADR-73 mechanics rule sanctions repointing broken links (not prose) on a move (commit ab9a43c8 body).

### Retired / removed this release

- **`deferred` ADR status** — retired from the lifecycle; scheduling moved to issue-tracker Readiness (README, `_template.md`).
- **Compile/Compose "knowledge cycle" vocabulary** — retired as an organizing/explanatory model; `workflows/compile-and-compose.md` deleted, how-to tree regrouped by space (ADR-82).
- **The "gates" name for navigation** — retired in favor of "spaces"; `src/gates/`, `types/gate.yaml`, and the `gate:` navigation enum removed (ADR-101). *Why:* one word can't carry the navigation and approval senses without ambiguity.
- **Desk / Library / Studio workspace dashboards** — deleted (superseded by ADR-81 gate/space dashboards).
- **Five ADR proposal bundles (58/59/61/62-adjacent/65)** — dissolved into single-decision ADRs 84-100; the bundle bodies reduced to supersede pointers.
- **Hardcoded kilocode model config in profiles** — replaced by installer-substituted model tokens + local-model overlay.
- **The colon skill-name display form** — retired; skills unified on one kebab-case form (commit a7323a43).

## alpha.9 — The truth-alignment checkpoint: enforce by mechanism, capture with less friction

**Theme:** stop crediting boundaries to labels, and stop describing behavior the code doesn't have. alpha.9 is the "UI/workflow and runtime-gate" checkpoint (`scratchpad/README.md`, `docs/releasing/0.1.0-alpha.9`). Three forces drove it: a **Hermes utilization + gate audit** that found the runtime capability wall was schema-hiding (a curtain, not a wall) with the policy plugin as the only real boundary — and that boundary was incomplete; an **ADR↔code audit** of all 75 accepted ADRs that found 20% not faithfully built and six ADRs crediting enforcement to a description rather than a mechanism; and a **401-paper literature review** whose adversarial refutation + on-box measurement passes forced a correction of the system's own framing (qwen is a *test fixture*, not the production engine). The shipped code is comparatively small (gate `process` fix + a contract doctor, a refined Obsidian capture flow, a runtime-package refactor, telemetry planes); the release's weight is in **verification, ADR corrections, and a new working principle** that changes how every future boundary claim is judged.

---

### Vault / concepts, note types & schemas

- **What:** New first-class **`claim.md` template** with an action-oriented body and a `[!suggestions]` callout + QuickAdd buttons (Link claim / Capture source / Delegate task / Archive claim), `schema_version: 2`, explicit `links.supports/contradicts`, and a `superseded_by` pointer field (`src/system/templates/claim.md`, #819). **Why:** the capture workflow refinement moved claim creation into a template-driven QuickAdd path (`write-claim.js`) so a PI can produce a schema-valid claim and immediately reach its next actions without hand-editing YAML — reducing the friction that pushes work into ad-hoc notes. The `superseded_by` field is the deterministic, human-set pointer the ADR-10 supersession filter needs (see Retrieval below) (`design-update-recommendations.md` §3.4).
- **What:** **`fleeting.md` template reworked** from a prose-prompt stub to a `title`/`body` capture with a triage `[!suggestions]` callout and four action buttons (Promote to claim / Capture source / Delegate task / Archive done); field renamed `thought`→`title` (`src/system/templates/fleeting.md`, #812/#819). **Why:** fleeting capture is meant to be frictionless and *queued for later triage* — "capture should not steal focus" (`capture-fleeting.js` header). The buttons turn a raw capture into a one-click path to its disposition, matching the JTBD action-first inbox design (ADR-70).
- **What:** **Exploration-trace note kind** — a QuickAdd flow records a rejected direction / dead end beside a Librarian map report as an ordinary fleeting note under `notes/fleeting/maps/`, never auto-promoted (`src/system/scripts/record-exploration-trace.js`, #780; ADR-100). **Why:** to make dead ends "visible, searchable, and easy to archive" as project-local context rather than canonical knowledge — negative-results capture the recommendations doc later formalized as a proposal (§4.6). The ADR audit confirms it shipped exactly as decided (ADR-100 IMPLEMENTED).
- **What:** **Zotero Tier-0 catalog stub** materialized — a QuickAdd flow reads the current Zotero selection over the Better BibTeX JSON-RPC and writes a catalog stub + an `intake:source` Librarian card (`src/system/scripts/capture-from-zotero.js`, #782). **Why:** completes the ADR-05/06 citekey-backbone capture path; a code comment records the load-bearing quirk (Zotero's local server rejects any request carrying an `Origin` header, so `curl` is used instead of Obsidian's `requestUrl`) — an external-system idiosyncrasy the AGENTS.md comment rule now requires be documented inline.

### Profiles / runtime (Hermes)

- **What:** **Runtime package spine refactor** — the stdlib-only policy/runtime core moved from `src/.memoria/memoria_runtime/policy/` to a repo-root `memoria/` package (`memoria/runtime/{vaultio,jsonl,time,paths,policy,diagnostics}`), compat paths removed, and shared helpers (`load_json`, retry loops) extracted (#763, #764, #788; the deleted `src/.memoria/memoria_runtime/` tree). **Why:** ADR-76 step 1-3 (the reconciling-installer prerequisite) landed ahead of its own prose; `test_package_spine.py` now pins the old path's *absence*. The ADR audit flags ADR-76's Decision-2 path citation as stale-prose to repoint (`adr-implementation-gap-audit.md`, ADR-76 PARTIAL).
- **What:** **"Build on the installed version; upgrade by verifying, not by reading"** added as a platform-runtime rule in AGENTS.md, with evidence tags (`on-box ✓` / `claim-only` / `untested`) and the ADR-106 upgrade→verify→re-enable order (`AGENTS.md`, #820). **Why:** the audit repeatedly caught the system reasoning about Hermes features from release notes rather than the installed v0.14.0 (`hermes-014-utilization-audit.md`). The rule "blocks shipping on marketing; it does not block upgrading." This is the general form of the **qwen correction**: qwen2.5:7b was repeatedly mis-framed as the production model when it is only the local *test fixture* — the live engines call an LLM API, making on-box numbers pessimistic floors, ingest a per-document API bill, and vault text leave the box on every call (`design-update-recommendations.md` §0c; #818).
- **What:** **Utilization audit disposition of unused/mis-relied Hermes features** (design decisions, mostly deferred): Bitwarden secrets vs the 5×`.env` fan-out (fleet/sandbox win, not a lone-laptop slam-dunk — U1); `auxiliary.*` model routing to Haiku/Flash for cheap side-jobs (production cost lever, moot on the local-qwen box — U2/A2); `reasoning_effort` per lane (recommended in 4 profile comments, set in none — "set it or drop the comment", U3); `session_search` for **Co-PI only** as a deliberate privacy trade (A4); confirmations that `memory` Co-PI-only, native-kanban-bypass, and external-cron are *correct as-is* (A5-A7) (`hermes-014-utilization-audit.md`). **Why:** to separate genuine gaps from deliberate divergences and stop the audit from reading "unused" as "wrong." Per-card `model_override` was flagged as plumbed-but-unwired in 0.14 — "not a feature to just turn on."
- **What:** **`checkpoints.enabled: true` recorded as inert** in the MCP-only model (filed #824 to drop it + the false "reversibility" comment from all 5 profiles). **Why:** Hermes checkpoints trigger only on native `write_file`/`patch`/`terminal`, none of which any Memoria profile ships; real reversibility comes from the `policy_hook` before/after-hash audit pair, not shadow-git (`hermes-014-utilization-audit.md` B5). *(Filed, not landed this release.)*

### Gate / provenance / trust / audit

- **What:** **`process` added to `DENY_DIRECT_TOOLS`** in the policy gate (`src/.memoria/mcp/policy_hook.py`, #825). **Why:** `process` is a real tool in Hermes's `terminal` toolset (`toolsets.py:142-145`) that the denylist missed, so the gate returned `{}` (allow) for it — the exact config-drift the denylist's own "fail closed" comment exists to prevent. The audit ranked this the highest-leverage real gap because ADRs 03/21/46 all ride this one mechanism (`adr-implementation-gap-audit.md` cross-cutting #1).
- **What:** **New `hermes_contract_doctor.py`** — reads the toolset registry from the *installed* Hermes and exits non-zero when any `file`/`terminal`/`code_execution` tool is not in `DENY_DIRECT_TOOLS` (importing the denylist as single source of truth, not re-listing it); also reports (as a non-failing warning) the ~36 egress/side-effect tools the gate allows by default (`src/.memoria/mcp/hermes_contract_doctor.py`, #825; wired into runbook S4). **Why:** to make denylist drift *catchable instead of silent* — "the executable form of AGENTS.md 'build on the installed version, upgrade by verifying'" and the generalization of the ADR-106 cost doctor. A completeness sweep test (`test_policy_gate_completeness.py`) proves the list is enforced, not merely declared, with a `process` regression guard.
- **What:** **Gate audit-completion failures now emit a diagnostics event** (`record_event(component="mcp.policy_hook", code="audit_completion_failed")`) in addition to stderr (`policy_hook.py` `evaluate_post`). **Why:** the audit pair (before/after hash) is the real reversibility/provenance record (ADR-104); a silent audit-completion failure previously left only a stderr line — routing it to the content-light diagnostic plane makes it operator-visible without breaking the agent loop.
- **What:** **Plugin fail-closed contract made explicit** — the gate plugin's broad `except` now carries `# noqa: BLE001 -- policy gate fails closed; any error blocks the write` and the post-hook `# noqa: BLE001 -- never block the agent on audit-completion failures` (`plugins/memoria-policy-gate/__init__.py`, #804/#825). **Why:** the two exception paths have *opposite* correct behaviors (pre-hook must block on error, post-hook must not) and the new AGENTS.md rule requires every `# noqa` to state its rationale on-line.
- **What:** **New working principle "Enforcement is a mechanism, not a label"** in AGENTS.md, with named done-right exemplars (ADR-55/74/80/105) and done-wrong-corrected list (ADR-28/23/60/04/46/41) (`AGENTS.md`, #820). **Why:** the through-line of the entire audit — a guarantee kept being credited to a *description* (a config key, a taxonomy, "the architecture") when a *mechanism* elsewhere actually held it. The canonical example is `disabled_toolsets`: it only hides a tool from the model; `registry.dispatch` still runs any registered tool by name, so the policy plugin's hard-deny is the boundary (`hermes-014-utilization-audit.md` B1; `adr-enforcement-audit.md`).
- **What:** **Enforcement-attribution corrections applied in-place to six ADRs** — 28 (`disabled_toolsets` is UX; plugin hard-deny + default-deny is enforcement), 46 ("only through MCP" bound by `DENY_DIRECT_TOOLS`+default-deny, not the layer contract), 04 (lifecycle write rules enforced by lane globs, not folder naming), 23 (substrate split is a routing table; isolation = per-profile dirs + denylist + card channel), 41 (card column-advance is process discipline; the code stop is at the write in `decision.py`), 60 (the named cross-vault enforcer is *not yet implemented* — a deferred design, not a live guarantee) (`docs/adr/{04,23,28,41,46,60}-*.md`, #820). **Why:** each credited a boundary to a non-mechanism; verified on-box against installed v0.14.0 (`registry.dispatch` has no enablement check; `vault_root()` returns a single root). ADR-60's correction explicitly warns it "must not be read as a live guarantee" and names what a real cross-vault boundary would require (foreign-vault scope + a deny-write test).

### Pipeline / ingest / enrichment

- **What:** **Ingest resolve-merge and structural-impact modules split** — `resolve_merge.py` → `+resolve_merge_logic.py`/`resolve_merge_pubmed.py`; the 813-line `structural_impact.py` → 6 focused modules (analysis/gap/graph/payload/render/survey) (#769, #770, #804). **Why:** helper-drift and duplicate-mirror reduction (a ponytail-audit clean-win, no behavior change); the structural-impact maturity logic itself is unchanged and confirmed exact (`>=5` relations, `>=1 supports`, `>=1 contradicts`; ADR-77 IMPLEMENTED).
- **What:** **classify divergence recorded** (ADR-30 dated note) — the Tier-1 embedding+zero-shot **tag-suggestion layer the ADR calls "the system's value" is not built**, and `classify` diverged to a deterministic OpenAlex-topic mapping (`classify.py:118-154`) (`docs/adr/30-*.md`, #830). **Why:** the audit found ADR-30's "implemented and validated" framing overstated the shipped slice; the recommendation is update-ADR-to-match-code + track the tag layer as deferred (`adr-implementation-gap-audit.md` ADR-30 PARTIAL). The recommendations doc separately confirmed the deterministic-ingest spine as **measured-green** on the test floor (MASSW 6/6 schema-clean, 90% verbatim warrants), retiring the QLoRA budget (§0a, §3.6).
- **What:** **Constrained-decoding engine contract adopted as the ingest direction** (design intent, `design-update-recommendations.md` §3.6, amend ADR-30) — decomposed per-aspect schema-constrained prompts, temperature=0, MASSW five-aspect schema with mandatory "N/A"; **blanket self-consistency dropped**. **Why:** on-box measurement refuted CrossTrace's "~0% compliance" claim (`format=schema` was 6/6 clean even on the test floor), and self-consistency "was free on a local model but is a per-token API bill on the hot path, and the API is more reliable at structure than the qwen floor" — reserve it for genuine uncertainty only (#818, #816).

### Retrieval / derived store

- **What:** **Pre-file similarity shadow telemetry** — QuickAdd source/claim creation now runs a report-only `qmd` neighbour check (top-3 within `notes/claims/`, `notes/sources/`), writes a `pre-file-similarity.jsonl` row, and renders a `[!similarity]` callout; **never blocks, auto-merges, or applies a calibrated threshold** (`src/system/scripts/quickadd-similarity.js`, #774; ADR-38 note). **Why:** alpha.8 shipped the shadow primitive as a passive filing-side signal; calibration/enforcement stays deferred to #562 — the ADR-38 prose was updated to say "shadow primitive, not enforcement" so it isn't read as a live gate.
- **What:** **ADR-10 supersession gap recorded as a live correctness bug** (filed #826) — the "exclude superseded from `query`/`write` by default" half is enforced only in `link-claim.js` ranking + the FAMA linter, with **no retrieval-layer filter** in the find/draft skills (`docs/adr/10`, `adr-implementation-gap-audit.md` ADR-10 PARTIAL). **Why:** a query can surface, and a draft can cite, an already-retired claim — the exact FAMA failure ADR-10 exists to prevent, live in alpha.9's own domain. The fix is deterministic and cheap (honor the human-set `superseded_by` pointer), so it belongs in the alpha.9 recommendations cut, not the deferred contradiction-precision engine.
- **What:** **Retrieval recommendations re-anchored to `qmd`** (the existing local hybrid BM25 + vector + cross-encoder-rerank index) instead of an abstract "BM25+dense" (`design-update-recommendations.md` §0c/§4.1; #818). **Why:** a grounding error symmetric to the qwen one — the recs proposed building a retriever that already ships. The substantive shift: since qmd *already* cross-encoder-reranks, the near-term action is to **evaluate that reranker on reasoning-relevance** (Wei 2026: MS-MARCO cross-encoders hurt there), not "add a reranker"; and what is retired is **cosine's role as *arbiter*** (the pre-file gate), never cosine as retriever — measured 0/8 on negation traps where NLI scored 8/8 (§0a).
- **What:** **Contradiction detection re-tiered down to a cheap soft-flag for alpha.9**; the NLI + decomposed-variable-match gate + MaxSAT apparatus **deferred** (`design-update-recommendations.md` §0e/§3.1). **Why:** a new N=1 error-cost model — a missed/late contradiction is *self-correcting and low-cost* for a single PI, so a precision engine is over-built and its propose-only queue (~28% precision, Mitchell 2022) would dominate the scarce supervision budget.
