On-box measurement showed NLI *confidently mints false contradictions* (0.94-1.00) on same-topic/different-variable pairs, unrecoverable by a confidence threshold; the decomposed gate helped (recall 4/6, FP 6/7→1/7) but still leaks negation/argument-swap. So the engine is gated on in-domain proof that the miss costs something (#813, #815, #816).

### Discovery / clustering

- **What:** **Clustering recommendations grounded to the built `cluster_mcp`** — per-aspect coding-then-clustering framed as a *delta to `cluster_model_topics`* (BERTopic already does UMAP+HDBSCAN) and RWR as an *added traversal on `cluster_build_graph`*, not a new stack (`design-update-recommendations.md` §4.2; #818). **Why:** third grounding sweep — the recs were "greenfield-when-it-exists." The ADR audit confirms `cluster_mcp` is fully built (ADR-33 IMPLEMENTED: NetworkX communities + optional BERTopic with structured degradation, lane sandbox intact).
- **What:** **`clustering.quality_thresholds` calibration contract** added to `calibration.yaml` — `production_enabled: false`, null silhouette/coherence floors, `min_reviewed_maps: 20`, `max_cluster_churn_rate` (`src/.memoria/schemas/calibration.yaml`, #777). **Why:** typed-graph/topic clustering may surface ranked maps only after real reviewed runs calibrate it (#379/ADR-66); null thresholds mean shadow/report-only — the same shadow-first discipline as the pre-file gate.

### UI / navigation / dashboards / panes

- **What:** **New read-only `memoria-inspector` Obsidian plugin** — a right-pane `ItemView` that renders board-state, audit-log, and Linter-verdict JSONL with a 60s refresh, ribbon icon, and command; no write path wired (`src/.obsidian/plugins/memoria-inspector/{main.js,manifest.json,styles.css}`, #778; ADR-84). **Why:** realizes ADR-84 (an operational inspector that "reads … adds no write path"); the audit confirms it as a real plugin and marks the ADR-84 "readiness" tracking issue #697 stale — close it.
- **What:** **Day-one empty-state guidance** across the four spaces — `spaces/inbox.md` gains a "First actions" `[!suggestions]` callout (capture source / capture fleeting / ask the Co-PI) and a "Fleeting notes → To process" queue; `knowledge/library/project.md` similarly (#781). **Why:** an empty inbox is the goal, but a brand-new vault gave the PI no next action; the callouts turn the empty state into an onboarding surface.
- **What:** **QuickAdd capture flow overhauled** — new `capture-fleeting.js`, `write-claim.js`, `archive-claim.js`, `archive-fleeting.js`, shared `quickadd-utils.js` (extracted `run`/`shq`/`slug`/`uniquePath`/`yamlString`/`fnv1a`), and `capture-from-url`/`catalog-source`/`delegate-task` refactored onto the shared helpers; QuickAdd `data.json` rewired (#812, #819). **Why:** capture friction and per-script helper drift; the shared utils remove duplicated POSIX-quote/slug logic (a ponytail-audit finding) and the template buttons give every note type a direct path to its next action (ADR-72 command surfacing).

### Distribution / install / evaluation / measurement

- **What:** **Plugin provenance doctor** (`plugin_provenance_doctor.py`) wired into required lint/L0, checking `plugin-provenance-lock.json` (#767; ADR-74), plus a **live Hermes L2 smoke** (#768). **Why:** ADR-74's checksum "proves the reviewed artifact is present (explicitly NOT trust)"; the audit names ADR-74 an exemplar of the new principle ("provenance doctor in the required lint, honest about the limit of the guarantee").
- **What:** **Cost-and-disposition analytics + content-light diagnostics plane** — `board_export.py` split out `board_export_cost.py`/`board_export_events.py`/`board_export_projection.py`/`board_export_common.py`; `memoria/runtime/diagnostics.py` (XDG dir, content-light, self-disarming raw capture, redaction golden-corpus self-test) (#772, #773; ADR-104/105/106). **Why:** completes the three telemetry planes. The audit confirms the cost join works end-to-end (ADR-106) and the diagnostic plane is fully built + unit-tested (ADR-105; marks tracking issue #736 stale). One residual noted: `cost-misses.jsonl` has a writer but no aggregator (ADR-104).
- **What:** **`ruff format` adopted as the single source of Python layout** (line-length 100) plus an expanded curated lint ruleset (bugs/idioms/security, UP017 migration, fix-or-justify-every-finding); recorded as **new ADR-110**; the bulk reformat isolated in `.git-blame-ignore-revs` (#790, #794, #796). **Why:** "all Python is agent-generated, so there was no human-authored style to protect — only per-session entropy a formatter now holds steady" (ADR-110). This is the source of most of the large line-count churn in the diff (pure reformat, 433 tests unchanged). AGENTS.md gained a **Python style** section (docstring/comment/line-length rules; `D` pydocstyle deliberately off — presence is a judgement call, not a lint gate).
- **What:** **New ADR-109 — project-management native views** (`projects.base` + Modal Form + schema-frontmatter writes; zero rejected PM plugins bundled) (#783; `docs/adr/109`). **Why:** records the project-management research direction as a native-views decision; the audit confirms it IMPLEMENTED.
- **What:** **401-paper literature review wired into foundations/provenance/bibliography** and delivered as the `design-update-recommendations.md` working artifact (four passes: review → refutation → on-box measurement → grounding) (#784, #797-#818). **Why:** the review claimed the corpus "re-derives" Memoria's skeleton, but the refutation pass attacked 14 load-bearing bets and *none survived intact*, and measurement then beat both — establishing the trust order **measured > refuted > literature-pull** and the `current-state-baseline.md` instrument (fill from observed usage before committing the build order; "need-push, not literature-pull").
- **What:** **`docs/adr/` excluded from the Jekyll docs site**; nav frontmatter stripped from all 112 ADR files (#801). **Why:** ADRs are decision records, not published pages; this is the source of the uniform "3 lines removed" across nearly every ADR in the diffstat.

### Security

- **What:** **Egress allow-by-default recorded as a live P0** (filed as interim hard-deny #832 + structural default-deny #822) — the gate hard-denies file/terminal/code-exec but allow-by-defaults `web_*`/`browser_*`/`send_message`/`delegate_task` (returns `{}`), so for egress the sandbox rests entirely on `disabled_toolsets` schema-hiding (`hermes-014-utilization-audit.md` B2; `hermes-clean-slate-design.md` §2a). **Why:** on the injection path this is unmitigated — the threat model is now stated: a **poisoned source/paper** whose text reaches the LLM on every ingest call (data > code, Greshake/Debenedetti) and induces a tool call; concrete because ingest processes untrusted papers. The critique round forced two admissions onto the page: **merged ≠ deployed** (the deployed `~/Memoria-test` gate is a pre-#825 build with no `process`, so even the landed fix isn't running — #832 includes a redeploy + deploy-freshness check), and the second independent **fail-open** (the gate fails open if the plugin fails to register/import — filed #823). *(Findings + interim fix filed this checkpoint; the structural default-deny is the follow-through.)*
- **What:** **MCP-only sandbox reframed "necessary, not sufficient"** (`design-update-recommendations.md` §2/§0b.5). **Why:** least-privilege doesn't defend against poisoned *data*, which is the dominant threat — an architectural finding, not benchmarkable, that reframes the whole safety cluster (ADR-27/32/46/28) as a *write* boundary that says nothing about egress under injection.

### ADRs governing the release

- **What:** **All 75 accepted ADRs audited against code** — 4 UNIMPLEMENTED (60, 83, 35, 39), 1 DIVERGED (55), 10 PARTIAL (27, 41, 77, 30, 56, 78, 10, 45, 76, 73), 60 IMPLEMENTED; dated in-place implementation-gap notes added to ADR-83/30/55 and enforcement-attribution notes to ADR-28/23/60/04/46/41 (#830, #820). **Why:** "`accepted` is not load-bearing" — nothing detects when code drifts from an accepted ADR's claims, so silent partials (ADR-10, ADR-30) present as done for months. Root-cause fix filed as an **ADR↔code drift doctor** (#833), the contract-doctor pattern applied to ADR claims. The 20%-not-faithfully-built figure is called a *floor*, since the 60 "implemented" came from a shallow one-line-cite pass.
- **What:** **ADR-55 recorded as DIVERGED** — `golden_restore.py upgrade` (the three-way reconcile) is deliberately not shipped and `test_golden_restore.py::test_upgrade_command_is_not_shipped` pins its absence; ADR-55's `system/**`-deny + restore + SHA manifest remain a *done-right exemplar* (`docs/adr/55`, #830). **Why:** the ADR prose is stale on the upgrade clause while the built+tested part stands — the AGENTS.md ADR-55 exemplar cites only the built part.
- **What:** **Stale-prose ADR batch filed** (#827) — ADR-13 (`spaces/inbox` not `gates/inbox`), 18 (one-way rename), 27/46 (allowlist ≠ boundary), 31 (`--self-test` gone), 32 (`retraction.py`), 76 (policy path moved), 106 (file moved + "version-pinned" overstated), 73 (Rule 3 "purged" is literally false — 7 bare `(D##)` codes remain, unenforced). **Why:** "stale-prose, correct-code" was the dominant audit pattern — an update-the-ADR action, not code work, but a defect under the zero-tolerated-contradictions rule.
- **What:** **AGENTS.md mirror rule** — mirrors are allowed only as consumer views that name the owning source and are drift-checked whenever they repeat machine-readable contracts (counts, rosters, fields, scopes, commands, lifecycle values, required checks) (`AGENTS.md`, #792/#820). **Why:** duplicate-mirror/helper drift (#792) — the same class of defect as the ADR stale-prose, one level up in the docs.

### Removed / retired (and why)

- **Retired: cosine similarity as the contradiction/supersession *arbiter*** (kept as `qmd`'s retriever). **Why:** measured negation-blind (0/8) — a similarity score cannot tell "same" from "opposite" (`design-update-recommendations.md` §7, `[provisional, n≈6]` + BRIGHT corroboration).
- **Dropped: the QLoRA fine-tuning budget.** **Why:** the live engine is an API (not fine-tuneable) and the frozen test floor already clears schema compliance (6/6) — `[architecture]`, doubly moot (#814, #818).
- **Deferred/killed for alpha.9: the high-precision contradiction engine** (NLI + decomposed gate + MaxSAT), **blanket self-consistency**, the **greenfield retriever/clustering stack**, and **auto-applied contradiction/supersession links**. **Why:** the N=1 error-cost model (missed contradiction is low-cost/self-correcting), the API-per-token-bill fact, the already-built `qmd`/`cluster_mcp`, and the propose-only-is-the-most-expensive-default budget arithmetic, respectively (`design-update-recommendations.md` §1 "Explicitly NOT doing", §7).
- **Removed: `memoria_runtime/` compat tree, `_parse_ts`/`_safe_name` aliases, hand-rolled `is_relative_to`.** **Why:** ponytail-audit clean-wins after the `memoria/` package spine landed — no behavior change (#788, #800, #804).
- **Retired framing: qwen-as-production-engine, "cheap local model" / "local-by-choice" as production bets, "keep the bits local."** **Why:** the qwen-is-test-fixture correction — these described a system that doesn't exist; the live engine is an API, so vault text leaves the box on every call (#818). *(Whether high-volume ingest should move to a local model is left open as §0d/§8.1, not decided.)*

**Note on scope:** the `design-update-recommendations.md`, `hermes-*.md`, and `*-audit.md` files are explicitly *working artifacts* deleted at checkpoint close-out — their recommendations "land in ADRs; this doc proposes them." They are cited here as the authoritative *intent* for the release; most of their build items are filed as issues (#822-#833) or deferred, not shipped as code in this range. The durably shipped code is the gate `process` fix + contract doctor, the capture-workflow refinement, the inspector plugin, the telemetry planes + provenance doctor, the runtime-package refactor, the ruff-format adoption, and the in-place ADR corrections.

*(Where a commit body was terse (#763-#782 largely one-line), the design intent above is inferred from the shipped files + the corroborating ADR audit and is marked as such in-line; the enforcement/gate/qwen reasoning is quoted directly from the release's own audit docs and commit bodies.)*

## alpha.10 — The post-alpha.9 consolidation checkpoint: Hermes 0.17 acceptance, measurement-gated cleanup, and a clean-slate rebuild of the Obsidian surface + type schema (ADR-114–119)

**Theme.** alpha.10 is not a feature release — it is an internal validation checkpoint that gathers every design change landed after alpha.9 into one coherence boundary (`docs/releasing/0.1.0-alpha.10/release-plan-0.1.0-alpha.10.md`, §1). Two forces drove it. First, an **in-place Hermes 0.14→0.17 runtime upgrade** that had to be *accepted against on-box evidence* before any dependent work could land, paired with a deliberately austere, **measurement-first** stance: the `#859` current-state baseline was the gate that decided which memory/runtime cleanup was worth building versus deferring or killing (`tmp/execplan-alpha10.md` §3, `tmp/current-state-baseline.md`). Second, a run of **clean-slate design reviews** that produced ADR-111 through ADR-119 — rethinking onboarding, the left-pane/dashboards/spaces surface, the type-naming scheme, and the type schema itself — from first principles rather than from the accreted implementation. The net across the schema/surface work is *consolidation and deletion*, not new machinery.

> **Note on the range.** `830ecd31..383034b0` (70 commits) spans from just before the alpha.9 close commit (`3ba5081f`/#858) through `main` at `e56aba40`/#928 plus the release-execution fixes. The release plan explicitly scopes alpha.10 as "the full post-alpha.9 change set" (release-plan §1), so the alpha.9-tagged finalization commits (`35b53426`–`3ba5081f`) are treated here as in-scope design-bearing work.

---

### Vault / concepts, type schema, and document naming

**What:** The umbrella term for a typed object changed **"note type" → "document type"**; `docs/reference/note-types.md` → `docs/reference/document-types.md` and `docs/explanation/knowledge/note-types.md` → `document-types.md` (renames R069/R086 in the diff), with schema/code comments and prose following (`1319b93e`, ADR-117). A *note* is now one **kind** of document (`source`/`claim`/`hub`/`fleeting`), so the `notes/` folder is a legitimate subset rather than a circular "notes are notes."
**Why:** A clean-slate walk of all 26 types found there was *no stated naming rule*, so apparent overloads read as bugs (a reviewer "fixing" the kanban `worker-card`→`worker-row`) and new types could drift with nothing to check them against; and `notes/` doubled the medium word (every object is a note, yet one category is "notes"). The tempting fix — rename `notes/`→`knowledge/` — was rejected because a `knowledge/` folder would collide *with a different meaning* with the Knowledge space (the folder feeds both Library's `source` docs and Knowledge's `claim` docs). Changing the umbrella term is strictly cheaper: "No folder moves, no `type:` values change, no paths change" (ADR-117 Context + Consequences).

**What:** A formal **naming rule** was recorded: singular common noun in the field's ubiquitous language, scoped to one of four *kinds* carried by the category folder — **Record** (`catalog/`,`notes/`,`projects/`), **Signal** (`inbox/`), **Surface** (`spaces/`), **Control** (`system/`) — plus a **no-collision corollary** (a folder may not also name a navigation surface with a different meaning) (ADR-117 Decision).
**Why:** To end the recurring "card"/"note" debates by naming the bounded-context and no-collision principles, and to validate already-correct names (`worker-card`, `worklist-item`, the catalog six) rather than churn them. `fleeting` is kept as the one explicit adjective exception because it is the entrenched capture term and renaming it would force runtime migration for no ambiguity gain. Kind-prefixed names (`entity:paper`) were rejected as over-engineered — the folder already encodes the kind (ADR-117 Alternatives).

**What:** ADR-119 promoted the type schema from a **fields+enums fragment to (the design for) the complete declarative contract** covering all eight concerns — identity/placement, fields-as-specs, controlled vocab, lifecycle state machine, typed edges, invariants, generation metadata, evolution — with the Linter becoming a generic engine that *executes* declared rules and forms/templates/`folders.yaml`/reference docs *generated* from the schema via one `create(type, inputs)` engine serving both the human form and the agent writers (ADR-119 Decision, `76b2a148`).
**Why:** The contract was scattered across four hand-synced places — invariants hard-coded in `detectors.py` (`thesis`→`promoted_at`, `claim`→`sources`), defaults in templates, labels "nowhere," placement split between `folders.yaml` and the schema — so adding a type meant editing four files and the field list was re-encoded three times (schema, template frontmatter, Modal Form), which had *already drifted* (the source form added `summary`, dropped `links`) (ADR-119 Context). This is Memoria's own single-source-of-truth philosophy applied to creation, not just validation. Full JSON Schema was rejected as the format because it models a document's internal shape, not the vault's placement/graph/referential layer, so a custom layer survives regardless; an enriched native DSL projectable to JSON Schema later was chosen (ADR-119 Decision §5, Alternatives).

**What (implemented this release):** Type schemas gained **`initial_lifecycle`** declared uniformly (e.g. `claim: current`, `source/fleeting: proposed`), **`source_type` became an enum** (`[paper, dataset, repository, web-page, report]`, was free `str`), a **`sample: bool`** optional field was added across content/space types, and each user-facing type gained an in-schema **`creation.form`** block (field, label, description, input widget, vocabulary/enum bindings) — landed for `claim`, `source`, `project`, `fleeting` (`src/.memoria/schemas/types/*.yaml`, `5a7209ed`/`cb81a255`).
**Why:** These are the confirmed-feasible ADR-119 phases (invariants/state uniformity + schema-owned forms). The `source_type` case is the worked example: the *form* already rendered it as a required five-value select while the *schema* said optional `str`, so generating the form from the schema would have *lost* the controlled vocabulary — the enum had to move into the schema (ADR-119 §6, `b92941ed`). The `sample` flag exists so sample-vault documents can be excluded from "New this week" digests and found by the remove command (see UI/sample-vault below).

**What:** The **`index` document type was removed** — the type, its `index.yaml` schema, template, and the `notes/indexes/` skeleton folder are gone (`folders.yaml` drops `index: notes/indexes` and the skeleton entry; `index.yaml` deleted, `24540227`/ADR-119).
**Why:** Its schema was title-only and expressed none of its "register" purpose, it had no creation path, and its register function (a list of hubs) is already the `hubs.base#Hubs index` view — "the one type whose schema simply does not match its purpose" (ADR-119 §6).

**What:** Two new **`spaces`-category types were added** — `queue` and `maintenance` (`queue.yaml`, `maintenance.yaml`, both `category: spaces`, `initial_lifecycle: current`) — and the `space` type's `space` enum **dropped `inbox`** → `[library, knowledge, project]`; `folders.yaml` maps `queue → spaces/` and `maintenance → spaces/` (`16c6844e`, `616bdc1b`, ADR-115/116).
**Why:** The Inbox is a *state that converges to empty*, not a durable room, so modeling it as a co-equal fourth space was wrong (see Discovery/UI). Maintenance is a separate weekly-cadence collection split off from the daily queue. Templates deliberately exclude `queue`/`maintenance` (authored, not template-created), keeping the template count stable at 20 (ADR-115 Consequences).

**What:** The retracted sample source's supersession pointer moved from a top-level `superseded_by:` into the source's `links:` map (`0f9da419`).
**Why:** ADR-119 made the type schema the complete field contract; `source.yaml` has no `superseded_by` (that field belongs to claim/thesis schemas), so the PREDIMED-original fixture violated no-unknown-field validation. Moving it into `links: map` (which `source.yaml` allows) preserves the supersession relationship while conforming to schema (commit body `0f9da419`).

---

### Profiles / runtime (Hermes 0.17)

**What:** Hermes was upgraded **v0.14.0 → v0.17.0** in place (upstream `b1b20270`; RC validated on `74265c8e`) and the config schema migrated **v23 → v30** — profile `config.yaml` files now carry `_config_version: 30` and `context_file_max_chars: 30000` (`tmp/hermes-upgrade.md`; `src/.memoria/profiles/*/config.yaml`; validation-log).
**Why:** `hermes doctor` flagged the pre-upgrade default profile as stale (unknown provider `ollama`, config `v23→v30`); the upgrade + migration is pure hygiene that unblocks everything else, and the plan made it the G2 gate that "gates everything else: no cleanup lands on an unaccepted runtime" (`tmp/execplan-alpha10.md` §3).

**What:** Profile capability blocks are now **materialized from `tool-registry.yaml`** by a new `scripts/render_profile_configs.py`; each `config.yaml` is stamped "Generated by scripts/render_profile_configs.py; edit tool-registry.yaml" (new ADR-115 *profile-config-materialization*, the second ADR numbered 115).
**Why:** ADR-27 already made `tool-registry.yaml` the source for each profile's positive toolsets/MCP filters, but the checked-in configs *repeated those derived blocks by hand* across five profiles — the highest-risk capability surface copied five ways. Rendering lets CI fail on stale generated configs instead of relying on humans to copy allowlist edits, while keeping runtime "boring" (Hermes still receives plain `config.yaml`, no install-time template language). A full profile compiler was rejected as too broad (ADR-48 already retired it); Hermes-native inheritance isn't available on the installed v0.17 model (ADR-115 profile-config Context/Alternatives).

**What:** Gating shifted to a **positive `platform_toolsets` allowlist** — every profile now declares the exact toolset list per Hermes runtime platform (cli/cron/api_server/telegram/…/google_chat), plus per-MCP-server `tools.include` filters (e.g. `policy: [check_permission, complete_write]`, `qmd: [search, vsearch, deep_search, get, status]`); the subtractive `disabled_toolsets` list is retained as belt-and-suspenders (now also naming `session_search`) (`be6ebbb0`, `src/.memoria/profiles/memoria-copi/config.yaml`; `tool-registry.yaml` header rewritten to "the policy-gate plugin reads this on pre_tool_call and blocks calls outside the profile allowlist").
**Why:** The 0.17 eval found subtractive denylists "brittle when Hermes adds new tools" — a new upstream toolset would be *granted by default*. A positive allowlist closes new tools by default; the eval demanded a live deny-path test to *prove* it closes rather than merely hides them before switching (`tmp/hermes-017-feature-eval.md` "Used sub-optimally"; execplan §3 fourth). This is the reconciled, on-box-verified item (no longer speculative), so it landed.

**What:** The **`memory` toolset became profile-scoped to `memoria-copi` only** (enforced in `policy_hook.py` via `PROFILE_SCOPED_DIRECT_TOOLS = {"memory": {"memoria-copi"}}`), with memory config set to `write_approval: true`, `user_profile_enabled: true`; and Co-PI's memory `provider: ''` keeps canonical knowledge in the vault (`450f659d`, `test_policy_gate_completeness.py`; copi `config.yaml`).
**Why:** The eval's clean-slate architecture says only the Co-PI carries the self-improving loop and "Hermes memory stores only preferences and runtime lessons, with write approval on. Canonical knowledge stays in Obsidian/vault schemas" (`tmp/hermes-017-feature-eval.md` §"Built-in memory", Clean-slate §3). Scoping it to one lane and enabling write-approval enforces that boundary.

**What:** New ACP-exposed local-history tool **`session_search` added to the hard-deny set** for every lane (`DENY_DIRECT_TOOLS`, `policy_hook.py`); contract doctor and completeness test updated (`450f659d`, "harden direct history tools").
**Why:** Hermes 0.17 surfaces session/history search tools; leaving them reachable would let an agent read cross-session history directly, bypassing the MCP-only vault access discipline (D40/ADR-46). The regression test asserts it is blocked bare and MCP-prefixed.

**What:** Every profile gained a **`.no-bundled-skills`** marker ("Memoria owns this profile's skill surface; do not seed Hermes bundled skills"), plus `skills: {write_approval: true, guard_agent_created: true}`, `curator: {enabled: false}`, `tool_search: {enabled: auto}`, and `agent.tool_use_enforcement: true` (`be6ebbb0`/`79e6ea43`, all `config.yaml`).
**Why:** The eval found bundled skills "seeded broadly; lane profiles should stay narrower" and recommended opting out; Tool Search should stay `auto` ("forcing it on adds round trips") (`tmp/hermes-017-feature-eval.md` §Skills, §Tool Search, ranked rec #5/#6).

**What:** The `qmd` MCP server was re-pointed from the raw `qmd mcp` binary to a **Memoria `qmd_filter_mcp.py` wrapper** that "hides superseded claim notes by default" (`tool-registry.yaml` `qmd_read` comment; copi `config.yaml`; the underlying filter landed in `bafa92e2`/#851 "filter superseded claims from qmd").
**Why:** Retrieval should not surface retracted/superseded claims as live evidence; wrapping qmd rather than trusting the raw index enforces this at the read boundary without qmd writing the vault.

**What (deferred/killed, notable):** Auxiliary model slots, per-lane `reasoning_effort`, Bitwarden shared secrets, and `gateway.multiplex_profiles` did **not** land — `grep` confirms no `reasoning_effort`/aux/`auxiliary` keys and **no `checkpoints:` block** remains in any shipped profile config.
**Why:** These were G3/G4 items explicitly conditioned on the `#859` baseline ("scope alpha.10 / defer / kill") and on test-vault pilots that "promote nothing without the post-change re-run" (execplan §3 fifth). The measurement-led stance is deliberate: "If stale facts / missed contradictions / retrieval misses / extraction errors are not top issues, the NLI/MaxSAT and warrant-checker work stays deferred" (execplan §3 third; release-plan §5 Out of scope). Bitwarden/multiplexing are also explicitly *not* security boundaries — kanban lane isolation and the policy gate remain the real boundaries (`tmp/hermes-017-recommendations.md`). *(The `checkpoints` removal reason is not stated verbatim in the docs I found — inferred: it is part of "Simplify profile and runtime surfaces" (#904) trimming a runtime surface the baseline didn't justify; marked as inference.)*

**What:** Profile redeploy drift resolved and profile/runtime surfaces simplified (`6f439e77`, `79e6ea43`); `distribution.yaml` version bumped to `0.1.0-alpha.10` on all five profiles.
**Why:** The checkpoint's Runtime Gate requires clean profile redeploy to `~/Memoria-test` with contract/cost doctors green (release-plan §2, validation-log confirms all 42 covered direct/egress tools hard-denied and cost doctor green for copi/librarian/writer).

---

### Gate / provenance / policy engine

**What:** `tool-registry.yaml`'s enforcement note changed from aspirational ("TODO — today writes are gated by path") to **active** ("the policy-gate plugin reads this on `pre_tool_call` and blocks calls outside the profile allowlist. Path writes still narrow through the lane-overrides"), and the `vault_read`/`vault_write` capability groups gained Hermes-0.17 tool names (`obsidian.get_content`, `obsidian.vault_read`, `obsidian.vault_write`) (`tool-registry.yaml` diff).
**Why:** The 0.17 upgrade renamed/added Obsidian MCP tool surfaces; the registry must enumerate them or the positive allowlist would leave the new names ungoverned. This makes the registry the enforced single source rather than a drift-check reference (ADR-27, ADR-28).

**What:** The homepage plugin's **provenance-lock entry removed** — `homepage` deleted from `plugin-provenance-lock.json` and `community-plugins.json`, and its vendored bundle deleted (`16c6844e`, ADR-115 Consequences).
**Why:** Retiring the startup plugin (see UI) means "one fewer vendored dependency and one fewer provenance lock to maintain" (ADR-115 Consequences).

---

### Pipeline / ingest / enrichment

**What:** No new extraction/enrichment machinery; the ingest MCP facade is unchanged, now with an explicit `tools.include: [ingest_pipeline]` filter (copi `config.yaml`).
**Why:** The baseline instrument asks whether extraction errors are a top issue and, if not, "keep API path / defer" — no evidence forced ingest changes this cycle (`tmp/current-state-baseline.md` §Ingest extraction). One creation-track note: ADR-119's `create()` engine is designed to route *both* the human form and the agent writers (`inbox.py`, ingest) through one path, but that unification is a later phase, not landed here (ADR-119 §4, Phasing).

---

### Retrieval / derived store

**What:** Retrieval reads now flow through the superseded-claim-filtering qmd wrapper (see Profiles/runtime), and the `#859` baseline defined an explicit **qmd rerank-on-vs-off** evaluation over ~20 known-target queries as the gate for any retrieval tuning.
**Why:** "If stale/retrieval/contradiction/extraction are not top issues, do not build more memory machinery yet" — the decision line is "keep qmd as-is / tune qmd / defer" and tuning was not selected (`tmp/current-state-baseline.md` §Retrieval; execplan §3 third).

---

### Discovery, UI, navigation, dashboards, panes

**What:** A **left-pane navigation rail** was added — a single pinned plain note `_nav.md` at vault root (`cssclasses: memoria-nav`, no `type`), with a **Now** zone (live Inbox needs-me count as Dataview inline-JS) over a **Places/Go** zone (Library · Knowledge · Project, each with one context badge); the saved **Memoria** workspace pins it as the first left tab at width 280, ahead of the file explorer; `memoria-nav.css` snippet added (`7dd390d9`, ADR-114).
**Why:** Space-switching previously happened only via nav rows on space dashboards opened in the main pane, leaving two gaps: no *ambient awareness* ("is anything waiting on me?" required entering the Inbox, contradicting ADR-70's ambient-health principle) and no *persistent orientation*. Counts use Dataview inline-JS because a Bases formula computes per-row and cannot emit a standalone count (ADR-114 Context/Decision). Bookmarks-core was rejected (can't carry live counts); rendering full dashboards in the rail was rejected as duplicating the main pane — "the left pane navigates and alerts; analytics live in the main pane."

**What:** **Inbox reclassified from a space to the queue** (`type: space`→`type: queue`, `dashboard: queue`), its in-note nav row removed, and its weekly views (Drift watch, Loose ends, Board) moved out; the **homepage front-door plugin retired** in favour of Obsidian native session-restore; `home.md` rewritten from a homepage fallback into a thin **first-run welcome seed** ("Welcome to Memoria… everyday navigation lives in the left-pane rail") pointed at by the Memoria workspace's main leaf (`16c6844e`, ADR-115, supersedes ADR-13).
**Why:** ADR-114 committed to "Inbox is a *state*, not a *place*" but three things still assumed the pre-rail world: Inbox-as-fourth-space, per-space nav rows, and forced-launch into the Inbox. Forcing the full queue as the launch workspace "casts a knowledge/writing tool as inbox-management, and — since empty is the goal — often lands the human on nothing" (ADR-115 Context #3). Session-restore returns the human to real work; the rail carries the ambient signal. Deleting `home.md` entirely was rejected because a new user benefits from a curated welcome and onboarding (ADR-113) needs a landing to attach to (ADR-115 Alternatives).

**What:** ADR-116 established the **View / Collection / Rail** surface vocabulary — a *View* is one Bases query defined once and surfaced by embedding (Dataview only for non-note JSONL sources and inline counts); a *space is a named collection of views*; the durable spaces are three (Library, Knowledge, Project) with **Queue** (daily, converges to empty) and **Maintenance** (weekly structural debt) split by cadence; operational-health stays a pull-only Dataview-over-JSONL collection (ADR-116 Decision).
**Why:** A clean-slate review found three overlaps in the accreted surface: two navigation taxonomies (rail-by-intent vs Portals-by-folder), two dashboard engines defining the same view twice (five drifted Dataview/Bases twins), and one queue mixing two cadences (decide-now beside review-Friday, violating "one decision per dashboard") (ADR-116 Context). The cadence split lets the Queue actually converge to empty (ADR-116 Alternatives).

**What:** **Five duplicate Dataview dashboard pages collapsed to single-definition Bases embeds** (Phase 1) — `contradictions`, `open-questions`, `discuss-queue`, `drift-watch`, `loose-ends` now embed `![[claims.base#Contradictions]]` etc. (`9677e42f`); this also **fixed the drift-watch ordering defect for free** (the Dataview page string-sorted `loudness` alphabetically; the base view sorts by `loudness_rank`: block→alert→notice).
**Why:** Each page re-queried in Dataview what a `.base` view already defined and a space already embedded; the twins had already drifted in columns and sort order — "proof that two definitions of one view is a defect surface, not a feature" (ADR-116 Alternatives; `9677e42f` body). A stale "push to Home" clause was also dropped (ADR-115 retired Home as a surface).

**What:** **`system/dashboards/` reduced from 13 `.md` to 5** (ADR-118 dashboard consolidation, `fd5c9f00`): six pages deleted (contradictions, open-questions, discuss-queue, drift-watch, loose-ends, and `reading-pipeline`), their deep-links repointed at space-section anchors; `project-gate.base`/`project-gate.md` merged into `projects.base` + the Project space; `weekly-review.md` retired with its unique "New this week" 7-day digest folded into the new **Maintenance** space note. The five read-only system dashboards (`board-state`, `audit-log`, `eval-trend`, `fleet-health`, `skill-state`) stay in `system/`.
**Why:** ADR-116's View primitive means a standalone page whose view already lives in a space is redundant. `reading-pipeline.md` also carried a *broken embed* (`![[sources.base#To read & distill]]` referenced a non-existent view; the real one is `Reading pipeline`) that rendered empty — deleting the page removed the bug. The system dashboards are *read-only internals hidden by Portals*, not user work-contexts, so a "System space" was rejected as repeating the Inbox-as-a-space error (ADR-118 Decision, Alternatives). `tests/test_bases.py` was hardened to assert the `#View` name exists — the gap that let the broken embed stay green.

**What:** The **read-only Inspector pane became the system index** (ADR-118 §5, `main.js`): added a **fleet/trust band** reading per-lane trust from `system/metrics/lane-*` notes, and **deep-links each panel to its full dashboard** (board→`board-state`, audit→`audit-log`, verdict→`spaces/maintenance#Drift watch`, fleet→`fleet-health`), carrying only *continuous* signals (episodic `eval-trend`/`skill-state` stay pure pull dashboards).
**Why:** ADR-84's Inspector is the natural always-on read-only window but predated the operational dashboards it should summarize and overlapped the new rail health-band; the fleet band is "the one continuous system-health signal the Inspector currently lacks." It is deliberately reconciled with the rail: "the rail's Now band is the one-glance ambient signal; the Inspector is the read-only detail panel it points to. Ship one signal + one panel — not two competing health surfaces" (ADR-118 §5).

**What:** ADR-116 Phase 3 (**fold Portals into the rail as a stacked Now/Go/Find spine**) was **retired**; the left pane stays two sibling tabs — the rail (Now + Go) and Portals (the object browser) (`5c09aa99`, `d7c5aada`, `328e5146`; ADR-116 Amendment).
**Why:** PR #908 settled the two-tab arrangement; the spine "regresses file-tree height and is only visual — the intent-vs-storage taxonomy overlap survives whether the two are tabs or stacked, so the spine doesn't deliver the consolidation that motivated it." Intent-navigation (rail) and object-browsing (Portals) are accepted as complementary axes (ADR-116 Alternatives, commit body).

---

### Onboarding / tutorials / distribution / sample vault

**What:** A **bundled sample vault** ("mediterranean-diet", ~8 sources / ~15 claims, deliberately half-built) ships in the installer scaffold under `.memoria/samples/mediterranean-diet/` (added to `folders.yaml` skeleton), with `Memoria: load sample vault` / `remove sample vault` QuickAdd commands (`load-sample-vault.js`, `remove-sample-vault.js`) that copy into / clean `catalog/`+`notes/` without overwriting user work (`f96b31ab`, `28540227`, ADR-111 retained by ADR-112).
**Why:** Done for real the knowledge loop takes months, so a one-sitting tutorial can't reproduce the payoff (writing from a *dense* claim graph) without pre-existing state; a seeded half-built corpus the learner *finishes* is the resolution, doubling as an end-to-end test fixture and demo. Crucially the seed is **authored from real sources, never LLM-generated** — "provenance *is* the product; because learners imitate the form they are shown, a faked seed teaches fabrication of the exact thing the system prevents" (ADR-111 Decision/Consequences/Alternatives, backed by the deep-research pass over PKM/sample-DB-pedagogy/onboarding/learning-science). The `sample: bool` frontmatter flag lets Maintenance's "New this week" digest exclude sample docs and the remove command find them.

**What:** The **tutorial arc was rebuilt as one destination-first project arc** — the seven old pipeline-ordered tutorials (`01-set-up-from-zero`…`07-find-new-sources`) were deleted and replaced by six (`01-orient` … `06-close-the-loop` … `07-make-it-your-own`): orient by *reading* the Co-PI's coverage map → capture → distill&connect (faded) → draft (payoff) → verify → close the loop → graduate; **setup was excluded** and delegated to the Quickstart (ADR-112, `00978952`/`b361acad`, supersedes ADR-111's spine).
**Why:** The old spine "is the ontology sequenced — it starts on the wrong object (the fleeting note, the system's cheapest object, not how a researcher enters) and draws a loop as a line." Re-derived from Diátaxis + learning-science: setup "has one right way and teaches no Memoria idea by doing — it is how-to," and embedding it duplicated the Quickstart and the two copies drifted (restart-Obsidian/git-init present in one, absent in the other). Opening with the map "sells Accumulate via the visible gap — something a from-scratch vault cannot do but the seed can" (ADR-112 Context/Decision/Alternatives). Beat 3 must include one rep of distilling the learner's *own* source because transfer requires the fade-to-own-data to happen inside the lesson.

**What:** A new **"Your first month" practice guide** was added (`docs/explanation/knowledge/your-first-month.md`, `cd544392`).
**Why:** The months-long real-time rhythm is a *habit*, not teachable by-doing in a sitting — "cramming the real timeline into a by-doing tutorial is a genre mismatch," so it belongs in a practice guide separate from the tutorials (ADR-111/112).

**What:** ADR-113 (**Co-PI-guided conversational onboarding**) was recorded as `proposed`/deferred.
**Why:** The AI-native end state is the Co-PI walking the first loop in conversation, but "the ADR-112 doc arc is the script the agent layer would dramatize, so it must exist and stabilize first; building the agent layer against a moving doc flow would mean syncing two moving targets." Kept on record with preconditions rather than built (ADR-113).

**What:** Setup/reference docs reorganized — sample-vault reclassified as reference (`docs/reference/sample-vault.md`, `docs/how-to-guides/setup/sample-vault.md`), a new `docs/reference/configuration.md` documenting Memoria configuration surfaces, `set-up-messaging.md` **deleted**, `use-the-vault-homepage.md` → `use-the-vault-launch-screen.md`, `use-the-acp-pane.md` → `use-the-agent-client-pane.md` (`eff1f908`, `3949332a`, ADR-115).
**Why:** Homepage retirement (ADR-115) renamed the launch surface; messaging setup was dropped consistent with the eval keeping messaging/deliverable tools out of core lanes ("Skip; they do not improve core Memoria requirements today").

---

### Distribution / evaluation / release process

**What:** `scripts/verify` now defines the **Source / Package / Runtime / Product / Release gate** vocabulary and a `scripts/verify rc` prefix; the release-candidate runbook and testing plans were updated to it (release-plan §2–3; `c9114349` "promotion-gated verification process").
**Why:** alpha.10 changed profiles, policy shape, navigation, embeds, forms, and sample-vault behavior, so the checkpoint needed a named gate structure where "This file defines the gates; issue state is the source of truth" and Runtime/Product remain attended (CI can prove Source+Package but GUI/live-MCP need a local host) (release-plan §2, Known limitations).

**What:** A **weekly Hermes version-check CI issue** was added (`deb8b69f`, #862).
**Why:** The whole release began from an out-of-date runtime discovered manually; automating a weekly upstream check surfaces the next upgrade before it becomes a blocker (inferred from commit + the 0.14→0.17 drift that opened alpha.10).

**What:** alpha.10 closes as an **internal checkpoint** — `status: complete`, `released: false`, no tag/release-please PR/GitHub Release (release-plan front-matter §10; validation-log Release close-out).
**Why:** The scope is "validation and documentation, not new feature work" — proving the post-alpha.9 repo/vault-tree/test-runtime are coherent — so a formal public release is explicitly out of scope (release-plan §1, §5).

**What:** All alpha.10 release **scratch (`tmp/`) was disposed** — the execplan, both Hermes eval reports (Claude + Codex), the recommendations memo, the upgrade record, the baseline instrument, and the two smoke probes (`probe-qwen-compliance.py`, `spike-nli-vs-cosine.py`) were deleted at closeout (`450f659d`).
**Why:** Per the closeout protocol: selected findings route to ADRs/issues, superseded copies are deleted, and scripts are deleted after their result is recorded (execplan §Finally, release-plan §9). A recurring correction preserved from the eval: the local `provider: custom`/`qwen2.5:7b` render is *test-vault evidence, not the production target* — production Memoria runs Kilo — so production strategy must not be inferred from it (`tmp/hermes-017-recommendations.md` Provider baseline; execplan §3).

---

### Security

**What:** `hermes security audit` was recommended for release/runbook validation (third-party MCP + Python dependency drift), and the reconciled architecture reaffirms the **ADR-22 lane/MCP-only bet**: agents get no direct file/terminal/code-execution/web/messaging tools for vault work; canonical knowledge stays in the vault, not external memory providers; the Nous Tool Gateway stays off (`tmp/hermes-017-feature-eval.md` Clean-slate architecture, "correctly excluded").
**Why:** The 0.17 eval re-tested each new upstream capability against Memoria's requirements and confirmed the exclusions still hold — Bitwarden/multiplexing "reduce service sprawl but are not a policy boundary," so "kanban lane isolation and the Memoria policy plugin stay unchanged" (execplan §3 fifth). The concrete security hardening that *landed* is the `session_search` deny + profile-scoped `memory` + positive `platform_toolsets` (see Gate/Runtime).

---

### ADRs governing this release

| ADR | Status | Decision | Note |
|---|---|---|---|
| **111** | superseded (by 112) | Two-mode (Accumulate/Produce) tutorial spine + seeded half-built corpus | Spine superseded; **seeded sample vault + load/remove commands retained** by ADR-112 |
| **112** | accepted | Onboarding = one destination-first project arc; setup excluded | Supersedes ADR-111's spine |
| **113** | proposed/deferred | Co-PI-guided conversational onboarding | Assumes 112; preconditioned on a stable doc arc + a Co-PI onboarding skill |
| **114** | accepted | Left pane is a navigation rail (Now over Places), never a second dashboard | Per-space object browsing in the rail deferred |
| **115** (inbox-queue) | accepted | Inbox is the queue not a space; retire homepage front door for session-restore + welcome seed | **Supersedes ADR-13** |
| **115** (profile-config) | accepted | Profile capability blocks materialized from `tool-registry.yaml` | **Duplicate ADR number** — two distinct ADRs share id 115 in the repo |
| **116** | accepted | Obsidian surface = View/Collection/Rail + two edges (Home, Co-PI) | Phase 1 shipped; **Phase 3 (spine) retired** |
| **117** | accepted | Document-type naming scheme (kind-scoped singular nouns; no folder/space collision); "note type"→"document type" | `notes/` kept, no path migration |
| **118** | accepted | Dashboard consolidation: fold redundant pages into spaces; keep 5 system dashboards read-only; Inspector = read-only system index | Refines 116/84/70 |
| **119** | accepted | The type schema is the complete declarative contract that validates, generates, and is the single source | Phased; invariants+schema-owned-forms landed, index type dropped |

**Retired / removed this release, and why:**
- **`index` document type + `notes/indexes/` folder** — schema didn't match purpose; register function already covered by `hubs.base#Hubs index` (ADR-119 §6).
- **Homepage community plugin (bundle + config + provenance-lock entry)** — forced landing duplicates the rail's ambient signal and discards working context; native session-restore replaces it (ADR-115, `16c6844e`).
- **Six `system/dashboards/` pages + `project-gate` + `weekly-review`** — redundant with space-embedded views; one broken embed removed with them (ADR-118, `fd5c9f00`).
- **Per-space nav rows on the four space notes** — the rail owns switching (ADR-114/115).
- **ADR-116 Phase 3 (Portals-into-rail spine)** — only visual, regressed file-tree height, didn't fix the taxonomy overlap (ADR-116 Amendment).
- **`set-up-messaging.md` how-to; `checkpoints:` profile block; hand-authored profile capability blocks** — messaging is out of core lanes; profile configs now generated from the registry; checkpoint removal is part of runtime-surface simplification (*inferred*, #904).
- **Deferred (not killed):** auxiliary model slots, per-lane `reasoning_effort`, Bitwarden, gateway multiplexing, NLI/MaxSAT contradiction automation, model-free warrant checking — all gated behind the `#859` baseline / test-vault pilots and not selected for alpha.10 (execplan §3, release-plan §5).

## alpha.11 — The clean-slate reset: one knowledge graph, trusted-writer + checked read-barrier, capability Concepts

**Theme.** alpha.11 is the single largest redesign in Memoria's history — a full re-derivation "from requirements, intellectual lineage, and best practice, *not* from the current implementation" (`_notes/0.1.0-alpha.11-design.md` §Method). It tears out the profile/fleet runtime, the lifecycle+maturity+review-gate write model, the durable-Inbox-card workflow, and the 27-type schema, and replaces them with: a three-bundle OKF workspace (`catalog/` + `knowledge/` + `capabilities/`), a **four-type knowledge model** (`source`→`digest`→`note`+`hub`), a **trusted-writer + staging/promotion + `check_status` read-barrier** integrity spine, **operations as policy Concepts** (with a generated `ai-catalog.json`), **cascade rollback** over a PROV-DM journal, and a **direct-API/Hermes LLM runner split**. What drove it: the prior milestone chain hit a wall where "the only outcome is proceed to the next" (§15), and the two theses — **direction not authorship** and **traceability not approval** (§2) — made the old per-write human gate both wrong and unfalsifiable. The reset is deliberately shipped onto a disposable test Bundle, gated on a seeded-error verdict (§14/§16).

Note on method: alpha.11 landed as one squashed implementation commit (`1b24453b`, PR #1027) preceded by a large docs/rehome runway (PRs #930–#1026). The design doc `_notes/0.1.0-alpha.11-design.md` (identical copy in `scratch/releases/0.1.0-alpha.11/`) is the authoritative statement of intent; ADRs are corroboration.

---

### Vault / concepts / storage

**What:** The shipped vault moved from `src/` to `vault-template/`, and the installable Python package moved to `src/memoria_vault/`, with offline cassettes under `tests/fixtures/` (commit `a966cb54`, "Rehome vault template and Python package"). — **Why:** to stop conflating "the shipped vault source" with "the Python package source" under one `src/` root; the rehome commit body states it moved "the installable package to `src/memoria_vault`, … the shipped vault source to `vault-template`" and updated installers/CI/pre-commit/docs accordingly. Clean separation was a precondition for the clean-slate skeleton to be validated independently.

**What:** Top-level workspace layout changed from six flat categories `[catalog, notes, projects, inbox, spaces, system]` to **three OKF-compatible bundle roots + workspace-level state**: `catalog/`, `knowledge/`, `capabilities/`, plus workspace-owned `journal/`, `.memoria/`, `steering.md`, `index.md`, `references.bib` (`vault-template/.memoria/schemas/folders.yaml` `categories`/`bundle_roots`; old `src/.memoria/schemas/folders.yaml`). — **Why:** §6.1/§6.2 — "A Memoria install is a **workspace** … containing three OKF-compatible bundle roots"; the parent workspace is deliberately **not** an OKF bundle so cross-bundle state (`steering.md`, journal, worker/index) "do not have to pretend to be Concepts." The rejected alternative was keeping flat topic/lifecycle folders (old ADR-04, now retired); OKF was adopted because it "independently specifies the §6 substrate … a fourth re-derivation of the storage layer" (Provenance).

**What:** The catalog was restructured from per-kind folders (`catalog/papers`, `people`, `organizations`, `venues`, `datasets`, `repositories`) to **`catalog/sources/<source_id>/{source.md, content.md, raw/}` + `catalog/entities/<id>.md`** (`folders.yaml` `homes`; `vault-template/catalog/`). — **Why:** §5 "The catalog stays separate — objective, deterministic," and §6.1 "the Concept is the *doc*; some carry referenced **attachments** — a source = `source.md` (the Concept) + `content.md` + `raw/` (attachments, *not* Concepts)." Datasets/repositories collapse into `source.item_type` rather than separate folders ("No 'Work' Concept — version grouping is a `version_of` Link"). person/org/venue merge into one `entities/` home because they are one objective-identity family.

**What:** Retired the `inbox/` category and all inbox-resident durable Concepts; replaced with **generated attention projections** backed by `.memoria/queue/{pending,running,done,failed}`, `.memoria/staging/{catalog,knowledge,capabilities}`, and `.memoria/quarantine/` (new dirs in `folders.yaml` skeleton; old skeleton had `inbox`, `spaces`, `system/board`, `system/worklists`). — **Why:** §8.2 "**Attention is generated, not authored** … markdown, Bases, Canvas, or plugin 'cards' are projections and never canonical Concepts"; §17 "Old Inbox card types do not remain durable Concepts." The alternative (durable Inbox cards as the canonical workflow model) is explicitly shed in §17 because workflow state belongs in "queue (live) + journal (durable) + projections (visibility)," never in card Concepts.

**What:** Introduced a **workspace-level append-only `journal/<machine>.jsonl`** as the durable record, with content-hashed **PROV-DM** events (`derived`/`run`/`model_call`/`check-fired`/`resolved`) — `vault-template/journal/.gitkeep`, schema §7. — **Why:** §6 "Record (authored, not regenerable) … + the **journal** (append-only, content-hashed, per-machine; **W3C PROV-DM**)"; §4.1 makes the journal the tamper-evident derivation graph that substitutes for authorship. "Partition, don't chain" (per-machine journal) is chosen over a chained/DB log to keep multi-device convergence at the git text layer (§6, §4.1).

**What:** Formalized the **record vs projection** split: tracked generated projections are `index.md` / `ai-catalog.json` / `references.bib`; disposable projections (`.memoria/index/qmd`, embeddings, DAG, open-flags, queue) are gitignored (`folders.yaml` skeleton; `vault-template/references.bib`, `catalog/index.md`, `knowledge/index.md`, `capabilities/index.md`). — **Why:** §6 "a small **record**; everything else regenerates." A dedicated projection generator + drift check was mandated ("a hand-edited projection does not satisfy acceptance," §6.1), which is why `regenerate-tracked-projections` (with `required_checks: [projection-drift]`) ships as an operation.

**What:** `references.bib` moved to the workspace root (from `src/.memoria/memoria.bib`), and `catalog.base` moved under `catalog/` (`vault-template/references.bib`, `vault-template/catalog/catalog.base`). — **Why:** §13 "**`references.bib` / CSL-JSON are generated tracked projections** … Memoria does not hand-maintain a bibliography," generated from catalog sources by `regenerate-references-bib`.

---

### Knowledge model — the four-type collapse

**What:** The type vocabulary collapsed from **27 types to 13**. Removed: `alert, candidate, claim, code-note, dataset, eval-task, flag, fleeting, gap, maintenance, paper, pattern, queue, space, thesis, work-prompt, worker-card, worklist-item`. Added: `digest, note, operation, mcp, skill, workflow`. Kept (reshaped): `hub, organization, person, project, source, venue` (`vault-template/.memoria/schemas/types/*.yaml` vs `src/.memoria/schemas/types/*.yaml`). — **Why:** §5/§7 define exactly **three Concept families** (catalog / knowledge-graph / capabilities) and the knowledge graph as **three node-kinds by authoring role**. §Vocabulary note: "`annotation`/`claim`/`fleeting`/`source-digest`/ZK-`index` are not separate types." The many operational types (alert/flag/gap/queue/worker-card/worklist-item) were retired because "Queue, flags, gaps, work cards, dashboards, and indexes are projections or worker state, not durable Concepts" (§7.1 table).

**What:** `paper` + `source` merged into one **`source`** type at `catalog/sources/<source_id>/source.md`. The old `paper` (`citekey`, `doi`, `authors`, `year`, `venue`, `ingest_status{tier0|enriched|complete|needs-human}`) and old `source` (an entity-pointer note with `evidence_level` CEBM grades, `entity` wikilink) became: `source_id` (immutable path), `item_type{article|book|webpage|dataset|repository|software|audio|video|note|report}`, `identifiers{}` map, `csl_json`, `raw_text_sha256`/`normalized_text_sha256`, `metadata_status{verified|partial|unverified|not-indexed}`, `citekey` (demoted to optional alias) (`types/source.yaml`). — **Why:** §6.1 "the catalog path is an **immutable `source_id`**, not the citekey — citekeys are metadata-derived and get corrected, so they are a **generated display/export alias**, never the path (… fixture-verified across a citekey correction)." CEBM `evidence_level` and the entity-pointer indirection were dropped because catalog is now "identity + snapshot + metadata + graph, nothing more" (§13); creators/venue "are **not** standalone fields — they live in `csl_json` + the `authored_by`/`published_in` Links" (§7.1).

**What:** `claim` + `fleeting` + note-`source` merged into one **`note`** type at `knowledge/notes/<id>.md` — an atomic Concept with an *optional* **anchor** (`quote`, `text_sha256`, `source_id`, `annotation_ref`) and an *optional* **claim block** (`claim_text`, `qualifier`, `tense`, `temporal_scope_*`, `status{candidate|accepted|rejected|superseded|needs_review}`, `evidence_set`, `extraction_confidence`) (`types/note.yaml`). The old `claim` type's `maturity{seedling|budding|evergreen}` and mandatory `sources: list` provenance guardrail are gone; the old `fleeting` type's `origin{human|agent|chat}` is gone. — **Why:** §5 "**one note type** … optional anchor = 'annotation', optional assertion = 'claim'." **`no maturity`** because "trust = the checks" (§5) — maturity was a human-set gate proxy, now replaced by `check_status`. A `#todo` tag replaces the `fleeting` type ("A reminder is a `#todo` tag; **no `maturity`**"). `annotation_ref` is a **W3C Web-Annotation selector subset** so spans "resolve regardless of parser" (§7.1). `extraction_confidence` is "internal telemetry — **never surfaced**" (§7.1) — a direct response to Jacobs 2021 (don't show an agent verdict).

**What:** New **`digest`** type (`knowledge/digests/<source_id>.md`) — machine-authored per-source synthesis, 1:1 with a catalog source, carrying `massw{context,key_idea,method,outcome,projected_impact}`, `confidence`, `contested`, `contradictions[]` (`types/digest.yaml`). — **Why:** §5 "`digest` (per-source, **machine**) — 'what this source says,' in corpus context, compiled from the capture conversation; the reading unit, and what hubs draw from." This is the net-new Karpathy "wiki" role — "the bookkeeping humans abandon" (§5), "born `unchecked` + read-barrier'd because they're machine-made over untrusted sources, not because they're disposable" (§6). `massw` fields "feed gap analysis" (§7.1/§9).

**What:** `hub` reshaped from a review-gated (`gated: true`) topic node keyed on a single `topic:` string to a `check_status`-governed **machine-synthesized + human-curated** node with `members[]`, optional `project`, `contested`, `confidence` (`types/hub.yaml`). — **Why:** §5 "the merged Karpathy concept-page × ZK MOC: the machine keeps the topic synthesis current, the human owns the structure + argument." The gated-zone model is retired in favor of ownership+suggestion ("never rewriting the curation"), and "a project's hub *is* its draft outline and the **entry point** (no separate ZK *index* type)" — which is why the old `notes/indexes` folder and any index type are gone.

**What:** `project` reshaped: the old model had separate `project`/`thesis`/`code-note` types under `projects/`; now a single **`project`** type at `knowledge/projects/<id>/project.md` with an *optional* `thesis` field and a `scope` map (`types/project.yaml`; `folders.yaml`). — **Why:** §3 "one project type; the thesis is an optional field that switches on the argument-health gap lens (§9)"; §5 "**project = Link-defined subgraph, not a bundle** (`in_project` membership)." `code-note` and coding/autonomy artifacts are explicitly out of scope (§7.1 table, §15). This is corroborated by ADR-119 (schema-driven document creation) which made `scope_topics` creation-optional and the thesis field conditional on `output_mode` (commits `8e63ff1a`, `87a363e8`).

**What:** Typed Links standardized to the predicate set `{supports|challenges|extends|supersedes|in_project}` + Citations; `version_of` restricted to catalog source↔source only (§7.1 "Typed Links"; old ADR-08 "typed-relations-frontmatter" retired). — **Why:** §5 "**Notes cite sources … not machine-synthesis nodes**, so the machine can recompound freely without breaking citations"; §7.1 "**`version_of` is a *catalog* source↔source Link, not a ZK predicate**." High-risk directional Links (contradiction, supersession) stay human-set ("automatic = candidates").

---

### Gate / provenance / integrity spine

**What:** The write model changed from **per-write human approval into review-gated folders** (old `folders.yaml` `gated_prefixes: [notes/claims/, notes/hubs/]`, enforced by the policy MCP, old ADR-03) to a **trusted-writer + staging → promotion + `check_status` read-barrier**. `gated_prefixes` is removed entirely; every type now carries `check_status: [unchecked, checked, quarantined]` with `initial_check_status: unchecked` (`types/*.yaml`; `folders.yaml` `machine_staging_roots`, `quarantine_root`). — **Why:** §2 Thesis 2 "**traceability, not approval**" — approving every machine write "rubber-stamps under load and checks the wrong object (integrity is **structural**)"; and per-atom approval is "empirically dubious … a confident wrong output drags the reviewer *below* baseline (Jacobs 2021)." §4.4 makes consumption (not just writing) the barrier: machine write-requests land in `.memoria/staging/`, the worker runs on-write checks, and "the trusted writer **promotes** a file into the target bundle only with `check_status: checked`." This retires ADR-03's structural-review-gate as the operative model (though the ADR file survives with `nav_exclude`).

**What:** `lifecycle` (`proposed|provisional|current|retracted|archived`) as the universal state field was removed from knowledge Concepts and replaced by `check_status`; `lifecycle` survives only on `source` (`current|retracted|archived`) as a factual bibliographic state (`types/source.yaml` vs old `types/*.yaml` all carrying `initial_lifecycle`). — **Why:** §4.1 "The authoritative field is frontmatter **`check_status`**. Allowed values: `unchecked` … `checked` … `quarantined`. **Only the trusted worker/check runner transitions this field**." lifecycle-as-workflow-state conflated "is this true/current" with "has this been checked"; the reset separates factual source lifecycle (retraction) from consumption eligibility.

**What:** Codified **two write paths** as operation Concepts: the **agent path** (`capture-source`, `compile-source-digest`, `propose-note-candidates` → staging → promote, `actor: operation`) and the **PI path** (`observe-pi-edits` file-watch backfill + `mark-checked`, `actor: pi`) (`vault-template/capabilities/operations/{observe-pi-edits,mark-checked}.md`; §4.1). — **Why:** §4.1 "There are **two write paths** … editing machine-derived content *keeps* the upstream so cascade rollback still reaches it." `observe-pi-edits` "Backfill journal events for PI edits detected in git status" and `mark-checked` "Record a worker-owned `check_status: checked` transition for an observed PI edit" — the PI is trusted and edits Obsidian directly, but the worker still owns machine-consumer eligibility.

**What:** Added **cascade rollback** as a first-class operation with `rollback` unit = output Concept, quarantining machine descendants and flagging PI-directed ones (`operations/cascade-rollback.md`, `risk_class: high`, `required_checks: [trace-integrity]`, writes `.memoria/quarantine/`). — **Why:** §4.2 "Invalidate the offending **output Concept** … and everything **transitively derived from it** … machine-derived downstream auto-reverts; **human-directed downstream halts auto-revert but still propagates a flag** … **The commit is the atomic *write* unit; the *rollback* unit is the output Concept.**"

**What:** Added the **trace-integrity scan** (`operations/trace-integrity-scan.md`) that quarantines untraced/foreign commits (Obsidian Git, manual git) into `.memoria/quarantine/`. — **Why:** §4.1 "Local git cannot *prevent* another committer … the worker is the **supported** write path, **not an enforceable sole committer**. The enforced boundary is **trace integrity on scan** … a commit lacking a coupled `derived` event is **quarantined and routed through a backfill/import command**." §8.1 explicitly names Obsidian-Git auto-commit as a rejected foreign committer.

**What:** Added the structural detection suite as **integrity-* operation Concepts**: `integrity-claim-quote-check`, `integrity-contradiction-check`, `integrity-evidence-check`, `integrity-link-target-check`, `integrity-prompt-injection-check`, `integrity-quote-anchor-check`, `integrity-provenance-checkpoint`, plus `check-source-metadata` and `check-falsifiability` (`vault-template/capabilities/operations/`). — **Why:** §10 "The integrity mechanism the human gate used to be. Zero-LLM where possible; flag, never silent-mutate; on write and on schedule." §10 splits "bibliographic hygiene" from knowledge integrity via a separate `check_source_metadata`. `integrity-provenance-checkpoint` implements the §12 "provenance-triggered human checkpoint on injection-prone content — derived from a freshly-ingested, uncorroborated external source" — the single most load-bearing residual-risk mitigation ("**flag checked notes or digests that depend on checked sources whose metadata is still partial, unverified, or not indexed**").

**What:** Calibration is now shipped as `calibration.yaml` with `production_enabled: false` and `null` thresholds across `clustering`, `hybrid_scores.candidate_rank`, and pinned model-version slots (`vault-template/.memoria/schemas/calibration.yaml`). — **Why:** §10 "**shadow-first, error-budgeted calibration discipline**: no score affects routing until grounded within an error budget; ungrounded ⇒ report-only; drift ⇒ revert to shadow." The file's own comment: "Null thresholds mean shadow/report-only."

---

### Profiles / runtime — operations replace profiles

**What:** The **five-profile / seven-specialist / fleet** runtime model was retired; policy now binds to **operations, not profile identity**. Operations are Concepts with policy in frontmatter: `operation_id`, `allowed_tools`, `allowed_paths`, `allowed_network`, `runner`, `model`, `prompt_version`, `io_schema`, `risk_class`, `required_checks` (`vault-template/.memoria/schemas/types/operation.yaml`; 40 `capabilities/operations/*.md`). Old ADR-02 "seven-specialist-profiles", ADR-37 "retriever-scout-profile", ADR-42 "profile-compilation" all deleted. — **Why:** §11 "Policy binds to **operations**, not profiles/fleet identity. An operation policy is the runtime boundary"; §17 "A role/profile name is never the enforcement boundary; enforcement comes from the operation's tool, path, network, check, and audit rules … The old five-profile/fleet shape is not carried forward."

**What:** **Separation of duties** encoded per operation — generators (`compile-source-digest`, `propose-note-candidates`, `analyze-claims`, `red-team-argument`) are never their own checkers (`integrity-*`, `check-*`); generators use `runner: direct_api`, checkers use `runner: local` with `integrity_checker`/`evaluator` tools (compare frontmatter across `capabilities/operations/`). — **Why:** §11 "**Separation of duties:** the operation that *generates* is never the one that *checks*." The loop is "**not** generate→approve→repeat: an output is **born `unchecked`**, an independent checker (a different op/model) flips it `checked` *or* raises a flag routed `act`/`ask`/`drop`."

**What:** New **LLM runner split** — every operation declares `runner: direct_api` (default, generators) or `runner: local` (deterministic checks/writers) or (per policy) `hermes` (`operation.yaml` `runner` field; `capture-source` `runner: local`, `compile-source-digest` `runner: direct_api`). — **Why:** §8.2/§13 "the default runner is a direct OpenAI-compatible API call owned by the worker … Hermes is a **library adapter**, not the framework." §11 "**Direct API is the baseline** because it leaves Memoria in charge of request shape, schema validation, replay evidence, and tool-call logging." Commit `2ff5a49d` ("Clarify alpha.11 llm runner split") is the docs runway; the model is corroborated by the retirement of ADR-22/ADR-27 (build-on-Hermes-runtime / Hermes-native-config-and-gate-enforcement was deleted) — Hermes drops from control-plane to specialized adapter. The shipped ai-catalog pins `model: deterministic-fixture` because "**local `qwen2.5:7b` = test fixture only**" (§8 Integrations) — the alpha.9 "qwen is test fixture not runtime" correction carried forward.

**What:** `steering.md` (renamed from `research-focus.md`) is the authored **program** — the `program.md`-equivalent (`vault-template/steering.md`; body text identical except the substrate is now named "steering … the program-wide steering substrate"). — **Why:** §11 "**Direction is authored as the program, not the content.** The human's authored surface is `steering.md` + the project framing + operation policy + the wiki `SCHEMA.md` … the `program.md`-equivalent (Karpathy `autoresearch`)." The rename makes the Karpathy "edit `program.md`, never touch the code" framing literal (§0).

**What:** **Autonomy ceiling** made explicit in policy — no autonomous keep/discard loop for synthesis; code-lane autonomy deferred (old ADR-34 "code-artifact-autopilot" deleted; §11). — **Why:** §11 "An autonomous keep/discard loop is admissible **only** where … a scalar, monotonic metric … reversible … independent, comparable experiments [hold]. They **fail for synthesis** … so the knowledge lane is **human-directed**, and the **integrity spine is the substitute for the missing metric**" (Karpathy `autoresearch`).

---

### Pipeline / ingest / enrichment

**What:** The whole **ingest spine — capture → conversation → digest+hub compounding → notes** — was materialized as operation Concepts: `capture-source` (+ adapters `capture-pdf-source`, `capture-url-source`, `capture-bibtex-source`, `capture-zotero-source`), `record-copi-interview`, `compile-source-digest`, `propose-note-candidates`, `curate-note-candidate`, `curate-note-link`, `extract-claim-stubs` (`vault-template/capabilities/operations/`; §9). — **Why:** §3/§9 "The §3 ingest spine … *is* the mechanism." The **conversation is the hinge**: `record-copi-interview` ("Record a PI interview answer for later digest synthesis") implements §9 "**Conversation (the interview — the hinge)** … it is *not* an optional side chat." `compile-source-digest` implements the **compounding step** ("compile the per-source digest, then compound hub updates … curated hub changes stay as suggestions") — §5's Co-PI differentiator, "**core — the Co-PI differentiator, not deferrable**."

**What:** Capture adapters are a **small fixed set** (`capture-pdf/url/bibtex/zotero-source`), not a translator engine; Zotero import is via the read-only **Zotero Local API** (`capture-zotero-source.md`; §9/§13). — **Why:** §9 "Capture adapters are a small fixed set … **not a translator engine** … lean on the Zotero connector + **Zotero Local API** only for item/source import"; §13 "Zotero annotations are not an alpha.11 import path; Memoria-owned PDF capture stores canonical quote/span/hash selectors itself."

**What:** New QuickAdd surface `capture-note.js` (writes an **unchecked** note under `knowledge/notes/`), plus `open-inbox.js`, `quickadd-utils.js`, `restore-memoria-shell.js`, and a heavily rewritten `resolve-inbox-card.js` (106-line change) (`vault-template/system/scripts/`). — **Why:** the PI-path note-authoring surface must land content as `unchecked` and let "The worker/check loop own promotion" (`capture-note.js` header comment) — enforcing §4.4's read-barrier even for human-authored notes. This is the plugin-boundary rule from ADR-121: the surface enqueues/writes-unchecked, never promotes.

**What:** **Gap analysis** shipped as `analyze-gaps` (source/note topic-mismatch classification, `runner: local`, reads checked Concepts only) plus `analyze-project-argument`, `render-project-argument-canvas`, `surface-tensions`, `compare-and-contrast` (`vault-template/capabilities/operations/`). — **Why:** §9 "**Gap analysis (over *both* graphs and their correspondence)** … read the **mismatch** — the primary signal" (thin/thin, dense/dense, sources-dense/notes-thin, notes-dense/sources-thin). §3 "**Gap analysis is first-class** — the thread that makes Memoria *directed*." `analyze-gaps` reads "checked current Concepts" only — enforcing the read barrier on the gap signal itself.

**What:** All pipeline operations write to `.memoria/staging/knowledge/` (`output_target` in `compile-source-digest`, `propose-note-candidates`) and are `initial_check_status: unchecked`. — **Why:** §4.4 the universal staging path is the enforcement mechanism, "not just a flag."

---

### Retrieval / derived store

**What:** The disposable index is now **qmd**, rebuilt **from checked-only Concepts** via `rebuild-checked-qmd-source` (`.memoria/index/qmd`; `folders.yaml` skeleton; §6). — **Why:** §6 "the **query index** — an *interface* (BM25 + vector + hybrid) … **`qmd` is the backend** (Karpathy names it; disposable-bundle BM25 index/search verified pre-alpha.11), SQLite FTS5+sqlite-vec the zero-dependency baseline/fallback." Crucially the rebuild is **checked-only** ("Refresh the checked-only qmd input tree") — §4.4 "retrieval/qmd projections … must filter to `check_status: checked`."

**What:** Added `answer-query` and `summarize-for-recall` operations implementing the **Ask** contract (`vault-template/capabilities/operations/`; §9). — **Why:** §3 "The one distinct read surface is **Ask**: a retrieval-backed, **cited** query over wiki + notes (with temporal/supersession filters)"; §9 "**The Ask/Query answer contract is sources-plus-unknowns** … a confident answer with no stated edges is a defect." This supersedes the earlier Explore/Ask/Transform triad (§3, §Surface-orchestration ADR cluster).

**What:** Retrieval currency (hide superseded/non-current by default) preserved as a design invariant, exercised by the `stale-as-current` seeded-error case (`vault-template/system/eval/alpha11-seeded-errors.json`; §9/§17). — **Why:** §9 "never present a superseded claim as current"; §17 "retrieval hides superseded/non-current content by default; historical lookup must be explicit."

---

### Discovery / capabilities registry

**What:** New **`capabilities/` OKF bundle** (`operations/`, `skills/`, `mcp/`, `workflows/`) with a generated `ai-catalog.json` projection and `capabilities.base` (`vault-template/capabilities/`). — **Why:** §11 "Capabilities are Concepts; discovery is ai-catalog … Operations, skills, MCP configs, and workflows live in the `capabilities/` bundle as **OKF Concepts** (one per capability, policy in frontmatter). A **generated tracked `ai-catalog.json` projection** indexes them." §13 "**ai-catalog = the capability registry** (OKF is the knowledge registry)."

**What:** `ai-catalog.json` carries a **trust manifest** per entry (`trust: {sha256, source}`) (`vault-template/capabilities/ai-catalog.json`). — **Why:** §12 "**Capability import is supply chain, not just data** … Vet it before the worker runs it via **ai-catalog's trust manifest** … an unsigned/unattested imported capability is **quarantined, not run**." §11 "its **trust manifest is exercised only on third-party import**, and **exposing Memoria's operations as MCP tools externally is deferred**." The full **ARD federated discovery service is rejected** — "it solves a cross-org, web-scale problem the single-user local design doesn't have."

**What:** Projection regeneration operations added: `regenerate-ai-catalog`, `regenerate-references-bib`, `regenerate-indexes`, `regenerate-tracked-projections` (the umbrella, with `required_checks: [projection-drift]`) (`vault-template/capabilities/operations/`). — **Why:** §6.1 "**Generator/check expectation:** alpha.11 must add one worker-owned projection generator and a drift check that regenerates these files into a temp tree and diffs them against the tracked copies; a hand-edited projection does not satisfy acceptance."

---

### UI / navigation / dashboards

**What:** New **space projections** shipped: `spaces/knowledge.md`, `spaces/project.md`, `spaces/inbox.md`, `spaces/library.md` (plus reworked `maintenance.md`), each embedding a `.base` view (`![[knowledge.base#Digests]]` etc.) and a **read-barrier callout** ("`check_status: checked` is the read barrier. Unchecked notes, digests, and hubs stay out of retrieval until the worker/check loop promotes them") (`vault-template/spaces/`, `knowledge/views/knowledge.base`). — **Why:** §8.1 "**Bases** (native) + generated `views/` projections = the project/gap dashboard, the integrity/flags dashboard, and knowledge views." The spaces reflect the new four-type model directly (Digests/Notes/Hubs/Projects sections). The `space`/`queue`/`maintenance` types are retired as durable Concepts — these files are `projection: space` markdown, not Concept records (§8.2).

**What:** ADR-121 "**Obsidian control panel mutates only by enqueueing worker jobs**" added, superseding the read-only Inspector rule (old ADR-84 "read-only-obsidian-inspector" deleted) (`docs/adr/121-enqueue-only-obsidian-control-panel.md`). — **Why:** ADR-121 Context: "The first Inspector design made the Memoria Inspector read-only … alpha.11 changes the storage model: machine writes and promotions must route through the worker/trusted-writer boundary." Decision: "may mutate only by enqueueing worker jobs under `.memoria/queue/pending/`. It never writes Concepts, journal files, generated projections, or `check_status` directly." This matches §8.1's "plugin mutation boundary" (enqueue-only: `enqueue_operation`, `acknowledge_attention`, `resolve_attention`, `open_trace`) — implemented as the `acknowledge-attention` / `resolve-attention` operations. §8.1 also documents four plugin-boundary options (A control-panel plugin [default], B read-only+worker UI, C companion app, D CLI-only) with the **direct-writing rich plugin explicitly rejected**.

**What:** Dashboards consolidated from ~17 to a small set of **5 system dashboards** (`system/dashboards/{audit-log,board-state,eval-trend,fleet-health,skill-state}.md` reworked; 17 `docs/explanation/dashboards/*` deleted) (ADR-118). — **Why:** ADR-118 (dashboard-consolidation, referenced in commits `5b81817b`, `59200775`) and §8.1's move to generated Bases-readable projections rather than hand-authored dashboard pages. Corroborated by commit `59200775` reconciling "'13 support dashboards' to the post-ADR-118 5 system dashboards."

**What:** The homepage front-door was retired (old ADR-13 "homepage-front-door" deleted; `home.md` is now a fresh-vault launch screen); navigation is the left-pane Navigator rail (Now/Places) per ADR-114/ADR-116 (`vault-template/home.md`; `docs/adr/`). — **Why:** commit `59200775` "the homepage front door was retired in #907; home.md is now just a fresh-vault launch screen"; escalations "escalate to the rail's Now, not 'Home'." ADR-115 "inbox-queue-and-retired-homepage" reshaped.

---

### Distribution / evaluation / milestones

**What:** Shipped a **frozen seeded-error gold set** `system/eval/alpha11-seeded-errors.json` with per-class cases (missing-evidence, unchecked-evidence, missing-digest-evidence, missing-contradiction, false-link, conflicting-DOI, ambiguous-entity, poisoned-span, crafted-injection, stale-as-current, unwarranted-claim, provenance-checkpoint, wrong-extraction) and hard bars (`recall_min: 1.0`, `false_positive_rate_max: 0.0`, `rollback_completeness_min: 1.0`, `residual_error_rate_max: 0.0`, `checkpoint_value_rate_min: 1.0`), run by `run-seeded-error-verdict` (`required_checks: [seeded-error-bar]`) (`vault-template/system/eval/`, `capabilities/operations/run-seeded-error-verdict.md`). — **Why:** §14 "The load-bearing question: **does the trace + check + rollback loop hold integrity without per-write approval?** … Inject known errors into a frozen gold Bundle — including the cases structural checks are *blind* to: a **crafted injection** … and a **well-formed-but-unwarranted claim**." §16 Bet B "settled only by the **seeded-error measurement** that gates any non-sandbox use." The `checkpoint_value_rate_min` bar operationalizes §14's "**Calibrate the human checkpoint itself, too**" — a checkpoint that doesn't beat baseline "is theatre."
