- **What:** `work update` routes through the worker and owns metadata/lifecycle changes (archive/restore, retraction/contested standing, classification, identifier corrections), recomputing views/filters/`references.bib` and resolving the linked attention item in the same request (#1075 `1fd4be0c`). `work interview` records the guided conversation and returns stable Work IDs, and `work digest` consumes interview answers (#1051 `dcf06cbc`, #1080 `116fba4f`, #1109 `a720d0c9`). **Why:** `work update` consolidates "archive/restore, retraction/contested standing, human classification, and corrected identifiers … There are no separate archive, restore, or classify commands" and resolves classification review as "one auditable operation" (`design.md` §5, §8). Digest fails if it requires a missing/blocked interview (§8).

---

### Retrieval / Store

- **What:** qmd is now the required CLI-first checked-only search backend. `memoria ask` uses qmd for checked retrieval (#1091 `e51039f5`), `project gaps` is backed by qmd evidence (#1093 `05b1c76d`), and checked Work graph context is indexed (#1072 `4f0fb1dd`). qmd runs with workspace-local `QMD_CONFIG_DIR`/`INDEX_PATH` under `.memoria/index/qmd/` but the **shared user/global qmd model cache** (stopped creating a per-workspace `XDG_CACHE_HOME`/qmd cache path, #1090 `e09c5c28`, #1092 `7ef0d722`); the qmd executable must resolve to an unambiguous absolute path (#1101 `c992e96b`) and the `memoria-checked` collection is verified in `doctor` (#1102 `0ab30f4c`); rebuild fails fast on missing binary/wrong collection/update/embed failure (#1089 `1ffafe11`). **Why:** "Memoria owns the checked-only input tree, read barrier, qmd collection registration, rebuild command, and result filtering; qmd owns keyword and semantic ranking" (`design.md` §10). Workspace-local `XDG_CACHE_HOME` was explicitly rejected because "qmd uses that for model files and per-workspace model downloads make runtime gates slow and brittle" (§10). Absolute-path resolution is required "because other packages can also ship a `qmd` binary" (§10, §11).

- **What:** Generated qmd graph-neighborhood documents now include raw OpenAlex topic rollups and authorship/institution/Source metadata, so retrieval can match on graph context (#1138 `613487d5`, #1154 `cf9f23ef`; `search_index.py`). Project-scoped `project ask` expands qmd queries with checked project scope/facet terms and checked linked-thesis terms, exposing them in `project_context` (#1146 `0c618042`). **Why:** "qmd indexes acquired work text, digests, notes, hubs, compact citations, and graph-neighborhood projection documents" and "Query expansion over citations, topics, facets, and argument terms is baseline; LLM-generated expansion still has to beat qmd+graph retrieval before it counts" (`design.md` §10). `project ask` "adds project steering, thesis, decisions, argument state, and output context" over the same read barrier (§10).

- **What:** Retrieval hides superseded/retracted content by default via a deterministic `standing`/claim-trace filter (enabled by the enforced `standing` frontmatter above). **Why:** "Retrieval hides superseded and retracted content by default; historical lookup is explicit. Supersession is a deterministic filter over the append-only claim trace, not just a dashboard, so the store does not silently surface outdated facts as it grows" (`design.md` §10, §14; TEMPO temporal-coverage lineage in `_papers/REVIEW-REFUTATIONS.md`).

- **What:** `project export` renders checked project compositions to Markdown deterministically (Pandoc formats when installed) via a new `export-project.md` capability (#1064 `955dd56b`). **Why:** "`project export` renders a checked project draft/composition to Markdown by default … It is a deterministic export step, not a Writer agent" (`design.md` §5, §10); the full Writer agent stays a non-goal (§13).

---

### Discovery / Gap Analysis

- **What:** `memoria project gaps <project_path>` became **project-scoped**: it feeds checked project argument/Toulmin health into the shared `analyze-gaps` runtime path, while project-less `operation run analyze-gaps` remains the workspace-wide maintenance scan (#1136 `4b1a4dc9`; `knowledge.py`, `worker.py`, `analyze-gaps.md`). **Why:** "With a thesis, gap analysis also reads argument health from the project's Toulmin graph: a claim that is unsupported, uncountered, or fragile … is a gap even where work/note coverage looks dense" (`design.md` §10); the project half is "the directed/writing half of the loop, not just coverage" (§4).

- **What:** Gap analysis now counts checked SQLite catalog source terms — from `csl_json.memoria.tags`, `topics`, `research_area` — deduped by catalog source ID and ignoring unchecked/archived rows (#1137 `d1af323a`), counts checked topic/keyword graph-edge terms as source evidence (#1138 `613487d5`, #1143 `ef99b11f`, #1149, #1155), and project gap analysis seeds checked project scope/facet terms + counts checked linked-thesis terms with no manual `--seed-term` input (#1148 `95e16dc3`). **Why:** gap analysis "reads both work coverage and knowledge graph coverage … topic/facet coverage" (`design.md` §10 Gap analysis reads); counting SQLite/graph terms replaces the removed legacy-Work-markdown scan and makes coverage measurable from the new authority (ADR-124).

- **What:** Missing-full-text is now flagged by gap scans: catalog rows that cannot produce checked digests/retrieval because full text is missing get PI-reviewable full-text attention flags (#1153 `0cb13abe`). SQLite-detected source/topic gaps carry checked source IDs into discovery candidate generation, so candidate Works are proposed from first-order reference/related graph edges without qmd rediscovery (#1147 `8283d07f`), and Crossref `related`/OpenAlex graph edges feed discovery (#1150). **Why:** "Full-text coverage" and "Discovery candidates not yet captured, enriched, or digested" are explicit gap dimensions (`design.md` §10); "Automated discovery is baseline but bounded … Discovery writes unchecked attention/worklist rows. It never silently imports a discovered Work as checked knowledge and never bypasses the provider allowlist" (§10). Routing graph edges straight to candidates avoids redundant qmd search for edges the graph already knows.

---

### UI / Navigation / Dashboards

- **What:** Retired the shipped dashboards `fleet-health.md` (Fleet nav target + Inspector lane-metric/Fleet trust panel) (#1122 `cc154cdd`) and `skill-state.md` (136 lines, removed with the Obsidian payload #1124). `home.md`, `spaces/{inbox,knowledge,library,maintenance,project}.md`, `audit-log.md`, and `eval-trend.md` dashboards were rewritten to the CLI baseline. **Why:** "`status --json` is the replacement for dashboard glance surfaces … Old board export and metrics aggregation become `status --json`, journal summaries, and generated `knowledge/_views/` reports; no board daemon survives" (`design.md` §5). Fleet/lane metrics presuppose the dropped lane/fleet runtime (§0, §12).

- **What:** Scheduled maintenance has **no internal daemon**: scheduled wrappers route through public CLI commands with a stable `--schedule-id` (queue-drain, file scan, structural check, projection rebuild, retraction/provider refresh, eval), and `workspace scan` reports that schedule id (#1083 `0f04909c`, #1130 `bd105a9f`; dead Hermes cron installer code removed). **Why:** "There is no internal daemon. A scheduler invokes normal CLI commands with `--schedule-id`; the request envelope records the schedule id but has no ingress-type field" (`design.md` §5, §2). Jobs "may be cron, systemd timers, launchd, Task Scheduler, or a human-run script."

- **What:** Docs were mass-rewritten to the standalone CLI baseline — a new `docs/reference/cli.md`, and heavy edits removing Obsidian/Hermes/Zotero/MCP/profile authority language across `hermes-cli.md`, `policy-mcp.md`, `profile-capabilities.md`, `kanban-board.md`, `fleet-metrics.md`, `obsidian-*.md`, `zotero-plugins.md`, `board-export.md`, `installer.md`, `troubleshooting/*`, and `using-obsidian/*` (#1096, #1100, #1125). **Why:** cleanup requirement: "Remove Hermes/profile/Zotero/MCP assumptions from default install, verification, package metadata, and current user docs. Keep old-layout discussion only in scratch/provenance/ADR history" (`design.md` §11); §14 gate: "`rg` checks fail the gate if current runtime or installer paths still require Hermes profiles, Obsidian, Zotero, MCP, or legacy markdown Work paths."

---

### Distribution / Eval / Packaging

- **What:** Install target became `pip install -e .` + `memoria init`/`doctor`; the Linux and Windows installers were made **standalone by default** (#374a702a, #4d761efe), the package verifier builds a dependency wheelhouse into `dist/` before the no-index install (#1127 `701ecbc3`), and profile/Hermes installer modes were removed (#1119). The package gate validates shipped `knowledge/`+`capabilities/` bundle roots and all capability files against the universal frontmatter contract, and ships `knowledge/_views/index.md` as a tracked projection. **Why:** installer requirements (`design.md` §11): create workspace skeleton/SQLite/blobs, seed steering+vocabulary+capability manifests + a package baseline manifest with content hashes, require Node ≥22 and qmd, resolve/persist the absolute qmd path, register the `memoria-checked` collection, and "Install no Obsidian plugin. Install no Hermes profiles. Require no Zotero setup."

- **What:** New `eval-run` capability manifest with worker dispatch (`eval-run.md`, `telemetry/eval/{eval_dispatch,eval_score}.py`); `regenerate-ai-catalog.md` was replaced by `regenerate-capability-index.md` and the generated file renamed to `capabilities/_generated/capability-index.json` (#1066 `f0da1a98`). Directory-only capability manifests are rejected by the loader (#1067 `23cae3b4`); `operation list` validates manifests (#1108 `849dfe1c`). New `update-work.md` capability manifest added. **Why:** "The old `patterns_list`/`patterns_run` compatibility tools are removed … Listing is `memoria operation list`; running is `memoria operation run`" (`design.md` §4). "a folder without the matching `<id>.md` file is invalid. The loader enumerates only capability Markdown files" (§4); §14 gate: "Directory-only capability manifests fail the runtime loader." Every operation declares `method_class` and runner policy or fails loading (§4).

- **What:** An `rg`-based negative gate (`scripts/alpha14_negative_gate.py`) was added and progressively expanded to reject any reappearance of the vacated `.memoria/operations/` home, shipped profiles/lane overrides/tool registry, `.memoria/mcp`, Hermes, Obsidian/QuickAdd, Zotero import/operation surfaces, MCP, lane/`task_id`/`session_id` fallbacks, and legacy markdown Work paths (#1118–#1130). **Why:** the cutover requires that dropped surfaces cannot silently return; the design mandates `rg` checks that "fail the gate if current runtime or installer paths still require Hermes profiles, Obsidian, Zotero, MCP, or legacy markdown Work paths" (`design.md` §14). Treats future dropped-surface hits "as regressions against the negative gate" (`release-plan.md` slice 7).

- **What:** A current-user-facing **parity fixture** exercises the five visible `Memoria:` palette actions, asserts the startup shell-restore macro as adapter-only, compares `operation list` against workspace manifests, and dispatches every manifest id through `operation run` (#1129 `b41b0a1d`); a thin CLI e2e fixture covers the full loop with project-aware Ask context (#1131 `01332309`). **Why:** "Alpha.14 is non-regressing only when every current Obsidian command-palette action and every current Inspector worker action has a CLI/engine equivalent" (`design.md` §5 parity floor); the gate "enumerates final `capabilities/operations/*.md` manifests at test time; every manifest file stem must be runnable through `memoria operation run` or explicitly marked adapter-only/dropped" (§5, §14).

---

### Security

- **What:** Network access hardened to fail-closed (see Gate/Provenance #1103); capability import remains supply-chain-quarantined; retracted/contested Works are blocked from checked promotion (retraction subsystem ported #1117); DB source rollback quarantine markers added and source-metadata/prompt-injection checks moved to DB source rows (#1121). **Why:** security controls (`design.md` §9): "External text is untrusted data. Data/instructions are separated. Raw work text is never system prompt material. Network access is operation-scoped and allowlisted. Generation and checking are separate operation roles. A retracted or contested work is never silently checked. Capability import is supply chain and starts quarantined." Injection-as-untrusted-code is the least-privilege-sandbox bet confirmed by Greshake/AgentDojo (`_papers/REVIEW-REFUTATIONS.md`, §Provenance).

- **What:** Capability supply-chain metadata is kept deliberately small (origin URL, SPDX license, content hashes, signed/unsigned, quarantine state); in-toto/SLSA attestations and RO-Crate/BagIt wrappers stay out. **Why:** "Add in-toto/SLSA only when third-party capability import becomes real" and "Add RO-Crate or BagIt only when there is an actual archive/deposit consumer" — simplest design that meets the stated requirement (`design.md` §13 Deferred-boundary posture; §14 gate).

---

### ADRs

- **What:** New **ADR-124 "Standalone catalog is the citation authority"** (`docs/adr/124-standalone-catalog-citation-authority.md`), `supersedes: [5]`, `assumes: [55]`. Decision: the Memoria SQLite catalog + source-content blobs drive `references.bib`, digest eligibility, retrieval, and metadata checks; Zotero/Better BibTeX become optional tools; citekeys are aliases while stable Work IDs/provider identifiers are the primary runtime keys; full text remains required for a checked digest. **Why (from ADR Context):** "Alpha.14 makes Memoria a standalone CLI/engine. A required Zotero library or live Better BibTeX auto-export would violate that." Alternatives rejected in the ADR: keeping Zotero as required authority ("makes the standalone CLI depend on a desktop reference manager"), a frontmatter-only catalog ("alpha.14 needs durable worker state, provider payload provenance, full-text gates, and generated projections better represented in SQLite"), and live API-on-demand metadata ("repeated provider calls produce drift and cannot be the local source of truth").

- **What:** ADR-05 (Zotero as bibliographic backbone), ADR-06 (citekey naming), ADR-22 (build on Hermes runtime), ADR-121 (enqueue-only Obsidian control panel), and ADR-118 (dashboard consolidation) were updated/annotated as superseded or historical; ADR-30 (deterministic ingest), ADR-10 (claim supersession), ADR-62 (measurement harnesses), ADR-64 (native Windows), ADR-80 (ephemeral test env), ADR-122 (SQLite boundary), and ADR-123 (DOI catalog enrichment gate) were reconciled with the standalone cut; `docs/adr/README.md` index updated. **Why:** slice 1 of the release plan is "Decision authority ADRs (alpha.14 as the cut; supersede Hermes/lane/profile/MCP/`direct_api`/Obsidian/OpenAlex-style graph markdown ADRs). New ADRs start at 124" (`release-plan.md` Implementation Slices §1). The design's cutover rule keeps "old-layout discussion only in scratch/provenance/ADR history, never as a runnable or documented current path" (`design.md` §11). *(ADRs cited as reference/corroboration per ground rules — the design/release docs are the governing authority.)*

---

### Removed / Retired (consolidated) and why

| Retired | Where | Why |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Obsidian `.obsidian/**` tree, QuickAdd scripts/buttons, plugin lock, `system/scripts/*.js` | `vault-template` (#1124) | Obsidian dropped as required surface; product must run on `vim`/file browser (`design.md` §0/§13). |
| Hermes runtime/library, cron installer, post-commit hook, L2 smoke | runtime/installer/scripts (#1119/#1128/#1130) | Hermes "dropped, not deferred" as runtime/runner/adapter/profile/library (§0, §7). |
| Installed profiles, lane/fleet runtime, `policy/lanes.py`, tool registry, profile rendering | `runtime/policy` (#1119/#1126) | Lane/fleet dropped; replaced by actor/workspace policy + `request_id` audit (§0, §12). |
| `.memoria/mcp/` adapter home, `mcp` capability type | `vault-template`, capabilities (#1116/#1120) | MCP dropped as required operation API; renamed to optional `adapter` (§0/§4). |
| Zotero-specific CLI format/operation/helper/capability (`capture-zotero-source.md`, `regenerate-ai-catalog.md`) | CLI/runtime/capabilities (#1123) | Zotero not required Work authority; only generic BibTeX/CSL import (§5/§8, ADR-124). |
| Legacy markdown Work source fallback + `direct_api` runner + schema-migration shim | runtime (#1121/#1056/#1057) | SQLite is sole authority; no compatibility branch with no production vault (§0/§3/§7). |
| `fleet-health.md`, `skill-state.md` dashboards; board export/metrics daemon | `vault-template/system/dashboards` (#1122/#1124) | Replaced by `status --json`, journal summaries, `knowledge/_views/` (§5). |
| Directory-only capability manifests | loader (#1067) | File-per-capability contract; a folder without `<id>.md` is invalid (§4). |
| `patterns_list`/`patterns_run`, `output_target`, `project create`, `pattern_id` | CLI/operations | Superseded by `operation list/run`, `output_intents[]`, scan-authored projects (§4/§5). |

**Net:** the range deletes far more than it adds at the surface level (docs −3962, plus the large `vault-template` payload removal), while the runtime *grows* (~+12,960 lines under `src/`) because 26 operation subsystems were ported in and the CLI spine, enrichment graph imports, and gap/discovery were built. The design's own framing: "This is a full architecture cut … Old mechanisms are either ported behind the new CLI/engine boundary or dropped from the baseline. No competing product paths" (`design.md` §0).

## alpha.15 — The clean-slate cut: standalone engine, four-type model, quarantine-and-verify, "checked ≠ approved"

**Theme:** alpha.15 is the release where Memoria stops pretending to be a Hermes/Obsidian product and becomes what it shipped as: a standalone local CLI + SQLite engine whose files own *meaning* and whose database owns *verdicts*. Two "cut over" PRs (#1164 concept model, #1165 CLI surface) collapse a 12+ type zoo into four Concept types and rename the whole command surface, while six consolidation ADRs (125–130) retire ~70 fine-grained ADRs into subsystem-sized decisions. The driving pressure was twofold: (1) the alpha.14 architecture cut had landed on `main` with *no decision-authority ADR*, so the corpus still described the retired Hermes runtime as current; and (2) an adversarial literature pass refuted the founding epistemic premise — that a human reviewing each machine write improves correctness — which, combined with alpha.14's now-reversible errors, let the team replace the structural write-gate with quarantine-and-verify plus calibrated, thinned human checkpoints. The result is the mature alpha end-state that beta.1 later diverged from.

What drove it (2–3 sentences): the release-plan frames alpha.15 as *"a delta on alpha.14 … pins the clean-slate stack and lands the integrity mechanisms that make the engine defensibly correct."* The ADR-128 Context section records the epistemic reversal from the `_papers/` adversarial pass (Jacobs 2021; AutoResearchClaw; Feng & Liu verification-asymmetry). The scope was deliberately fenced by a *negative* gate: "alpha.15 cannot close with Obsidian plugin implementation counted as release scope" (design index Scope Boundary).

---

### 1. Vault structure & concept model

- **What:** The type roster collapsed from 12+ types across three bundles to **four knowledge Concept types** — `note`, `work`, `hub`, `project`. Nine type schemas were deleted outright: `source.yaml`, `person.yaml`, `organization.yaml`, `venue.yaml`, `digest.yaml`, `adapter.yaml`, `operation.yaml`, `skill.yaml`, `workflow.yaml` (all `REMOVED` at 5b1ea8bc; `git show 88b7f0f5:…/types/` confirms they existed prior). A new `work.yaml` was added. (PR #1164, commit `71ec0dc4`; `vault-template/.memoria/schemas/types/`.) — **Why:** the roster "grew by accretion … each with folder homes, lifecycle fields, and per-type rules. The multiplicity itself caused drift and confusion" (ADR-126 Context). The discriminator is now "a fundamentally different artifact"; a flippable check regime is a *mode*, and a thing on a different layer (a source record) is not a knowledge type. Rejected alternative: keeping claim/question/thesis as types — "flippable states and roles, not artifacts; separate types make the question→claim transition destructive" (ADR-126 Alternatives).

- **What:** `note` gained `mode: claim | question` (declared intent), `question_status: open | resolved`, and claim-context fields `temporal_scope`/`tense`/`qualifier` + `anchors`; it lost `check_status`, `note_status`, `standing`, `resource`, `quote`, `text_sha256`, `source_id`, `annotation_ref`, `extraction_confidence` (note.yaml diff). — **Why:** a mode is "declared intent creating obligations the gap engine feeds on — a claim without evidence is an `under-warranted` gap; an open question is a compose-flow lead" and "field-derived typing could not tell a plain thought from a claim missing its evidence" (ADR-126). The excerpt/quote fields relocate to a W3C `TextQuoteSelector` `anchor`, not a type (ADR-126 "Relocations").

- **What:** `hub` now **owns exactly one ID-backed controlled-vocabulary tag** via a required `tag:` field; it dropped `members: list`, `confidence`, `contested`, `project` (hub.yaml diff). Membership = "everywhere that checked tag appears"; only checked tags confer membership. — **Why:** hand-curated hub membership "rots (every relevant new note requires a hub edit)"; the owned checked tag is maintained at write time (ADR-126 Alternatives). This splits *membership* (mechanical, inclusive) from *salience* (human, curated in prose), directly answering ADR-19's recorded hazard "a generated list that looks curated but isn't" (ADR-126, disposition map).

- **What:** `project` gained `outcome_frame: map` and `paper_plan: map`, kept `thesis: str`, and dropped `scope: map` (project.yaml diff). Project is defined as "the compose-flow working frame: a nested, detachable sub-bundle with one-way project→corpus references … deliverable targets (`outline`/`section`/`figure`/`code` — **artifacts, not Concepts**)." — **Why:** absorbs ADR-77 (project gate), ADR-79 (argument graph/warrant/saturation floor → the gap engine's saturation block), and ADR-78 (thesis is now a *role* link, not a type; "no note is born thesis-designated-and-checked; a falsified thesis is a preserved result via the refuting subgraph") (ADR-126).

- **What:** `work` is a **new** type: "a source's subjective digest + tags, 1:1 with the catalog work (`work_id`)"; the objective record stays in SQLite. `digest` materialization moved onto `work` (work.yaml has `work_id` required, `citations`/`evidence_set` optional; `digest.yaml` deleted). — **Why:** the split-authority rule — files own meaning, the DB owns records/verdicts (ADR-124/125). The old `digest` type conflated the human-authored subjective take with the machine-owned bibliographic record.

- **What:** `folders.yaml` rewritten: `categories`/`bundle_roots` cut from `[catalog, knowledge, capabilities]` to `[knowledge]`; the `catalog/*` and `capabilities/*` folder-homes and staging roots removed; `knowledge/works` added, `knowledge/digests` removed (folders.yaml diff). — **Why:** catalog sources/entities are now SQLite records (not markdown Concepts), and operations became product code shipped in the package, so there is no workspace `capabilities/` tree (ADR-125: "Operations are product code"; ADR-126 relocations).

- **What:** **Meaning-only frontmatter** enforced: the universal contract is ULID `id`, `type`, `title`, `tags`, typed `links`, `aliases`, optional `archived`, plus per-type fields; `check_status`, `standing`, `note_status`, and every derived/verdict field were removed from *all* type schemas and the templates (`note.md`, `hub.md`, `project.md` diffs; `initial_check_status` key deleted everywhere). (PR #1164 + PR #1179 terminology sweep.) — **Why:** "`check_status` lived in frontmatter, so checking a note rewrote it, hand-edits forged status, and every consumer had to distrust the file it was reading" (ADR-126 Context). Rejected alternative: keeping `check_status` as a generated-but-ignored projection — "hash churn plus a forged-status foot-gun; meaning-only is stronger" (ADR-126). Note this *retires* the enforcement PR #1157 landed the same day (`id`/`standing`/`check_status` across 74 files) — the retirement negative gate had to cover #1157's just-added surface (exec-plan §Relationship to alpha.14).

- **What:** ULID identity introduced as a schema kind (`id: ulid`); `schema.py` added `ulid` and `links` field kinds and `is_ulid` validation (schema.py diff). — **Why:** "identity ≠ filename ≠ title" (ADR-126 meaning-only section) — decoupling identity from the path so renames/moves don't break references.

- **What:** Frontmatter validation flipped from **permissive to closed**: `validate_frontmatter` now rejects undeclared fields ("undeclared field: … (put custom data under x)"); every type schema gained an `x: map` extension escape hatch (schema.py diff: "Unknown extra fields are rejected"). (PR-AC #1197.) — **Why:** closes the field-closure part of ADR-119 (schema-as-single-declarative-contract), now enforced in product code rather than as a gated content edit.

- **What:** `links:` became a **nested, relation-typed map** validated against a fixed relation set `{supports, contradicts, extends}`, rejecting scalar values, absolute/URL/mail targets, and traversal-like (`..`) targets (schema.py `_check_links`, `LINK_RELATIONS`). (PR-AE #1199.) — **Why:** ADR-52's distinction carried verbatim — authored `links:` are the human/argument layer; given `relationships` are engine-built DB records (ADR-126). Guarding target shapes prevents a link from escaping the workspace or smuggling active content.

### 2. Profiles / runtime / stack

- **What:** The Hermes agent runtime, installed profiles, board lanes/fleet, and the MCP policy plugin were **dropped from the product, not deferred**; the stack is pinned to Python 3.12+, `uv tool install memoria` (with `pip install -e .` contributor fallback), Typer CLI, stdlib `sqlite3` (WAL + FK, **no ORM**), `.sql` DDL gated by `PRAGMA user_version`, pydantic-ai as the sole typed LLM runner (ADR-125 Decision; PR-A #1160/#1161/#1162; enforced Python 3.12 in PR #1216/#1217). — **Why:** alpha.14 cut Hermes out but "its decision-authority ADR was never written, so the corpus still presents the Hermes-era architecture as current" (ADR-125 Context). Rejected: staying on any agent framework — "the framework owned state, workflow, and the write boundary; every integrity mechanism had to be threaded through it"; ADR-22's "never build your own runtime" warning is "acknowledged and accepted as a cost, bounded by ADR-127's explicit contracts" (ADR-125 Alternatives). ORM + migration framework rejected: "the integrity schema is the product; single-user scale needs `.sql` + `user_version` only."

- **What:** SQLite schema formalized as a loaded `.sql` DDL file (`runtime/schema_v1.sql`, `PRAGMA user_version = 3` by release end) with tables for `operation_requests`, `journal_events`, `concepts`, `concept_verdicts`, `concept_flags`, `outputs`, `materialization_payloads`, `catalog_sources`, `external_ids`, `enrichment_runs`, `provider_payloads`, `field_provenance`, `work_graph_edges`, `work_aspects`, `derivations` (`git show 5b1ea8bc:…/schema_v1.sql`). At `88b7f0f5` the schema was inline `CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS` Python with only `PRAGMA foreign_keys = ON` — no WAL, no `user_version` (exec-plan Verified baseline facts). (PR-A #1160; `be2ea1b9` "load sqlite schema from ddl".) — **Why:** SQLite is "the authority for records, operations, queue, journal, and verdicts," explicitly overturning ADR-49's rejected "SQLite: never the source of truth" (ADR-125 State).

- **What:** Console script routed through a Typer entrypoint (`typer_cli.py` added, `afa83639` "route console script through typer"); the argparse CLI with `note propose/accept/reject`, `work capture` was retired. — **Why:** verb-first canonical surface (ADR-125/design §5); the argparse surface with propose/accept was a live retirement target (exec-plan baseline facts).

- **What:** **Runner policy** — `providers.yaml` gained `runner_providers:` with two OpenAI-compatible connections (`local` → `127.0.0.1:11434/v1`, `gateway` → OpenAI with `KILOCODE_API_KEY`); operation manifests must pin per-operation `runner.test`/`runner.live`, selected by `--mode test|live`; resolved model + actual token cost journaled per run; the legacy root `providers.local/gateway` fallback was removed (PR-H #1175; providers.yaml diff; PR #1218 `c3fd37a3`). — **Why:** "no threshold in the prior corpus was ever validated"; the manifest is the hard ceiling and non-sandbox use is licensed only by the **live** model's seeded-error verdict per `(operation, model, mode)` (ADR-129 Runner policy). Removing the fallback forces explicit config so a silent default can't run unlicensed.

- **What:** `eval select-models --operation --mode` added as a build-time seeded-error-bar selector that "pins the cheapest candidate that passes the operation's bar — human-triggered and inspectable, never an online optimizer" (PR-Q #1185; `88ec2ddb`). — **Why:** an explicit **amendment to ADR-11**: whole-system vault-eval stays diagnostic and never gates work, but "`eval select-models` gating a build-time model choice is a different act and is permitted" (ADR-129 Amendment).

- **What:** Agent posture carried without the profile system — "Memoria never grants an agent file, terminal, code-execution, or send tools"; substantive coding stays delegated to external agents as the alpha.16 module target (ADR-125). — **Why:** the surviving invariant of ADR-07/32/46/48; ADR-35/43 (skill insights/governance) marked dead.

### 3. Gate / provenance / epistemics

- **What:** The founding epistemic was **reversed**: "Correctness is not conferred at write time by any approver, human or machine … A human-authored note and an LLM digest are epistemically equal." The structural per-write human gate (ADR-03) was superseded; `checked` now means only "checks passed and warrants resolve — never approved," enforced by `checked_terminology_gate.py` blocking approved/verified/trusted drift (ADR-128; PR-L #1179 `2ad8e886`). — **Why:** the adversarial literature pass refuted the premise that human-reviewing-each-write improves correctness: Jacobs 2021 (N=220) found clinician+ML accuracy 0.356 ≈ clinician-alone 0.357, both far below ML-alone 0.667, and an incorrect recommendation dragged the human *below* their own baseline (0.299, p=0.0018); AutoResearchClaw's HITL ablation showed targeted 3–6 checkpoints dominate per-step approval; Feng & Liu's verification asymmetry means the gate degrades to a cursory nod under load (ADR-128 Context, inlined because `_papers/` is gitignored). Rejected: keeping the structural gate — "it charged the scarcest resource (PI attention) for correctness it measurably did not buy"; LLM-reviewer-as-gate — "a probabilistic verdict is never a structural control" (ADR-128 Alternatives).

- **What:** The human checkpoint is now **calibrated or thinned**: humans are routed to act/ask/log only where checkpointed items are "measurably more correct than the same items un-checkpointed"; a checkpoint that can't beat its no-checkpoint baseline "is theatre and is thinned" (ADR-128). — **Why:** deliberately re-admits the consequence/uncertainty routing ADR-21 foreclosed, "with the theatre-check as the new guard in place of the blanket rule." The precondition that justified gating creation (irreversibility) "no longer holds" because ADR-127's quarantine/rollback restored reversibility.

- **What:** **Disposition telemetry** made first-class and non-backfillable: every `attention resolve` journals the routing class (act/ask/log) and outcome (apply/reject/defer) with decision time, from first ingest; apply-rate bounds (>0.9 or <0.2) are the rubber-stamp detector (ADR-128; PR-B3 #1165 §S5.6). — **Why:** "This is what makes 'calibrated' falsifiable" — without recorded dispositions the theatre-check cannot be evaluated. The borrow-doc's "state-based dogfood evaluation" (Tau-bench, EpiBench) and "personal-informatics lifecycle → dogfood metrics" pressures.

- **What:** The review queue as an **approval surface was removed**; replaced by a consequence-routed attention worklist keeping the honesty-card obligations (arguments not verdicts; batch worklists; graded loudness quiet/notice/alert/block) (ADR-128 Consequences; ADR-130). — **Why:** ADR-51's honesty card and ADR-121's enqueue-only rule carried verbatim; the inbox-as-Obsidian-category mechanism is dead.

- **What:** From ADR-57, "the writer half survives; the disposal half does not": any rule-derivable write is engine code, never an LLM ("engines write"); "agents judge, PI approves" replaced by "checks route, propagation protects, calibrated humans decide where they measurably help" (ADR-128). — **Why:** pinned models "bound drift, they do not buy reproducibility," so deterministic engines must own rule-derivable writes.

### 4. Integrity, quarantine & recovery

- **What:** **Universal quarantine-and-verify invariant**: every mutation to tracked content, regardless of origin, is non-consumable until a verification pass dispositions it act/ask/log; one shared check suite, two ingresses (operation lifecycle for engine writes, `workspace scan` for foreign edits); detection covers **all tracked paths** including `references.bib` and `.memoria/overrides.jsonl` (ADR-127; PR-C3 #1168 moved the projection change detector into `runtime.projections`). — **Why:** alpha.14's engine "leaves the guarantees implicit"; ADR-128's epistemics are only safe if "errors become detectable, attributable, and reversible instead of gated at creation" (ADR-127 Context/preamble).

- **What:** **Consumption guard (refuse + enqueue)**: at machine consumption the on-disk hash must equal the recorded `checked` hash; mismatch refuses to serve and enqueues scan — no write on the read path; scan demotes under the lock (`runtime/read_barrier.py` added; PR-C1 #1166 enqueues `observe-pi-edits` with `schedule_id=read-guard`). — **Why:** synchronous demote-on-read rejected — "a write on the read path races the workspace lock; refusal alone is already fail-closed" (ADR-127 Alternatives).

- **What:** **Two-tier demotion propagation**: depth-1 machine consumers flip to `unchecked`; PI-authored descendants raise an ask-routed flag and stay live (never auto-destroy human work); depth-≥2 machine descendants get a DB `stale` flag (a derived signal, excluded from correctness-bearing consumers but still served to `ask` with mandatory stale framing); retraction-driven demotions propagate one level deeper before going stale (ADR-127; PR-C2 #1167). — **Why:** the build-system stale-vs-invalid lesson, "so one demoted foundational node cannot cascade a whole subgraph into an attention flood"; hard exclusion rejected because "hard exclusion breaks cross-period queries."

- **What:** **Cross-store recoverability (observable atomicity)**: 2PC with journal states `pending`→`materialized` (materializing commit SHA recorded after `git commit`), write-ahead fsync ordering (payload fsynced before the DB commit that references it), one workspace-scoped write lock per operation, crash-at-any-boundary recovery via `workspace recover`; connections pinned WAL + `synchronous=FULL` (ADR-127; PR-D1 #1169, PR-D2 #1170; `worker.py` +306 lines). PR-D3 kept the deployed `pending` name rather than adding a separate `prepared` enum (exec-plan PR-D3). — **Why:** ADR-22 warned against owning durable state/retries/crash-recovery; ADR-125 accepts the cost and "ADR-127 is where that obligation is paid" (ADR-125 Consequences).

- **What:** **Git/journal division**: git owns file-tree history + the tamper-evidence root via the tracked `.memoria/journal-head` anchor (newly *created* — at `88b7f0f5` `journal_head()` was a DB query only, no tracked file); the SQLite journal stores git refs (never file bytes) and is row-hash-chained; one commit per operation staging **only** materialized paths + control files, **never `git add -A`** (a swept foreign edit would bypass quarantine) (ADR-127; PR-E1 #1171). — **Why:** narrows ADR-104's rejection of hash-chaining (which targeted an in-vault log file) — "DB rows plus a git anchor get row-level tamper evidence without that cost." Git-as-sole-history rejected: "verdicts and the records graph are relational, high-cardinality, and deliberately not file-recoverable."

- **What:** **Storage recovery classes**: files own authored meaning (file-recoverable); provider-derived records replay from content-addressed blobs; verdicts/journal are DB-only accepted-loss; **DB loss fails closed to `unchecked`** (rebuild ignores any forged frontmatter status); human `work update` dispositions live in the git-tracked append-only `.memoria/overrides.jsonl`, **tiered on DB-loss replay — restrictions reapply, permissions re-earn** (ADR-127; PR-B #1163, PR-D2). — **Why:** "the journal witness is gone, so the log cannot be trusted to *unblock* anything"; "No human-authored datum is ever in the accepted-loss class." A three-store backup contract (git remote, SQLite streaming replication à la Litestream, blob file-sync) is documented and `doctor`-reported, "never a runtime dependency."

- **What:** `golden_restore.py` **removed** (155 lines deleted; `b12ac8a1` "Remove golden restore product path", PR #1206); operation/capability policy relocated out of the workspace `capabilities/` tree into packaged product data, `memoria init` no longer seeds `capabilities/`, capability-index output is a local `.memoria/index/` cache (PR-E2 #1172, `7d071d8f`; `capabilities/` tree and `capability-index.json` 1421-line file deleted). — **Why:** package reinstall is the restore path for product files (supersedes ADR-26/55/74 repo-as-install-unit + golden-copy); behavior changes are now PR-reviewed code, "a stronger review than a gated content edit" (ADR-125).

### 5. Pipeline / ingest / enrichment

- **What:** **Enrichment merge by static field authority**: per-field best-source-wins with provenance; references are the DOI-deduped **union** across providers; author sub-fields never paired by index across sources; `provider_coverage = full|partial|degraded`; high-authority conflict marks `degraded` and raises attention (never silent overwrite); `update-work` cannot mark degraded coverage checked (ADR-129; PR-F #1173, `ingest_paper.py` +114; new `field_provenance`/`enrichment_runs`/`provider_payloads` tables). — **Why:** supersedes ADR-30's tiered-ingest merge; "no single provider is complete"; "provider output is claims, not ground truth" (ADR-129). ADR-30's spike lessons (capture-commits-first, scriptable-before-LLM) are binding.

- **What:** Two operational drift policies bound: **work-ID merges raise attention and never auto-merge** works/digests (historical provider IDs kept as aliases; per-field drift journaled); anchors are **re-anchored, never silently rebound or dropped** across extractor upgrades (exact-then-fuzzy; failures → orphaned-anchor attention) (ADR-129). — **Why:** "providers drift, extractors upgrade" — "the Hypothes.is lesson" (borrow-doc "untrusted data sealing"/provenance pressures).

- **What:** Semantic Scholar is **conditional, default-on when keyed** (reference union, citation intents as free Tier-0 contradiction candidates, TLDRs, SPECTER embeddings; never promotion-required); scite.ai is optional opt-in (ADR-129). — **Why:** "Like every provider and judge: proposers, never authorities."

- **What:** **Untrusted-input sealing**: operation manifests declare untrusted fields; the runner serializes them into sealed data blocks — "raw source text never interpolates into an instruction template (a manifest violating this fails to load)"; every text-reading operation carries a negative poisoned-input fixture (ADR-129 Runner policy; `classify.py`, `extract.py`, `runner.py` diffs). — **Why:** borrow-doc "untrusted data sealing" pressure (Greshake, AgentDojo, InjecAgent) — sealing "narrows the channel without making the model unsteerable."

- **What:** **Deterministic edge extraction (raw)**: on materialization, explicit-typed body links extract to **unchecked candidate edges** with zero LLM calls; bare wikilinks yield at most weak `mentions`/`related`; argument-class edges (`supports`/`contradicts`/`extends`) are **never** auto-promoted; act-promotable allowlist is `{mentions, related, cites, version-of}`, tuning deferred (ADR-129; PR-J #1177, `link.py` diff; writes `edge-candidate` Inbox prompts). — **Why:** auto-typing bare wikilinks rejected — "corrupts the argument graph; a bare link means 'see also'" (ADR-129 Alternatives).

- **What:** **Work-aspect read model**: schema v3 `work_aspects` table populated from CSL aspects + Markdown full-text sections (context/key_idea/method/outcome/limitation/assumption); included in checked Work search documents (PR-AB #1196, `5b426316`). — **Why:** ADR-99 (MASSW aspects) accepted "via the DB `work_aspects` read model … Keep files simple" (disposition map; borrow-doc "structured work aspects," MASSW/Knows) — adapted as DB sidecars, *not* author-facing YAML.

### 6. Retrieval / derived store

- **What:** Retrieval stays on **qmd for alpha.15** after a baseline-gated spike; the committed verdict lives in `tests/fixtures/retrieval-substrate-spike.json` and `runtime/retrieval_substrate.py` (new); SQLite FTS5 covers lexical cases but "the packaged product does not yet carry sqlite-vec plus a local embedding pipeline, so the semantic/hybrid replacement bar did not clear" (ADR-125; PR-A #1162, `d502ac20`). — **Why:** the honest premise that no threshold was ever validated — the replacement had to *beat a declared baseline* on a committed fixture, and it didn't (ADR-129 "each tier must beat a declared cheap baseline or it is disabled").

- **What:** Checked-only retrieval enforced through the read barrier: `include_stale` parameter on `checked_search_documents`; stale content served to `ask` only with mandatory stale framing, excluded from promotion inputs/export-readiness/gap scoring (ADR-127; `search_index.py` +89, `retrieval_substrate.py`). — **Why:** "hard exclusion breaks cross-period queries" — stale is a derived signal, not a verdict change.

- **What:** Generated `index.md` bundle projections described as "OKF-style" (`projections.py`, `BUNDLE_ROOTS = ("catalog", "knowledge")`). ADR-107 (OKF interchange bundle) stays **proposed/deferred**, but ADR-126 records a *new* decision: "the project layer's internal OKF sub-bundle is a new decision … deliberately beyond 107's boundary-only stance" (disposition map). — **Why:** OKF's convergence with Memoria's shape "is validation of ADR-126/125," but "OKF's defining trait is the inverse of Memoria's thesis" (mandatory permissive consumption vs. quarantine), so full OKF import/export stays deferred (ADR-107 Context).

### 7. Discovery, gaps & machine judgment

- **What:** **Native gap analysis**: checked-only inputs, canonical gap kinds (`full-text-missing`, `citation-neighborhood`, mapped `argument-*`), fixed `{0,1,2}` ordinal severity (`score 0..8`, bands ≥4/≥2/else), `--json` findings with `why`/`next_actions`/`candidate_work_ids`, project `saturation` block, discovery candidates as unchecked attention rows (never promoted Works) (ADR-129; PR-G #1174, `3fa82bc6`). Saturation = a claim with ≥1 addressed support AND ≥1 counterpoint. Advisory, never gating. — **Why:** absorbs ADR-79's saturation floor; "gap analysis reads checked inputs only" so unverified content can't drive the compose-flow phase signal.

- **What:** **Discovery relevance scoring** (ADR-92 accepted): `analyze-gaps` annotates provider-discovered candidates with deterministic `steering.md` relevance, sorts ranked ahead of a separate exploration channel; "model embedding similarity remains out until candidate abstracts/full text are reliably present" (PR-AA #1195, `79b2e6a6`). — **Why:** the cheap deterministic path clears the bar; ML deferred until data exists.

- **What:** **Tag candidates from gaps** (ADR-93 accepted): `analyze-gaps` runs a deterministic stdlib phrase pass over checked Work text, suppresses existing vocabulary/frontmatter terms, emits unchecked `inbox/` tag-candidate cards, never writes tags — "KeyBERT or YAKE stays unnecessary until real corpus misses prove it" (PR-W #1191, `1977cd14`). — **Why:** simplest-design-that-meets-the-requirement; avoids adding ML deps speculatively.

- **What:** **Record-linkage attention** (ADR-94 accepted across #1190/#1192/#1193/#1194): `check-source-metadata` flags checked sources sharing exact external IDs, title/year/first-author blocks, duplicate person ORCID/OpenAlex IDs, and normalized entity name blocks as `record-linkage` findings with stable `inbox/` prompts — **never merges records** (`detectors.py` +66). "fuzzy thresholds stay out until real corpus misses justify them." — **Why:** deterministic ID + string-blocking clears the bar; automatic merges are irreversible and unvalidated (ADR-94 disposition).

- **What:** **Contradiction Tier-1 (NLI proposer)** (PR-I #1176): `surface-tensions` runs a pinned local NLI comparator, tri-class SUPPORTED/REFUTED/NOTENOUGHINFO with first-class abstain and an FP budget, canonical-id dedup; it may gate candidates **only after passing a HANS-style overlap-but-opposite acceptance set**; failing HANS is a **loud degraded mode** (cosine/BM25 → ask, attention raised) — never a silent no-op; no automatic `contradicts` writes (ADR-129; `retraction.py`, `eval_score.py` diffs). — **Why:** "NLI shares cosine's lexical-overlap blind spot"; "NLI silence is never presented as 'no contradiction.'"

- **What:** **Tier-2 tension judge** (PR-AF #1200, `0a1c1b09`): an LLM judge admissible **only** on Tier-1 abstain/HANS-degraded hard cases, retrieval-grounded, abstain-first, temperature 0, requires quote grounding from both consumable checked files, refuses dirty DB-checked files through the read barrier, never writes checked `contradicts` links — "a proposer, never an authority; its verdict never promotes or demotes anything by itself." — **Why:** LLM-judge-as-authority rejected (GBrain's failure; "~28% wrong belief-flips in ConCoRD-class systems") (ADR-129 Alternatives).

- **What:** **Shadow-first calibration generalized** (ADR-66 → the rule for every score): a new score reports/journals but changes no routing/promotion/visibility "until its thresholds are grounded on recorded PI dispositions with a named fixture and pinned model"; `calibration.yaml` **deleted** (`git show 88b7f0f5:…/calibration.yaml`) (ADR-129). — **Why:** "Every tunable number ships behind `production_enabled: false` semantics; the first grounded thresholds arrive with beta-era disposition data." The static calibration.yaml (entity_resolution/classify/clustering/hybrid_scores floors) was retired because none of its constants were ever validated and the clustering-config surface itself was removed (PR #1204 "remove stale clustering config surface").

### 8. Surfaces / UI / navigation / distribution

- **What:** The engine's **JSON read-API is the sole read path** for every Memoria-built surface and agent; alpha.15 implements CLI (`--json`, transport 0), scoped **FastMCP** stdio server, and **loopback HTTP** server as "pure marshalling skins" over one `engine/api` module; "a wrapper holding logic is a gate failure" (ADR-130; PR-K #1178 `engine/api`, PR-R #1186 HTTP, PR-T #1188 MCP behind `.[mcp]` extra, PR-U #1189 view-specs). — **Why:** "Under ADR-125 the engine is the product and every surface is a client"; MCP-as-product-surface rejected — "MCP is one transport over `engine/api`; the CLI remains the no-daemon recovery surface" (ADR-130 Alternatives).

- **What:** **Per-agent read scoping** enforced (`read_scope` filtering in `engine/api` before transports see payloads; out-of-scope reads return the not-found shape; MCP requires a non-root scope; HTTP parity added) (PR-S #1187, PR-AD #1198, `52ab9ad7` "enforce http read scope"). The first-rung all-vault CLI agent is "trusted-local dogfood only, never a supported safe surface." — **Why:** the lethal-trifecta / exfiltration mitigation; threat model stated: "read scoping is a policy boundary for tool-limited/cooperating agents; a local agent with its own file tools is in the trusted-local class regardless of transport" (ADR-130). Direct-vault-access for agents (obsidian-local-rest-api-class) rejected — "bypasses read scoping and verdict tagging."

- **What:** **All writes enqueue-only**: carried verbatim from ADR-121 — "a UI mutates only by enqueueing — it never writes concepts, verdicts, frontmatter, or commits"; the agent contract exposes plan/sources/assumptions/unknowns/pending-writes before any enqueue (chat transparency), chat additive not primary (ADR-130). — **Why:** ADR-121 carried verbatim as "the universal UI write rule" (disposition map).

- **What:** **Declarative verdict-carrying view-specs** from a fixed component vocabulary (table/card); clients render known kinds only; agent-generated components, shared mutable agent↔UI state, and rendering untrusted text as active content are rejected (ADR-130; PR-U #1189). — **Why:** carries ADR-102/116 "one view definition, projections disposable and never a second truth"; framework-hosted UX (CopilotKit-class) rejected — "inverts the boundary via shared mutable agent↔UI state." ADR-103 (projected Canvas spatial axis) **rejected**: "spatial-at-scale refuted; tabular/faceted is the validated default; small-graph view must beat a tabular baseline" (disposition map; borrow-doc visualization defaults, Heer/Bostock).

- **What:** **Honesty-card + code-review ergonomics** (ADR-51 carried, extended): attention items present argument-for/against, what-tipped-it, and certainty (never a verdict on a proposal); high-cardinality decisions become one batch worklist; loudness graded; sessions are bounded, presentation span-first with source evidence adjacent (the Elicit table pattern), `--apply` one click — "review effectiveness collapses beyond ~60 minutes/bounded batches" (ADR-130; PR-O `--ready-only` export, attention view-specs). — **Why:** "Making each review cheaper is the other half of ADR-128's bargain" (borrow-doc "static review cockpit," Horvitz/Amershi/Shneiderman).

- **What:** **Serve-hosted file watcher**: `memoria serve --watch` (stdlib polling over the existing `workspace scan`/`observe-pi-edits` path; `--once` for deterministic gating) — "the worker remains the correctness boundary, so the watcher adds no new promotion or demotion path" (PR-P #1184, `13411f3e`). — **Why:** watcher-as-required-daemon rejected — the accepted form is "real-time when the on-demand process runs, scan + consumption guard otherwise, guard never retired" (ADR-127 Alternatives), preserving the no-daemon architecture.

- **What:** **PI direct access carried from ADR-72** — every routine action reachable by the researcher directly without conversing with an agent; in alpha.15 the direct-access surface is the CLI plus the read-API transports; the CLI command scheme cut over to verb-first (`new note`, `work add/enrich/interview/digest`, `new hub <tag>`, `link`, `check`, `show`, `list`, `ask`, `export`; `project`/`workspace`/`vocab`/`attention`/`request`/`journal` groups); candidate instantiation via `attention resolve --apply`; `note propose`/`accept` do not exist in 15 (ADR-130; PR-B3 #1165, `16131e72`). — **Why:** ADR-72's "never agent-only" carried; the propose/accept surface was destructive-transition modeling now unified under one id via journaled mode flips.

- **What:** **Distribution** = `uv tool install memoria`, one command, no external runtime, no always-on process; scheduled work is plain CLI invocations under cron/systemd/Task Scheduler; docs reframed accordingly (README/AGENTS.md rewritten — "shared instruction layer for any human, local tool, or delegated agent"; cron scripts `--no-hermes`-style flags dropped) (ADR-125 Consequences; PR-AG #1201–#1222; vault AGENTS.md diff). — **Why:** the Hermes/board/profile install unit is gone; scheduled jobs are "operator-managed wrapper invocations rather than installer-wired cron."

### 9. Evaluation / measurement

- **What:** **Seeded-error verdict ported to the four-type schema**: `alpha15-seeded-errors.json` added; `alpha12-seeded-errors.json` (and alpha.11) **deleted** (`git diff …/system/eval/`); verdicts keyed by `(target operation, bundle, mode, provider, model, params)`; a live-only `non_sandbox_licensed` flag; the seeded stale-source fixture moved from CSL `standing` into DB Concept flags (`seeded_errors.py` diff; PR-M #1180, PR #1219 `f47fcf88` required the alpha15 bundle as the only one). — **Why:** ADR-10 (PR 10 harness) already existed on main, so this was a **port not a build** (exec-plan §Relationship to alpha.14); the old bundles referenced retired types/`standing` frontmatter and had to be deleted for the four-type cut.

- **What:** **CLI dogfood checkpoint reporter**: `scripts/alpha15_dogfood_checkpoint.py` (read-only workspace-state reporter — request counts, checked/unchecked backlogs, attention counts, per-work interaction count, unchecked-backlog slope, model/tool-call budget proxies) executed on `~/Memoria-test`; evidence in `dogfood/` (baseline + after-CLI JSON, provider/interview replay, Markdown export) (PR-N #1181; dogfood report shows the minimum loop end-to-end with a `missing-thesis` structural gap correctly surfaced). — **Why:** borrow-doc "state-based dogfood evaluation" (Tau-bench, AgentDojo, ScienceAgentBench, EpiBench) — "Build one tiny Memoria-specific harness for dogfood, not a general benchmark suite"; ADR-11 diagnostic-never-gates stays intact.

- **What:** ADR-11 amended (not superseded) to permit build-time model selection via `eval select-models` (see §2). — **Why:** whole-system verdicts stay diagnostic; a build-time knob choice is a different act.

### 10. Security

- **What:** **Fail-closed enforcement** as an architecture invariant: the request envelope, checks, and read barrier fail closed on any internal error — "a logged denial is policy, silence is wiring" (ADR-125; `read_barrier.py`, `trusted_writer.py` +185). — **Why:** ADR-28's load-bearing lesson — "a gate that proceeds on its own failure is not a gate."

- **What:** **No agent tool grants**: Memoria never grants an agent file/terminal/exec/send tools; untrusted work text returned as tagged data, never instructions; loopback HTTP binds only loopback hosts, token-auth (`MEMORIA_HTTP_TOKEN`), no raw SQLite/file routes; MCP behind an optional extra with a closed tool roster (ADR-125/130; PR-R/PR-S/PR-T). — **Why:** surviving ADR-32/46 invariant + lethal-trifecta mitigation; cross-channel credential-reuse fixture documents the residual (any local bearer credential is readable by a trusted-local agent).

- **What:** **HTTP read-scope enforcement / declared-frontmatter enforcement / prompt-injection sealing** (see §5, §8) with negative poisoned-input fixtures per text-reading operation (ADR-129; `52ab9ad7`, `19d7d006`). — **Why:** borrow-doc "untrusted data sealing" (Greshake/AgentDojo/InjecAgent).

- **What:** **DB-loss fails closed to `unchecked`**, ignoring forged frontmatter status (see §4). — **Why:** a rebuild "cannot be trusted to unblock anything" (ADR-127).

### 11. ADRs (consolidation sweep)

- **What:** Six consolidation ADRs (**125** standalone-cli-engine, **126** four-type-knowledge-model, **127** quarantine-and-verify, **128** no-write-time-oracle, **129** layered-machine-judgment, **130** read-api-surfaces-and-copi) landed in `docs/adr/` (PR #1158/#1159); ~70 fine-grained ADRs tombstoned as **superseded** (text kept, `status: superseded`, `superseded_by`), four **rejected** (95 nightly loop, 97 Writer claim-notes, 103 Canvas spatial axis, 106 Hermes cost-capture), several **stay-proposed/deferred** (16, 88–91, 98, 107, 108); ADR-124 absorbed ADR-06; the ADR index was regenerated and the README now directs new decisions to the six subsystem ADRs by default (`1a8664da`, `a3b3f1f4`). — **Why:** "a corpus of ~90 fine-grained ADRs has repeatedly caused confusion and contradiction — decisions were re-litigated, superseded-in-practice ADRs read as current, and reviews missed collisions. The unit of decision is now the **subsystem**, not the mechanism" (disposition map Consolidation rationale). Rejected-alternatives memory is never pruned — "numbers are permanent."

- **What:** In-15 proposed ADRs flipped to **accepted** as slices landed: **92** (discovery relevance, #1195), **93** (keyphrase tags, #1191), **94** (record-linkage dedup, #1190/#1192/#1193/#1194), **99** (MASSW aspects, #1196) — each on a deterministic path *without* the ML dependency the original ADR contemplated (disposition map). — **Why:** "Correct, not cheap" but "simplest design that meets the *stated* requirement" — the cheap deterministic path cleared the bar and ML was deferred until real corpus data justifies it.

- **What:** ADR-64 lost stale `-WithHermes`/`--with-hermes` installer-flag claims (#1207); ADR-130 lost stale CLI+plugin/second-wave wording (#1208); future editor adapters now **require their own ADR** rather than inheriting an alpha.15 commitment (#1203, `d5131811`). — **Why:** the negative scope gate — "adapter-specific UI needs its own ADR before it is scheduled" and "alpha.15 cannot close with Obsidian plugin implementation counted as release scope" (design index Scope Boundary; ADR-130).

---

### Notable removals / retirements (consolidated)

| Removed / retired | Why |
| --- | --- |
| 9 type schemas (`source`, `person`, `organization`, `venue`, `digest`, `adapter`, `operation`, `skill`, `workflow`) | Catalog entities → SQLite records; operations → product code; digest → `work`; the type zoo caused drift (ADR-126). |
| `check_status`/`standing`/`note_status` frontmatter fields (incl. PR #1157's just-added enforcement) | Meaning-only frontmatter; verdicts are DB-only; frontmatter checking caused hash churn + forged-status foot-gun (ADR-126/128). |
| `calibration.yaml` | No constant was ever validated; shadow-first generalized; clustering surface removed (ADR-129; PR #1204). |
| `capabilities/` workspace tree + `capability-index.json` (1421 lines) | Operations are PR-reviewed product code, not gated vault data (ADR-125; PR-E2 #1172). |
| `golden_restore.py` + `.memoria/golden` path | Package reinstall is the restore path (ADR-125; PR #1206). |
| Argparse CLI `note propose/accept/reject`, `work capture` | Verb-first surface; propose/accept modeled destructive transitions now unified via journaled mode flips (ADR-130; PR-B3 #1165). |
| `alpha12`/`alpha11` seeded-error bundles | Referenced retired types/CSL `standing`; replaced by `alpha15-seeded-errors.json` keyed per (operation, model, mode) (PR-M #1180, PR #1219). |
| The review-queue **approval** surface; the honesty-card inbox-as-Obsidian-category mechanism | Structural write-gate reversed to quarantine-and-verify; approval no longer confers correctness (ADR-128). |
| Hermes runtime, installed profiles, board lanes/fleet, MCP-as-required-API, Obsidian policy plugin, Zotero-as-authority | Dropped from the product (not deferred) under the standalone-engine cut (ADR-125). |
| ADRs 95, 97, 103, 106 | Rejected: unattended loop conflicts with no-daemon arch; Writer claim-notes is a non-goal; spatial-at-scale refuted; Hermes cost-capture mechanism dead (disposition map). |

**Deferred out of alpha.15 (explicitly, with reason):** Obsidian plugin/manifests/command-palette/Inspector, adapter-specific UI, rich UI frameworks, remote/OAuth transport (no consumer), multi-user infra, edge-extraction act-promotion tuning (no real usage data yet), sqlite-vec + local-embedding semantic retrieval (didn't clear the baseline bar), full OKF import/export (ADR-107 proposed), and candidate cost-table/manifest-rewrite mechanics in `select-models` (current data has one candidate per mode). All gated by the design index Scope Boundary's negative gate.


---

# Part IV — Synthesis: evolution arcs (alpha.1 → alpha.15)

## Evolution arcs (alpha.1 → alpha.15)

Memoria's alpha series is not a feature-accretion history; it is a sequence of **re-derivations**, three of which (alpha.7, alpha.11, alpha.14) discarded a standing architecture and rebuilt from requirements. The through-line is a steady transfer of authority away from autonomous agents and configurable runtime toward a **deterministic, gated, single-writer engine** whose safety rests on traceability rather than approval. The dates below are the release-folder/design-doc authoring dates in git; the "biggest change" is the one decision that reframed the product at that step.

### Timeline

| Version | Date | One-line theme | Single biggest design change |
|---|---|---|---|
| alpha.1 | 2026-06-14 | First v0.1 cut of the Hermes + Obsidian + Zotero stack | Establishes the release-gate discipline and the three-layer (board · workers · vault) product on the Hermes runtime (ADR-01, ADR-22) |
| alpha.2 | 2026-06-14 | Consolidation checkpoint | Folds scattered v0.1 build work into one coherent checkpoint |
| alpha.3 | 2026-06-14/15 | UI build milestone | First dedicated Obsidian UI research/build pass (`tmp/ui-design-research-report.md`) |
| alpha.4 | 2026-06-15 | Build/defect closure + engine vocabulary | Names the deterministic layer **"operations"** (ADR-69) and pins **engines-write / agents-judge** (ADR-57) |
| alpha.5 | 2026-06-15 | The Project gate | Adds the fourth navigation gate plus the **thesis note, argument graph + warrant** (ADR-77/78/79) and the ephemeral test-env (ADR-80) |
| alpha.6 | 2026-06-16 | Conformance + test-env harness | Makes accepted ADRs actually true and ships containerized-test-env Phase 1 (ADR-80) |
| alpha.7 | 2026-06-18 | Clean-slate Obsidian UI & navigation | **Persistent-shell four-space model** (Inbox/Library/Knowledge/Project nav row) + Bases view layer + capture forms; retires the workspace-swap (ADR-68 → ADR-81) |
| alpha.8 | 2026-06-18/19 | Runtime foundations & observability | Splits the omnibus ADR-58/59/61/65 into the granular ADR-84…100 (classical-method displacements, retrieval/schema extensions) |
| alpha.9 | 2026-06-21 | UI/workflow + runtime-gate hardening | The literature-review **"qwen2.5:7b is the test fixture, not the runtime — the live engine is an API"** correction, plus a Hermes-version decision |
| alpha.10 | 2026-06-22 | Hermes/runtime governance + onboarding | **Promotion-gated verification** process; ADR-116/117/118/119 schema & dashboard work; tutorials + sample vault |
| alpha.11 | 2026-06-27 | Clean-slate re-derivation from requirements | The **integrity spine** (attributable/reversible/detected + read-barrier) over an **OKF workspace** (catalog/knowledge/capabilities); one knowledge graph (digest/note/hub); direction-not-authorship |
| alpha.12 | 2026-06-28 | The keep-test / storage boundary | **SQLite as SSOT for catalog + ops**, markdown only for the keep-set; **CLI-first**, Obsidian demoted to optional adapter; typed pydantic-ai operations (ADR-122) |
| alpha.13 | 2026-06-30 | Multi-source catalog enrichment | **capture→enrich split** pulling OpenAlex/Semantic Scholar/PubMed/Unpaywall/Crossref/arXiv with per-field provenance + retraction gate (ADR-123/124) |
| alpha.14 | 2026-06-30 | Standalone CLI + engine consolidation | **Removes Obsidian, Zotero, Hermes, MCP, and installed profiles from the required baseline**; OpenAlex graph import; universal concept frontmatter (#1157) |
| alpha.15 | 2026-07-01/02 | Engine + integrity hardening | The **four-type knowledge model** (note/work/hub/project) with **meaning-only frontmatter** — every verdict moved out of files into SQLite; quarantine-and-verify; uv/Typer/stdlib-sqlite; ADR consolidation 125–130 |

The shape of the series: alpha.1–6 build out the Hermes-era product; alpha.7 resets the *UI*; alpha.8–10 harden the *runtime*; alpha.11 resets the *architecture*; alpha.12–14 progressively strip the runtime down to a standalone engine; alpha.15 hardens and consolidates it.

---

### (a) Seven specialist profiles → five → no agent autonomy at all

**What:** The agent model collapsed in three moves. It began as **seven specialist Hermes profiles over one generalist** (ADR-02, `_notes/docs-exports/adr-full.md`: "Seven specialist profiles over one generalist agent"). At the **alpha.7-era clean-slate (ADR-48)** it flipped to **"one Co-PI fronts everything; specialists consolidate to posture-defined agents"** — five profiles, the retriever/scout profile (ADR-37) and profile-compilation (ADR-42) both folded in (`adr-full.md`: 37 and 42 "superseded → ADR-48"). By **alpha.14/15 the profile system was deleted from the product entirely** (ADR-125 supersedes 26, 48, 120; "Dropped from the product, not deferred: … installed profiles and lane/fleet (26, 48, 120)"). What survives is a single **read-only Co-PI posture plus capability-backed operation postures**, where "the dividing line is posture and write-permission, not capability or tool" (`docs/design/why-specialist-postures.md`).

**Why:** A generalist agent has "unclear responsibility … ambiguous permissions … no separation of stances" (`why-specialist-postures.md`), which is why roles were split in the first place. But finer role-splitting fragments the system: "more routing, more permission matrices, and — decisively — a fragmented learning loop" (same doc), so seven collapsed to postures-per-family. The deeper flip — removing *autonomy* — is forced by the autonomous-loop analysis: Karpathy's keep/revert loop is only safe when "the metric is monotonic … changes are reversible … experiments are independent," and knowledge work fails all three because "synthesis quality is not scalar," "synthesis errors compound," and "later sources reinterpret earlier ones" (`docs/design/why-not-autonomous.md`). Confidence-routing (SmartPause) was refused because "confident-wrong is the failure mode" (same doc; `why-review-gate-is-structural.md`). The literature review corroborated the *mechanics* but stripped the autonomy: the ~47-system survey found the useful patterns are "structural: stage gates, explicit roles, typed handoffs, persistent graphs" while the refused ones are "scalar-optimization loops: autonomous keep/revert, tournament evolution, confidence-routed gate bypass" (`docs/design/why-pattern-provenance.md`). Net effect: "from agent-assisted to bounded, phase-gated knowledge production" (same). The alpha.11 design states the destination bluntly — "the PI is a director + spot-corrector, not an approval queue … Trust shifts from 'a human approved this' to 'the system guarantees this trace'" (`scratch/releases/0.1.0-alpha.11/…-design.md` §4). ADR-125 keeps only the posture invariant with the runtime gone: "Memoria never grants an agent file, terminal, code-execution, or send tools."

### (b) Numbered folders (10-inbox / 02-answers) → type-first folders → state-not-folders

**What:** The original scheme was **lifecycle-numbered folders** — ADR-04, "Folders encode lifecycle stage, not subject area" (`adr-full.md`). At the alpha.7-era reset it flipped to **type-first category folders** (ADR-47, "Type-first category folders — catalog · notes · projects · inbox · system"), superseding ADR-04. Alpha.15 completed the move by taking read-state *out of folders entirely*: "a Concept's position in the system is its type, never its topic, and read state is record state, not a folder" (`docs/design/lifecycle-over-topic.md`), consolidated into the four-type homes of ADR-126.

**Why:** Numbered lifecycle folders forced a **file move on every state change**, which breaks the one property the system exists to protect. The current doc makes the argument: "Topics are many-to-many; a folder is one location," so folders are reserved "for the one fact that is one-to-one: what kind of checked bundle this is" (`lifecycle-over-topic.md`). Moving state into a record instead of a path is "strictly better" because "a state change does not move a file, so it cannot break wikilinks, lose Git history continuity, or invalidate saved queries," and "a claim cited by twelve other notes can be retracted, superseded, and archived without a single inbound link breaking" (same doc). This is the same provenance-first logic (design principle 5, `design-principles.md`) that later drove `check_status` out of frontmatter (arc d).

### (c) Emergence of the four-type knowledge model (work / note / project / hub)

**What:** There was no clean type model early — types accreted. ADR-126 records the damage: "The type roster grew by accretion (47, 50, 78, 117, 119): claim, question, excerpt, synthesis, thesis, steering, vocabulary, asset, digest, fleeting — each with folder homes, lifecycle fields, and per-type rules … 12+ types across three bundles." Alpha.11 already tried to tame this to a **three-node knowledge graph — digest (machine) / note (human) / hub (both)** (`0.1.0-alpha.11-design.md` §5). The **flip to exactly four types happened at alpha.15**: ADR-126 "Four concept types … replaces the accreted type zoo … with four types" — **note** (with optional `mode: claim | question`), **work** (a source's subjective digest, 1:1 with the SQLite catalog record), **hub** (owns exactly one controlled-vocabulary tag; membership is mechanical, salience is curated), and **project** (the compose-flow frame with one-way project→corpus references). It landed in code as PR-B2 (#1164), "the largest single change in 15": schema/templates/runtime cut to "the four knowledge Concept types (`note`, `work`, `hub`, `project`); Concept ids are ULIDs … `digest` materialization moved to `work`" (alpha.15 exec-plan §3).

**Why:** "The multiplicity itself caused drift and confusion" (ADR-126 Context). The discriminator was tightened to "a fundamentally different artifact" — a flippable check regime is a *mode*, not a type, and a layer-difference is not a knowledge type. That test dissolved most of the zoo into relocations ("excerpt → a `anchor` on a note/work; index → generated views; fleeting → an unchecked note; steering → the `instructions` config; thesis → a role, not a type"). The four earn their place by *creating distinct obligations the gap engine feeds on*: a `claim` mode without evidence is an `under-warranted` gap; an open `question` is a compose-flow lead — "field-derived typing could not tell a plain thought from a claim missing its evidence" (ADR-126). The model is genealogically Luhmann's: catalog work ≈ literature note, note = permanent note, hub = structure note/Map-of-Content (`docs/design/intellectual-foundations.md`, `hubs-and-navigation.md`), with the net-new machine-digest role borrowed from Karpathy's compiler.

### (d) Frontmatter: optional → universal enforcement (alpha.14) → meaning-only (alpha.15)

**What:** Early frontmatter was per-type and optional, and it *carried verdict state* — `check_status` lived in the file. **Alpha.14 forced universal frontmatter**: PR #1157 (`88b7f0f5`), "universal-concept-frontmatter enforcement … `id`/`standing`/`check_status` frontmatter enforcement across templates and operation manifests" (alpha.15 exec-plan §0). **Alpha.15 then inverted it**: PR-L (#1179) and the §S5 principle made frontmatter **meaning-only** — "`check_status` (and all verdict/derived state) is *not written to frontmatter at all*, and a gate asserts frontmatter carries no verdict fields" (exec-plan §1). Verdicts moved to SQLite (PR-B, #1163: "frontmatter `check_status` no longer trusted as verdict authority"). PR-AC (#1197) then closed the field set: the validator "rejects undeclared Concept frontmatter fields."

**Why:** The alpha.14 universal enforcement was the natural endpoint of read-barrier logic — a consumer must be able to trust every file's status, so every file must declare it. But that created the exact hazard ADR-126 names: "`check_status` lived in frontmatter, so checking a note rewrote it, hand-edits forged status, and every consumer had to distrust the file it was reading." The fix is the split-authority rule of ADR-125: "files own meaning, the DB owns verdicts and records." This is enforced structurally, not by convention, because the value only holds if it *can't* be forged — `checked_terminology_gate.py` even "blocks checked = approved/verified/trusted drift" (exec-plan PR-L). Fail-closed follows: "rebuild-from-files starts fully `unchecked` and ignores frontmatter status" (PR-B). The move is the same provenance-integrity principle as arc (b), applied to state instead of location.

### (e) The OKF interchange bundle (alpha.11 / alpha.15)

**What:** Memoria discovered its own substrate was a near-match for Google Cloud's **Open Knowledge Format**. ADR-107 (proposed 2026-06-19, the alpha.9 era) records the convergence: "OKF's *Concept* is a typed markdown document, its *Concept ID* is the file path minus `.md`, relationships are markdown links … That an external, vendor-backed spec landed on the same shape is validation." **Alpha.11 adopted OKF nouns for the whole workspace**: "A Memoria workspace contains three OKF-compatible bundle roots — `catalog/`, `knowledge/`, and `capabilities/`," with Memoria as a "strict producer, permissive consumer" (`0.1.0-alpha.11-design.md` §6.1). **By alpha.15 OKF was narrowed to the boundary only** — export/interchange, not the internal representation. ADR-107 states the reason it can only be a boundary: "OKF mandates permissive consumption … and holds that 'the specific kind of relationship is conveyed by the surrounding prose, not by the link itself.' Memoria deliberately rejected prose-typed relationships in favor of typed edges (ADR-126) … OKF is therefore a fit for the boundary, not the core."

**Why:** OKF solved Memoria's "least-defined layer … its outbound layer" — it "supplies exactly that missing unit: the Knowledge Bundle … consumable without Memoria's gates, MCPs, or Hermes runtime" (ADR-107). But OKF's permissive-consumer thesis is "the inverse of Memoria's thesis," which needs the relationship type *on the edge* for graph queries and enforces "strict schemas, controlled vocabularies, and category-error rejection." So the interchange format could not become the internal contract without discarding the integrity model. The retreat from workspace-wide OKF (alpha.11) to export-only (alpha.15) tracks the broader alpha.12 keep-test: only the keep-set must be portable markdown; working state is SQLite (arc g).

### (f) The Hermes runtime's rise (alpha.9/10) and its role by alpha.15

**What:** Hermes was the *foundation* of the product from alpha.1: ADR-22 "Build on the Hermes Agent runtime rather than a bespoke one," ADR-26 "The repo is the install unit; profiles are hand-authored," ADR-27/28 the write-gate as a Hermes plugin, ADR-32 external access over MCP, ADR-46 the seven-layer architecture on Hermes. Its **peak was alpha.9/10**, whose themes are literally "Hermes-version decision" (alpha.9 README) and "Hermes/runtime governance" (alpha.10 README), with cost/session accounting read straight from the Hermes session store (ADR-106: "hermes kanban show … `~/.hermes/profiles/<lane>/state.db`"). Then it was demoted, then removed. **Alpha.11** kept Hermes only "as a specialized adapter … where a specific Hermes feature pays for itself," with a **direct OpenAI-compatible API as the default runner** (`0.1.0-alpha.11-design.md` §8). **Alpha.12** made the engine standalone and CLI-first. **Alpha.14** put Hermes explicitly "Outside the baseline" (`0.1.0-alpha.14-design.md` §0). **Alpha.15/ADR-125 dropped it from the product**: "Dropped from the product, not deferred: Hermes (22, 35, 43, 80's Hermes-flavored harness)." By alpha.15 the runtime is Python 3.12 + uv + Typer + stdlib sqlite3 + pydantic-ai + git CLI (ADR-125); "Hermes is not part of the runtime" (exec-plan PR-AG). Hermes plays **no role** in shipped alpha.15.

**Why:** The rise was pragmatic reuse — "a durable state machine across sessions and retries — the runtime Memoria builds on" (`_notes/ai-research-systems-survey.md`). The fall was driven by the same alpha.9 literature correction that reset the model tier: the review "was run assuming `qwen2.5:7b` (local) is Memoria's production engine. It is not: `qwen2.5:7b` is the local test fixture; the live … engines call an LLM API" (`_notes/REVIEW-SUMMARY.md`, `REVIEW-REFUTATIONS.md`). Once the live engine is an API, the Hermes control-plane DB, profiles, Kanban, and MCP-as-required-API become weight the single-user local tool doesn't need — the alpha.11 design lists them among what to "deliberately shed": "per-write approval … profiles/fleet as the primary runtime model, the Hermes control-plane DB, the seven-layer ceremony" (`_notes/0.1.0-alpha.11-design.md`). ADR-125 turns the reuse argument back on itself: "The engineering ADR-22 warned against (durable state, retries, crash recovery) is now owned in-house — ADR-127 is where that obligation is paid." The consequence is the design goal all along: "One install command, no external runtime, no always-on process."

### (g) The SQLite / derived-store state boundary (alpha.12)

**What:** Alpha.11 held a **files-are-SSOT-everywhere** rule with "a passive rebuilt index over files" — the query index (`qmd`), embeddings, DAG, and queues were all "disposable projections (gitignored, rebuilt)" (`0.1.0-alpha.11-design.md` §6). **Alpha.12 flipped this with the keep-test** (ADR-122): "The thing you keep if Memoria dies must be markdown files in OKF, plus a portable bibliography export. Everything else is free to be SQLite" (`0.1.0-alpha.12-design.md` §1). SQLite became **SSOT for the catalog, source/entity/link graph, journal, queue, flags, check status, and rollback graph**, with markdown reserved for the keep-set (knowledge + capabilities + a materialized `references.bib`). Alpha.15/ADR-125 hardened it into a **split-authority rule**: "SQLite is the authority for records, operations, queue, journal, and verdicts; markdown files are the human corpus; content-addressed blobs hold raw payloads," explicitly "overturning ADR-49's rejected alternative ('SQLite as the store: never the source of truth')."

**Why:** The alpha.11 all-files rule was honest about ownership but wrong about *relational* state: a passive file-index cannot give "records, queues, and verdicts a transactional home markdown cannot provide" (ADR-125). The keep-test replaced "the fuzzy 'ownership feels important'" with an objective question — "does the user need this to keep thinking and writing outside Memoria" (`0.1.0-alpha.12-design.md` §1) — so ownership is preserved exactly where it matters and SQLite is used everywhere it doesn't. Two enabling constraints were relaxed to make this affordable: "no multi-device sync (single machine)" and "ownership/portability scoped to the keep-set + bibliography export, not the whole workspace" (same doc §0). Alpha.15 then paid the durability bill this boundary implies: WAL + `synchronous=FULL`, write-ahead fsync ordering, crash-at-each-boundary recovery, and fail-closed-to-`unchecked` on DB loss (exec-plan PR-D2, §1; ADR-127).

### (h) Enrichment / graph (DOI, OpenAlex, Crossref — alpha.13/14)
